org.pronzato.fabric.stitch

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/Stitch.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchLauncher;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchSettings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatures;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuItem;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenusBuilder;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchFabricSettings;

public final class Stitch {
  private final StitchFabricSettings fabric;
  private final StitchSettings stitch;
  private final StitchFeatures features;
  private final Class<?> applicationClass;
  private final StitchMenuProvider menuProvider;

  private Stitch(Builder builder) {
    this.fabric = builder.fabricBuilder.build();
    this.stitch = builder.stitchBuilder.build();
    Set<String> requestedEntries = builder.menusBuilder.referencedEntryIds();
    this.features = builder.featuresBuilder.build(requestedEntries);
    this.applicationClass = builder.applicationClass;
    this.menuProvider =
        composeMenuProvider(
            builder.menusBuilder.build(features.registry().menuContributions()));
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public StitchFabricSettings fabric() {
    return fabric;
  }

  public StitchSettings stitch() {
    return stitch;
  }

  public StitchFeatures features() {
    return features;
  }

  public StitchRuntime start() {
    return start(new String[0]);
  }

  public StitchRuntime start(String... args) {
    return StitchLauncher.run(
        Objects.requireNonNull(applicationClass, "applicationClass is required for start()"),
        this,
        menuProvider,
        args == null ? new String[0] : args);
  }

  public Map<String, Object> asSpringDefaults() {
    Map<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(stitch.asSpringDefaults());
    values.put("stitch.fabric.group", fabric.group());
    values.put("stitch.fabric.name", fabric.name());
    values.put("stitch.fabric.instance", fabric.instance());
    values.put("stitch.fabric.discoveryUrls", fabric.discoveryUrls());
    values.put("stitch.fabric.kerberosKeytab", fabric.kerberosKeytab());
    values.put("stitch.fabric.kerberosUsername", fabric.kerberosUsername());
    if (fabric.kekFile() != null) {
      values.put("stitch.fabric.kekFile", fabric.kekFile());
    }
    if (fabric.trustCert() != null) {
      values.put("stitch.fabric.trustCert", fabric.trustCert());
    }
    return Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static StitchMenuProvider composeMenuProvider(List<StitchMenuItem> menus) {
    if (menus == null || menus.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    List<StitchMenuItem> resolvedMenus = List.copyOf(menus);
    return () -> resolvedMenus;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final StitchFabricSettings.Builder fabricBuilder = StitchFabricSettings.builder();
    private final StitchSettings.Builder stitchBuilder = StitchSettings.builder();
    private final StitchFeatures.Builder featuresBuilder = StitchFeatures.builder();
    private final StitchMenusBuilder menusBuilder = new StitchMenusBuilder();
    private Class<?> applicationClass;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withApplicationClass(Class<?> value) {
      this.applicationClass = Objects.requireNonNull(value, "value");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFabric(Consumer<StitchFabricSettings.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(fabricBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withStitch(Consumer<StitchSettings.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(stitchBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMenus(Consumer<StitchMenusBuilder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(menusBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFeatures(Consumer<StitchFeatures.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(featuresBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Stitch build() {
      return new Stitch(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/StitchRuntime.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication;
import org.springframework.context.ConfigurableApplicationContext;

public final class StitchRuntime implements AutoCloseable {
  private final ConfigurableApplicationContext context;

  public StitchRuntime(ConfigurableApplicationContext context) {
    this.context = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
  }

  public boolean isRunning() {
    return context.isRunning();
  }

  public void stop() {
    SpringApplication.exit(context);
    context.close();
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    stop();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app;

import java.lang.annotation.Documented;
import java.lang.annotation.ElementType;
import java.lang.annotation.Retention;
import java.lang.annotation.RetentionPolicy;
import java.lang.annotation.Target;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;

@Target(ElementType.TYPE)
@Retention(RetentionPolicy.RUNTIME)
@Documented
@SpringBootApplication
public @interface StitchApplication {}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;

import org.springframework.boot.web.servlet.FilterRegistrationBean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.ClassPathBeanDefinitionScanner;

public final class StitchLauncher {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchLauncher.class);

  private StitchLauncher() {}

  public static StitchRuntime run(Class<?> appClass, Stitch stitch) {
    return run(appClass, stitch, null);
  }

  public static StitchRuntime run(
      Class<?> appClass, Stitch stitch, StitchMenuProvider stitchMenuProvider) {
    return run(appClass, stitch, stitchMenuProvider, new String[0]);
  }

  public static StitchRuntime run(
      Class<?> appClass,
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchMenuProvider stitchMenuProvider,
      String... args) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(appClass, "appClass");
    Objects.requireNonNull(stitch, "stitch");
    StitchComponents.configureDebugLabels(stitch.stitch().componentLabelsEnabled());
    StitchSpringRuntime.setPageTitle(stitch.stitch().appTitle());
    StitchSpringRuntime.setFaviconPath(stitch.stitch().shell().brandLogoPath());

    SpringApplication app = new SpringApplication(StitchSpringRuntime.class);
    app.setBannerMode(stitch.stitch().startupBannerEnabled() ? Banner.Mode.CONSOLE : Banner.Mode.OFF);
    app.setRegisterShutdownHook(true);
    app.setDefaultProperties(defaultProperties(stitch));
    app.addInitializers(stitchInitializer(appClass, stitch, stitchMenuProvider));
    ConfigurableApplicationContext context = app.run(args == null ? new String[0] : args);
    return new StitchRuntime(context);
  }

  private static Map<String, Object> defaultProperties(Stitch stitch) {
    Map<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(stitch.asSpringDefaults());
    values.put("vaadin.productionMode", "false");
    return Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static ApplicationContextInitializer<GenericApplicationContext> stitchInitializer(
      Class<?> appClass, Stitch stitch, StitchMenuProvider stitchMenuProvider) {
    return context -> {
      if (appClass.getPackageName() == null || appClass.getPackageName().isBlank()) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("applicationClass must be in a named package");
      }
      AutoConfigurationPackages.register(
          context, appClass.getPackageName(), Stitch.class.getPackageName());
      new ClassPathBeanDefinitionScanner(context).scan(appClass.getPackageName());
      context.registerBean(Stitch.class, () -> stitch);
      context.registerBean(
          Fabric.Session.class,
          () -> {
            try {
              return createSession(stitch);
            } catch (Exception error) {
              throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to create Fabric session", error);
            }
          },
          definition -> definition.setDestroyMethodName("close"));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchRuntimeContext.class,
          () ->
              StitchRuntimeContext.of(
                  context.getBean(Stitch.class), context.getBean(Fabric.Session.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          SsoConfig.class, () -> buildSsoConfig(context.getBean(Stitch.class).stitch()));
      context.registerBean(SsoService.class, () -> new DefaultSsoService(context.getBean(SsoConfig.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchSsoUsers.class, () -> new StitchSsoUsers(context.getBean(Stitch.class).stitch()));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchSsoFilter.class,
          () ->
              new StitchSsoFilter(
                  context.getBean(SsoService.class),
                  context.getBean(SsoConfig.class),
                  context.getBean(Stitch.class).stitch().sso().fallbackSubject()));
      context.registerBean(
          "stitchSsoFilterRegistration",
          FilterRegistrationBean.class,
          () -> {
            FilterRegistrationBean<StitchSsoFilter> registration = new FilterRegistrationBean<>();
            registration.setFilter(context.getBean(StitchSsoFilter.class));
            registration.addUrlPatterns("/*");
            registration.setOrder(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE);
            registration.setName("stitchSsoFilter");
            return registration;
          });
      context.registerBean(
          StitchSsoController.class,
          () ->
              new StitchSsoController(
                  context.getBean(SsoService.class),
                  context.getBean(SsoConfig.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchSsoUsers.class),
                  context.getBean(Stitch.class).stitch()));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchStatusDataProviders.class,
          () -> new StitchStatusDataProviders(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAssetsDataProviders.class,
          () -> new StitchAssetsDataProviders(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchPlatformDataProviders.class,
          () -> new StitchPlatformDataProviders(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchDiscoveryBrowserProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchDatasetsProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchDatasetsProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchDatasetViewProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchDatasetViewProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchDatasetLiveProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchDatasetLiveProvider(
                  context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchDatasetsProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchStorageS3QueryProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchStreamsProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchStreamsProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchEntitlementsAdminProvider(
                  context.getBean(StitchAssetsDataProviders.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchDatasetsProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchDocsBrowserProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchDocsBrowserProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchDocsResourceController.class,
          () -> new StitchDocsResourceController(context.getBean(StitchDocsBrowserProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchCatalogProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchCatalogProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAgentsProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchAgentsProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchConfigsProvider.class,
          () -> new StitchConfigsProvider(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchConfigsApprovalsProvider(
                  context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchConfigsProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchConfigsRollbacksProvider(
                  context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchConfigsProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchConfigsSchemasProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchConfigsSchemasProvider(
                  context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchConfigsProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchConfigsWatcherProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchConfigsWatcherProvider(
                  context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class),
                  context.getBean(StitchConfigsProvider.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAuditStatusFeedAdapter.class,
          () -> new StitchAuditStatusFeedAdapter(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAuditConfigsFeedAdapter.class,
          () -> new StitchAuditConfigsFeedAdapter(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAuditDiscoveryFeedAdapter.class,
          () -> new StitchAuditDiscoveryFeedAdapter(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAuditEntitlementsFeedAdapter.class,
          () -> new StitchAuditEntitlementsFeedAdapter(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class)));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchAuditProvider.class,
          () ->
              new StitchAuditProvider(
                  List.copyOf(context.getBeansOfType(org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit.StitchAuditFeedAdapter.class).values())));
      context.registerBean(
          StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.class, StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry::new);
      registerConnectionWarmupRunner(context, stitch);
      if (stitchMenuProvider != null) {
        context.registerBean(StitchMenuProvider.class, () -> stitchMenuProvider);
      }
    };
  }

  private static void registerConnectionWarmupRunner(
      GenericApplicationContext context, Stitch stitch) {
    List<String> names = stitch.stitch().connectionWarmupNames();
    if (names.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    context.registerBean(
        "stitchConnectionWarmupRunner",
        ApplicationRunner.class,
        () ->
            args ->
                CompletableFuture.runAsync(
                    () -> runConnectionWarmup(context.getBean(StitchRuntimeContext.class))));
  }

  private static void runConnectionWarmup(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    List<String> names = runtimeContext.settings().connectionWarmupNames();
    for (String connectionName : names) {
      warmupConnection(runtimeContext, connectionName);
    }
  }

  private static void warmupConnection(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, String connectionName) {
    long startedAt = System.nanoTime();
    LOGGER.info("[Stitch][ConnectionWarmup] start connection={}", connectionName);
    try {
      AutoCloseable handle =
          runtimeContext
              .session()
              .connections()
              .get(
                  ConnectionRequest.builder(AutoCloseable.class)
                      .withConnectionName(connectionName)
                      .build());
      String type = touchWarmupHandle(handle);
      long elapsedMs = (System.nanoTime() - startedAt) / 1_000_000L;
      LOGGER.info(
          "[Stitch][ConnectionWarmup] success connection={} type={} elapsedMs={}",
          connectionName,
          type,
          elapsedMs);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      long elapsedMs = (System.nanoTime() - startedAt) / 1_000_000L;
      LOGGER.warn(
          "[Stitch][ConnectionWarmup] failed connection={} elapsedMs={} reason={}",
          connectionName,
          elapsedMs,
          error.getMessage(),
          error);
    }
  }

  private static String touchWarmupHandle(AutoCloseable handle) {
    if (handle == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Connection warmup resolved to null handle");
    }
    if (handle instanceof S3Connection s3) {
      // Touch metadata so lazy connector initialization happens during warmup.
      s3.bucket();
      return "S3";
    }
    if (handle instanceof HttpConnection http) {
      http.baseUri();
      return "HTTP";
    }
    if (handle instanceof AmpsConnection amps) {
      amps.client();
      return "AMPS";
    }
    if (handle instanceof OdbcConnection) {
      return "ODBC";
    }
    return handle.getClass().getSimpleName();
  }

  private static SsoConfig buildSsoConfig(StitchSettings settings) {
    StitchSettings.Sso sso = Objects.requireNonNull(settings, "settings").sso();
    SsoConfig.Spoof spoof =
        SsoConfig.Spoof.builder()
            .withEnabled(sso.spoofEnabled())
            .withAllowEditing(sso.spoofAllowEditing())
            .withCookieName(sso.spoofCookieName())
            .withDefaultUsername(sso.spoofDefaultUsername())
            .withCookieMaxAgeSeconds(sso.spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds())
            .withAttributeResolver(
                username ->
                    sso.spoofGroups().isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.of("groups", List.copyOf(sso.spoofGroups())))
            .build();
    return SsoConfig.builder()
        .withEnabled(sso.enabled())
        .withMode(sso.mode())
        .withForwardedHeadersEnabled(sso.forwardedHeadersEnabled())
        .withOidc(sso.oidc())
        .withSpoof(spoof)
        .build();
  }

  private static Fabric.Session createSession(Stitch stitch) throws Exception {
    var sessionBuilder = stitch.fabric().toSessionBuilder();
    String delegatedSubject = Strings.trimToNull(stitch.stitch().sso().spoofDefaultUsername());
    if (delegatedSubject != null) {
      sessionBuilder.withStatusUserTag(delegatedSubject);
    }
    Fabric.Session session = sessionBuilder.build();
    session.start();
    return session;
  }
}




===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/app/StitchSettings.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.oidc.FabricOidcConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchSettings {
  private final String appTitle;
  private final int serverPort;
  private final boolean pushEnabled;
  private final boolean startupBannerEnabled;
  private final boolean componentLabelsEnabled;
  private final List<String> connectionWarmupNames;
  private final String docsRootPath;
  private final Help help;
  private final Shell shell;
  private final Sso sso;

  private StitchSettings(Builder builder) {
    this.appTitle = require(builder.appTitle, "appTitle");
    this.serverPort = requirePort(builder.serverPort);
    this.pushEnabled = builder.pushEnabled;
    this.startupBannerEnabled = builder.startupBannerEnabled;
    this.componentLabelsEnabled = builder.componentLabelsEnabled;
    this.connectionWarmupNames =
        List.copyOf(normalizeConnectionWarmupNames(builder.connectionWarmupNames));
    this.docsRootPath = Strings.trimToNull(builder.docsRootPath);
    this.help = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.helpBuilder, "helpBuilder").build();
    this.shell = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.shellBuilder, "shellBuilder").build();
    this.sso = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.ssoBuilder, "ssoBuilder").build();
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public String appTitle() {
    return appTitle;
  }

  public int serverPort() {
    return serverPort;
  }

  public boolean pushEnabled() {
    return pushEnabled;
  }

  public boolean startupBannerEnabled() {
    return startupBannerEnabled;
  }

  public boolean componentLabelsEnabled() {
    return componentLabelsEnabled;
  }

  public List<String> connectionWarmupNames() {
    return connectionWarmupNames;
  }

  public String docsRootPath() {
    return docsRootPath;
  }

  public boolean helpEnabled() {
    return help.menuEnabled() && help.referenceEnabled();
  }

  public Help help() {
    return help;
  }

  public Shell shell() {
    return shell;
  }

  public Sso sso() {
    return sso;
  }

  public Map<String, Object> asSpringDefaults() {
    Map<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("server.port", Integer.toString(serverPort));
    values.put("stitch.app.title", appTitle);
    values.put("stitch.push.enabled", Boolean.toString(pushEnabled));
    values.put("stitch.startupBanner.enabled", Boolean.toString(startupBannerEnabled));
    values.put("spring.main.banner-mode", startupBannerEnabled ? "console" : "off");
    values.put("stitch.debug.componentLabels.enabled", Boolean.toString(componentLabelsEnabled));
    values.put(
        "stitch.connectionWarmup.names",
        connectionWarmupNames.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(",", connectionWarmupNames));
    if (docsRootPath != null) {
      values.put("stitch.docs.rootPath", docsRootPath);
    }
    values.put("stitch.help.enabled", Boolean.toString(helpEnabled()));
    values.put("stitch.help.menu.enabled", Boolean.toString(help.menuEnabled()));
    values.put("stitch.help.reference.enabled", Boolean.toString(help.referenceEnabled()));
    values.put("stitch.shell.brandLogoPath", shell.brandLogoPath());
    values.put("stitch.sso.enabled", Boolean.toString(sso.enabled()));
    values.put("stitch.sso.mode", sso.mode().name());
    values.put("stitch.sso.spoof.enabled", Boolean.toString(sso.spoofEnabled()));
    values.put("stitch.sso.spoof.allowEditing", Boolean.toString(sso.spoofAllowEditing()));
    values.put("stitch.sso.spoof.cookieName", sso.spoofCookieName());
    if (sso.spoofDefaultUsername() != null) {
      values.put("stitch.sso.spoof.defaultUsername", sso.spoofDefaultUsername());
    }
    values.put(
        "stitch.sso.spoof.cookieMaxAgeSeconds",
        Integer.toString(sso.spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds()));
    values.put(
        "stitch.sso.spoof.controlVisible",
        Boolean.toString(sso.spoofControlVisible()));
    values.put("stitch.sso.fallbackSubject", sso.fallbackSubject());
    values.put("vaadin.pushMode", pushEnabled ? "AUTOMATIC" : "DISABLED");
    values.put("vaadin.copilot.enable", "false");
    values.put("vaadin.devmode.devTools.enabled", "false");
    return Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static int requirePort(int value) {
    if (value <= 0 || value > 65535) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("serverPort must be between 1 and 65535");
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeConnectionWarmupNames(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String candidate = trimmed.trim();
      if (!normalized.contains(candidate)) {
        normalized.add(candidate);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String appTitle = "Stitch Application";
    private int serverPort = 8080;
    private boolean pushEnabled = true;
    private boolean startupBannerEnabled;
    private boolean componentLabelsEnabled;
    private final List<String> connectionWarmupNames = new ArrayList<>();
    private String docsRootPath;
    private final Help.Builder helpBuilder = Help.builder();
    private final Shell.Builder shellBuilder = Shell.builder();
    private final Sso.Builder ssoBuilder = Sso.builder();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withAppTitle(String value) {
      this.appTitle = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServerPort(int value) {
      this.serverPort = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPushEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.pushEnabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withStartupBannerEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.startupBannerEnabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSpringBannerSuppressed(boolean value) {
      this.startupBannerEnabled = !value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withComponentLabelsEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.componentLabelsEnabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDebugComponentLabels(boolean value) {
      return withComponentLabelsEnabled(value);
    }

    public Builder withConnectionWarmup(String... connectionNames) {
      this.connectionWarmupNames.clear();
      appendConnectionWarmups(this.connectionWarmupNames, connectionNames);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addConnectionWarmup(String... connectionNames) {
      appendConnectionWarmups(this.connectionWarmupNames, connectionNames);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDocsRootPath(String value) {
      this.docsRootPath = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withHelpEnabled(boolean value) {
      helpBuilder.withMenuEnabled(value);
      helpBuilder.withReferenceEnabled(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withHelp(Consumer<Help.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(helpBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBrandLogoPath(String value) {
      shellBuilder.withBrandLogoPath(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBrandLogoAlt(String value) {
      shellBuilder.withBrandLogoAlt(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSso(Consumer<Sso.Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(ssoBuilder);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchSettings build() {
      return new StitchSettings(this);
    }

    private static void appendConnectionWarmups(List<String> target, String... values) {
      if (target == null || values == null || values.length == 0) {
        return;
      }
      for (String value : values) {
        String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (trimmed == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String candidate = trimmed.trim();
        if (!target.contains(candidate)) {
          target.add(candidate);
        }
      }
    }
  }

        this.referenceEnabled = value;
        return this;

      }
    }

  public static final class Shell {

      this.brandLogoPath = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(builder.brandLogoPath), DEFAULT_BRAND_LOGO_PATH);
      this.brandLogoAlt = Strings.trimToNull(builder.brandLogoAlt);

  public static final class Sso {
    private final SsoMode mode;
    private final boolean enabled;
    private final boolean forwardedHeadersEnabled;
    private final boolean spoofEnabled;
    private final boolean spoofAllowEditing;
    private final String spoofCookieName;
    private final String spoofDefaultUsername;
    private final int spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds;
    private final List<String> spoofUsers;
    private final List<String> spoofGroups;
    private final boolean spoofControlVisible;
    private final String fallbackSubject;
    private final FabricOidcConfig oidc;

    private Sso(Builder builder) {
      this.mode = builder.mode == null ? SsoMode.SPOOF : builder.mode;
      this.enabled = builder.enabled;
      this.forwardedHeadersEnabled = builder.forwardedHeadersEnabled;
      this.spoofEnabled = builder.spoofEnabled;
      this.spoofAllowEditing = builder.spoofAllowEditing;
      this.spoofCookieName =
          Strings.trimToNull(builder.spoofCookieName) == null
              ? "fabric_spoof_user"
              : builder.spoofCookieName.trim();
      this.spoofDefaultUsername = canonicalUser(builder.spoofDefaultUsername);
      this.spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds = builder.spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds <= 0 ? 60 * 60 * 24 * 30 : builder.spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds;
      this.spoofUsers = List.copyOf(canonicalUsers(builder.spoofUsers));
      this.spoofGroups = List.copyOf(trimmed(builder.spoofGroups));
      this.spoofControlVisible = builder.spoofControlVisible;
      this.fallbackSubject =
          Strings.trimToNull(builder.fallbackSubject) == null
              ? "service:stitch"
              : builder.fallbackSubject.trim();
      this.oidc = builder.oidc;
    }

    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public SsoMode mode() {
      return mode;
    }

    public boolean enabled() {
      return enabled;
    }

    public boolean forwardedHeadersEnabled() {
      return forwardedHeadersEnabled;
    }

    public boolean spoofEnabled() {
      return spoofEnabled;
    }

    public boolean spoofAllowEditing() {
      return spoofAllowEditing;
    }

    public String spoofCookieName() {
      return spoofCookieName;
    }

    public String spoofDefaultUsername() {
      return spoofDefaultUsername;
    }

    public int spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds() {
      return spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds;
    }

    public List<String> spoofUsers() {
      return spoofUsers;
    }

    public List<String> spoofGroups() {
      return spoofGroups;
    }

    public boolean spoofControlVisible() {
      return spoofControlVisible;
    }

    public String fallbackSubject() {
      return fallbackSubject;
    }

    public FabricOidcConfig oidc() {
      return oidc;
    }

    private static List<String> trimmed(List<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (trimmed != null) {
          normalized.add(trimmed);
        }
      }
      return normalized;
    }

    private static List<String> canonicalUsers(List<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of("alice", "bob", "bella", "lenny");
      }
      List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String canonical = canonicalUser(value);
        if (canonical != null) {
          normalized.add(canonical);
        }
      }
      return normalized;
    }

    private static String canonicalUser(String value) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed == null) {
        return null;
      }
      if (trimmed.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("user:")) {
        String id = Strings.trimToNull(trimmed.substring("user:".length()));
        return id == null ? null : "user:" + id;
      }
      return "user:" + trimmed;
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private SsoMode mode = SsoMode.SPOOF;
      private boolean enabled = true;
      private boolean forwardedHeadersEnabled = true;
      private boolean spoofEnabled = true;
      private boolean spoofAllowEditing = true;
      private String spoofCookieName = "fabric_spoof_user";
      private String spoofDefaultUsername = "user:alice";
      private int spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds = 60 * 60 * 24 * 30;
      private List<String> spoofUsers = List.of("alice", "bob", "bella", "lenny");
      private List<String> spoofGroups = List.of();
      private boolean spoofControlVisible;
      private String fallbackSubject = "service:stitch";
      private FabricOidcConfig oidc;

      private Builder() {}

      public Builder withMode(SsoMode value) {
        this.mode = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
        this.enabled = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withForwardedHeadersEnabled(boolean value) {
        this.forwardedHeadersEnabled = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofEnabled(boolean value) {
        this.spoofEnabled = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofAllowEditing(boolean value) {
        this.spoofAllowEditing = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofCookieName(String value) {
        this.spoofCookieName = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofDefaultUsername(String value) {
        this.spoofDefaultUsername = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds(int value) {
        this.spoofCookieMaxAgeSeconds = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofUsers(List<String> value) {
        this.spoofUsers = value == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(value);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofGroups(List<String> value) {
        this.spoofGroups = value == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(value);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSpoofControlVisible(boolean value) {
        this.spoofControlVisible = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withFallbackSubject(String value) {
        this.fallbackSubject = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withOidc(FabricOidcConfig value) {
        this.oidc = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withOidc(Consumer<FabricOidcConfig.Builder> customizer) {
        FabricOidcConfig.Builder oidcBuilder = FabricOidcConfig.builder();
        if (customizer != null) {
          customizer.accept(oidcBuilder);
        }
        this.oidc = oidcBuilder.build();
        return this;
      }

      private Sso build() {
        return new Sso(this);
      }
    }
  }

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.page.AppShellConfigurator;
import com.vaadin.flow.server.AppShellSettings;
import com.vaadin.flow.theme.Theme;
import com.vaadin.flow.theme.lumo.Lumo;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.theme.StitchTheme;
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication;

@Theme(value = StitchTheme.NAME, variant = Lumo.DARK)
@SpringBootApplication
public class StitchSpringRuntime implements AppShellConfigurator {
  private static volatile String pageTitle = "Stitch Application";
  private static volatile String faviconPath = "/images/studio.png";

  static void setPageTitle(String value) {
    pageTitle = Strings.trimToNull(value) == null ? "Stitch Application" : value.trim();
  }

  static void setFaviconPath(String value) {
    faviconPath = Strings.trimToNull(value) == null ? "/images/studio.png" : value.trim();
  }

  @Override
  public void configurePage(AppShellSettings settings) {
    settings.setPageTitle(pageTitle);
    settings.addFavIcon("icon", faviconPath, "any");
    settings.addLink("shortcut icon", faviconPath);
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/badge/StitchStatusBadge.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchStatusBadge extends Span {
  private Tone tone = Tone.NEUTRAL;

  public StitchStatusBadge() {
    this("", Tone.NEUTRAL);
  }

  public StitchStatusBadge(String text) {
    this(text, Tone.NEUTRAL);
  }

  public StitchStatusBadge(String text, Tone tone) {
    addClassName("stitch-status-badge");
    setTextValue(text);
    setTone(tone);
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_STATUS_BADGE);
  }

  public StitchStatusBadge setTextValue(String value) {
    setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchStatusBadge setTone(Tone value) {
    Tone next = value == null ? Tone.NEUTRAL : value;
    removeClassName(cssClass(tone));
    tone = next;
    addClassName(cssClass(next));
    return this;
  }

  public Tone tone() {
    return tone;
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge neutral(String text) {
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, Tone.NEUTRAL);
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge info(String text) {
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, Tone.INFO);
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge success(String text) {
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, Tone.SUCCESS);
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge warning(String text) {
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, Tone.WARNING);
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge error(String text) {
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, Tone.ERROR);
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge forEnum(Enum<?> value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return neutral("");
    }
    return forValue(value.name());
  }

  public static StitchStatusBadge forValue(String value) {
    String text = formatToken(value);
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, toneForValue(text));
  }

  public static Tone toneForValue(String value) {
    String normalized = formatToken(value);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return Tone.NEUTRAL;
    }
    if (isAny(normalized, "ONLINE", "RUNNING", "READY", "STARTED", "ENABLED", "SUCCESS", "UP", "ACTIVE", "TRUE")) {
      return Tone.SUCCESS;
    }
    if (isAny(normalized, "STALE", "WARNING", "WARN", "DEGRADED", "PENDING", "PARTIAL", "STARTING")) {
      return Tone.WARNING;
    }
    if (isAny(
        normalized,
        "OFFLINE",
        "ERROR",
        "FAILED",
        "FAIL",
        "DOWN",
        "STOPPED",
        "DISABLED",
        "DISCONNECTED",
        "CRITICAL",
        "FALSE")) {
      return Tone.ERROR;
    }
    if (isAny(normalized, "INFO", "INFORMATION", "NOTICE")) {
      return Tone.INFO;
    }
    if (isAny(normalized, "UNKNOWN", "NO STATUS")) {
      return Tone.NEUTRAL;
    }
    return fallbackTone(normalized);
  }

  private static String cssClass(Tone value) {
    return "stitch-status-badge--" + value.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static boolean isAny(String value, String... tokens) {
    for (String token : tokens) {
      if (value.equals(token)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static Tone fallbackTone(String value) {
    int slot = Math.floorMod(value.hashCode(), 3);
    return switch (slot) {
      case 0 -> Tone.INFO;
      case 1 -> Tone.SUCCESS;
      default -> Tone.WARNING;
    };
  }

  private static String formatToken(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim().replace('-', '_').replace(' ', '_').toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT).replace('_', ' ');
  }

  public enum Tone {
    NEUTRAL,
    INFO,
    SUCCESS,
    WARNING,
    ERROR
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchActionIcons.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import java.util.Locale;

/** Shared curated Feather icon mapping for row and toolbar actions. */
public final class StitchActionIcons {
  private StitchActionIcons() {}

  public static Component forAction(String label, VaadinIcon fallback) {
    Span icon = new Span();
    icon.addClassName("stitch-feather-icon");
    icon.addClassName("stitch-feather-icon--" + resolveIconKey(label, fallback));
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private static String resolveIconKey(String label, VaadinIcon fallback) {
    String normalized = normalize(label);
    if (containsAny(normalized, "JSON", "PAYLOAD", "DOCUMENT", "CODE")) {
      return "code";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "EDIT")) {
      return "edit-2";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "DELETE", "REJECT", "ROLLBACK", "REMOVE")) {
      return "trash-2";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "RUN", "PLAY", "LIVE", "START")) {
      return "play";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "EXPAND")) {
      return "chevrons-down";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "COLLAPSE")) {
      return "chevrons-up";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "REFRESH", "RELOAD")) {
      return "refresh-cw";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "RELATED", "LINK", "SESSION", "NAMESPACE")) {
      return "link-2";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "SHIELD", "ENTITLEMENT")) {
      return "shield";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "TABLE")) {
      return "table";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "CLOSE", "CANCEL")) {
      return "x";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "COPY")) {
      return "copy";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "OPEN", "EXTERNAL")) {
      return "external-link";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "DETAIL", "INFO", "INSPECT")) {
      return "sliders";
    }
    if (containsAny(normalized, "VIEW")) {
      return "eye";
    }
    return resolveIconFromFallback(fallback);
  }

  private static String resolveIconFromFallback(VaadinIcon fallback) {
    if (fallback == null) {
      return "eye";
    }
    return switch (fallback) {
      case EDIT -> "edit-2";
      case EXTERNAL_LINK -> "external-link";
      case FILE_CODE, CODE -> "code";
      case LINK, SHARE -> "link-2";
      case PLAY -> "play";
      case TABLE -> "table";
      case SHIELD -> "shield";
      case REFRESH -> "refresh-cw";
      case ANGLE_DOUBLE_DOWN, ANGLE_DOWN, PLUS_SQUARE_O -> "chevrons-down";
      case ANGLE_DOUBLE_UP, ANGLE_UP, MINUS_SQUARE_O -> "chevrons-up";
      case INFO_CIRCLE, INFO_CIRCLE_O -> "sliders";
      default -> "eye";
    };
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static boolean containsAny(String value, String... tokens) {
    if (value.isBlank() || tokens == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String token : tokens) {
      if (token != null && !token.isBlank() && value.contains(token)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchActionStyles.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import java.util.Locale;

/** Shared semantic action styling for Stitch buttons. */
public final class StitchActionStyles {
  private static final String TONE_PRIMARY = "stitch-action-primary";
  private static final String TONE_SECONDARY = "stitch-action-secondary";
  private static final String TONE_NEUTRAL = "stitch-action-neutral";
  private static final String TONE_DANGER = "stitch-action-danger";

  private StitchActionStyles() {}

  public static void applyPrimary(Button button) {
    apply(button, TONE_PRIMARY);
  }

  public static void applySecondary(Button button) {
    apply(button, TONE_SECONDARY);
  }

  public static void applyNeutral(Button button) {
    apply(button, TONE_NEUTRAL);
  }

  public static void applyDanger(Button button) {
    apply(button, TONE_DANGER);
  }

  public static void applyByLabel(Button button, String label) {
    if (button == null) {
      return;
    }
    String normalized = normalize(label);
    if (normalized.contains("SAVE")
        || normalized.contains("SUBMIT")
        || normalized.contains("APPLY")
        || normalized.contains("APPROVE")) {
      applyPrimary(button);
      return;
    }
    if (normalized.contains("DELETE")
        || normalized.contains("REJECT")
        || normalized.contains("ROLLBACK")
        || normalized.contains("NUCLEAR")
        || normalized.contains("EMERGENCY")) {
      applyDanger(button);
      return;
    }
    if (normalized.contains("CANCEL")
        || normalized.contains("CLOSE")
        || normalized.contains("CLEAR")
        || normalized.contains("RESET")) {
      applyNeutral(button);
      return;
    }
    applySecondary(button);
  }

  private static void apply(Button button, String toneClass) {
    if (button == null) {
      return;
    }
    button.removeClassName(TONE_PRIMARY);
    button.removeClassName(TONE_SECONDARY);
    button.removeClassName(TONE_NEUTRAL);
    button.removeClassName(TONE_DANGER);
    button.addClassName(toneClass);
    button.removeThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchBooleanToggle.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;

public class StitchBooleanToggle extends Checkbox {
  private static final String DEFAULT_ARIA_LABEL = "Toggle value";

  public StitchBooleanToggle() {
    this(null, false);
  }

  public StitchBooleanToggle(String label) {
    this(label, false);
  }

  public StitchBooleanToggle(String label, boolean initialValue) {
    super(label, initialValue);
    addClassName("stitch-boolean-toggle");
    if (label == null || label.isBlank()) {
      setAriaLabel(DEFAULT_ARIA_LABEL);
    } else {
      setAriaLabel(label.trim());
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchEmptyState.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Paragraph;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchEmptyState extends VerticalLayout {
  private final Span title = new Span();
  private final Paragraph message = new Paragraph();
  private Component icon;

  public StitchEmptyState() {
    this("No results", "Try adjusting filters or search.");
  }

  public StitchEmptyState(String emptyTitle, String emptyMessage) {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    addClassName("stitch-empty-state");
    getElement().setAttribute("role", "status");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    title.addClassName("stitch-empty-state-title");
    message.addClassName("stitch-empty-state-message");

    setTitle(emptyTitle);
    setMessage(emptyMessage);

    add(title, message);
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_EMPTY_STATE);
  }

  public StitchEmptyState setTitle(String value) {
    title.setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    title.setVisible(!title.getText().isBlank());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchEmptyState setMessage(String value) {
    message.setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    message.setVisible(!message.getText().isBlank());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchEmptyState setIcon(Component component) {
    if (icon != null) {
      remove(icon);
      icon = null;
    }
    if (component != null) {
      icon = component;
      icon.addClassName("stitch-empty-state-icon");
      addComponentAsFirst(icon);
    }
    return this;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchFiltersBar.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/** Shared top-of-screen filter/action row for Stitch screens. */
public final class StitchFiltersBar extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final HorizontalLayout filters = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout actions = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final List<Component> middleFilters = new ArrayList<>();
  private Component groupSelector;
  private Component searchFilter;

  public StitchFiltersBar() {
    setWidthFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.END);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    addClassName("stitch-filters-bar");
    getElement().setAttribute("role", "toolbar");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Page filters");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_FILTERS_BAR);

    filters.setPadding(false);
    filters.setSpacing(false);
    filters.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.END);
    filters.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    filters.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    filters.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    filters.addClassName("stitch-filters-bar-left");
    StitchComponents.withCode(filters, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_FILTERS_BAR_LEFT);

    actions.setPadding(false);
    actions.setSpacing(false);
    actions.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    actions.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    actions.getStyle().set("margin-inline-start", "auto");
    actions.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    actions.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    actions.addClassName("stitch-filters-bar-right");
    StitchComponents.withCode(actions, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_FILTERS_BAR_RIGHT);

    Div spacer = new Div();
    spacer.getStyle().set("flex", "1 1 auto");
    spacer.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    add(filters, spacer, actions);
    expand(spacer);
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withGroupSelector(Component component) {
    if (component == null) {
      return this;
    }
    component.addClassName("stitch-filters-group-selector");
    if (component == searchFilter) {
      searchFilter = null;
    }
    middleFilters.remove(component);
    groupSelector = component;
    syncFilterOrder();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withFilter(Component component) {
    if (component == null) {
      return this;
    }
    if (isGroupSelector(component)) {
      return withGroupSelector(component);
    }
    if (isSearchFilter(component)) {
      return withSearch(component);
    }
    if (component == groupSelector) {
      groupSelector = null;
    }
    if (component == searchFilter) {
      searchFilter = null;
    }
    middleFilters.remove(component);
    middleFilters.add(component);
    syncFilterOrder();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withFilters(Component... components) {
    if (components == null) {
      return this;
    }
    for (Component component : components) {
      withFilter(component);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withRightAction(Component component) {
    if (component != null) {
      actions.add(component);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withRightActionFirst(Component component) {
    if (component == null) {
      return this;
    }
    actions.remove(component);
    actions.addComponentAtIndex(0, component);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withRightActions(Component... components) {
    if (components == null) {
      return this;
    }
    for (Component component : components) {
      withRightAction(component);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withSearch(Optional<? extends Component> search) {
    if (search != null) {
      search.ifPresent(
          value -> {
            if (value == groupSelector) {
              groupSelector = null;
            }
            middleFilters.remove(value);
            searchFilter = value;
            syncFilterOrder();
          });
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar withSearch(Component search) {
    return withSearch(Optional.ofNullable(search));
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar clearFilters() {
    groupSelector = null;
    searchFilter = null;
    middleFilters.clear();
    filters.removeAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar clearActions() {
    actions.removeAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchFiltersBar clear() {
    clearFilters();
    clearActions();
    return this;
  }

  private void syncFilterOrder() {
    filters.removeAll();
    if (groupSelector != null) {
      filters.add(groupSelector);
    }
    for (Component filter : middleFilters) {
      if (filter != null) {
        filters.add(filter);
      }
    }
    if (searchFilter != null) {
      filters.add(searchFilter);
    }
  }

  private static boolean isSearchFilter(Component component) {
    if (component == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (component.getClassNames().contains("stitch-results-search")) {
      return true;
    }
    String simpleName = component.getClass().getSimpleName();
    if ("StitchResultsSearch".equals(simpleName)) {
      return true;
    }
    return matchesToken(component, "search");
  }

  private static boolean isGroupSelector(Component component) {
    if (component == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return component.getClassNames().contains("stitch-filters-group-selector")
        || component.getClassNames().contains("stitch-group-filter")
        || matchesToken(component, "group");
  }

  private static boolean matchesToken(Component component, String token) {
    if (component == null || token == null || token.isBlank()) {
      return false;
    }
    String normalizedToken = token.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    String placeholder = normalize(component.getElement().getProperty("placeholder"));
    String label = normalize(component.getElement().getProperty("label"));
    String aria = normalize(component.getElement().getAttribute("aria-label"));
    return placeholder.contains(normalizedToken)
        || label.contains(normalizedToken)
        || aria.contains(normalizedToken);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchGroupFilter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.server.VaadinServletRequest;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoAttributes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoPrincipal;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchGroupAccess;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchGroupSelectionContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/**
 * Standard reusable Stitch group filter.
 *
 * <p>Semantics:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>Admin users (platform group) see "All" + all configured groups.
 *   <li>Non-admin users see "All" + their own membership groups.
 * </ul>
 */
public class StitchGroupFilter extends Select<StitchGroupFilter.Option> {
  private static final String ALL_KEY = "__all__";
  private static final String ALL_LABEL = "All";
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = StitchGroupAccess.PLATFORM_ADMIN_GROUP;

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchGroupAccess groupAccess;
  private List<String> currentVisibleGroups = List.of();
  private boolean currentAdmin;

  public StitchGroupFilter(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this(runtimeContext, null);
  }

  public StitchGroupFilter(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchGroupAccess groupAccess) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.groupAccess = groupAccess;
    addClassName("stitch-group-filter");
    setLabel("");
    setPlaceholder("GROUP");
    setAriaLabel("Group");
    setWidth("220px");
    setItemLabelGenerator(value -> value == null ? "" : value.label());
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_GROUP_FILTER);
    addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient()) {
            return;
          }
          StitchGroupSelectionContext.remember(selectedGroup());
        });
    refresh();
  }

  public void refresh() {
    String subject = StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
    StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope = resolveScope(subject);
    currentAdmin = scope.admin();
    currentVisibleGroups = List.copyOf(scope.visibleGroups());
    Option current = getValue();
    List<Option> options = toOptions(currentVisibleGroups);
    setItems(options);
    Option next = resolveSelection(current, options, StitchGroupSelectionContext.current());
    if (next == null) {
      clear();
    } else {
      setValue(next);
    }
    setEnabled(!currentVisibleGroups.isEmpty());
  }

  private StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope resolveScope(String subject) {
    StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope configured = scopeFromConfiguredAccess(subject);
    if (hasGroups(configured)) {
      return configured;
    }
    StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope lazyRuntime = scopeFromRuntimeSession(subject);
    if (hasGroups(lazyRuntime)) {
      return lazyRuntime;
    }
    return scopeFromSsoPrincipal(subject);
  }

  private StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scopeFromConfiguredAccess(String subject) {
    if (groupAccess == null) {
      return emptyScope(subject);
    }
    try {
      StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope = groupAccess.scopeForSubject(subject);
      return scope == null ? emptyScope(subject) : scope;
    } catch (RuntimeException ignore) {
      return emptyScope(subject);
    }
  }

  private StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scopeFromRuntimeSession(String subject) {
    try {
      StitchGroupAccess access = new StitchGroupAccess(runtimeContext.session());
      StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope = access.scopeForSubject(subject);
      return scope == null ? emptyScope(subject) : scope;
    } catch (RuntimeException ignore) {
      return emptyScope(subject);
    }
  }

  private StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scopeFromSsoPrincipal(String subject) {
    List<String> subjectGroups = groupsFromCurrentPrincipal();
    List<String> configuredGroups = normalizeSorted(runtimeContext.settings().sso().spoofGroups());
    boolean admin = containsIgnoreCase(subjectGroups, PLATFORM_GROUP);
    List<String> visible = admin && !configuredGroups.isEmpty() ? configuredGroups : subjectGroups;
    return new StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope(subject, admin, visible, configuredGroups, subjectGroups);
  }

  private static List<String> groupsFromCurrentPrincipal() {
    VaadinServletRequest current = VaadinServletRequest.getCurrent();
    HttpServletRequest request = current == null ? null : current.getHttpServletRequest();
    if (request == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Object currentPrincipal = request.getAttribute(SsoAttributes.CURRENT_PRINCIPAL);
    if (currentPrincipal instanceof SsoPrincipal principal) {
      return normalizeSorted(readGroupsValue(principal.attributes().get("groups")));
    }
    if (currentPrincipal instanceof Map<?, ?> values) {
      return normalizeSorted(readGroupsValue(values.get("groups")));
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  private static List<String> readGroupsValue(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof Collection<?> values) {
      List<String> groups = new ArrayList<>(values.size());
      for (Object entry : values) {
        if (entry != null) {
          groups.add(entry.toString());
        }
      }
      return List.copyOf(groups);
    }
    if (value instanceof String text) {
      String trimmed = text.trim();
      if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      if (trimmed.contains(",")) {
        String[] parts = trimmed.split(",");
        List<String> groups = new ArrayList<>(parts.length);
        for (String part : parts) {
          groups.add(part);
        }
        return List.copyOf(groups);
      }
      return List.of(trimmed);
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  private static boolean hasGroups(StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope) {
    if (scope == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return !(scope.visibleGroups().isEmpty()
        && scope.configuredGroups().isEmpty()
        && scope.subjectGroups().isEmpty());
  }

  private static StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope emptyScope(String subject) {
    return new StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope(subject, false, List.of(), List.of(), List.of());
  }

  public boolean admin() {
    return currentAdmin;
  }

  public List<String> visibleGroups() {
    return List.copyOf(currentVisibleGroups);
  }

  /**
   * Returns effective groups for filtering calls on the owning page.
   *
   * <p>"All" resolves to all visible groups for this user.
   */
  public List<String> effectiveGroups() {
    Option selected = getValue();
    if (selected == null || ALL_KEY.equals(selected.key())) {
      return List.copyOf(currentVisibleGroups);
    }
    String group = normalizeGroup(selected.key());
    if (group == null || !containsIgnoreCase(currentVisibleGroups, group)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return List.of(resolveCanonical(currentVisibleGroups, group));
  }

  /**
   * Returns the explicit group selected in the filter, or {@code null} when the filter is on
   * "All"/unset.
   */
  public String selectedGroup() {
    Option selected = getValue();
    if (selected == null || ALL_KEY.equals(selected.key())) {
      return null;
    }
    String group = normalizeGroup(selected.key());
    if (group == null || !containsIgnoreCase(currentVisibleGroups, group)) {
      return null;
    }
    return resolveCanonical(currentVisibleGroups, group);
  }

  private static Option resolveSelection(Option current, List<Option> options, String rememberedGroup) {
    if (options == null || options.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (current != null) {
      for (Option option : options) {
        if (option != null && current.key().equals(option.key())) {
          return option;
        }
      }
    }
    String remembered = normalizeGroup(rememberedGroup);
    if (remembered != null) {
      for (Option option : options) {
        if (option == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (remembered.equalsIgnoreCase(option.key())) {
          return option;
        }
      }
    }
    return options.get(0);
  }

  private static List<Option> toOptions(List<String> groups) {
    LinkedHashSet<Option> options = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    options.add(new Option(ALL_KEY, ALL_LABEL));
    if (groups != null) {
      List<String> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String group : groups) {
        String normalized = normalizeGroup(group);
        if (normalized != null) {
          ordered.add(normalized);
        }
      }
      ordered.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
      for (String group : ordered) {
        options.add(new Option(group, group));
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(options);
  }

  private static boolean containsIgnoreCase(List<String> values, String value) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String candidate : values) {
      if (candidate != null && value.equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.trim())) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String resolveCanonical(List<String> values, String value) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || value == null) {
      return value;
    }
    for (String candidate : values) {
      if (candidate != null && value.equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.trim())) {
        return candidate;
      }
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeSorted(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String group = normalizeGroup(value);
      if (group != null) {
        normalized.add(group);
      }
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(normalized);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static String normalizeGroup(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("group:")
        && normalized.length() > "group:".length()) {
      normalized = normalized.substring("group:".length());
    }
    normalized = normalized.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }

  public record Option(String key, String label) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
