/** Shared inspector composition block for tree-browser detail panels. */
public final class StitchInspectorPreviewPanel extends VerticalLayout {
  private final Span contextLine = new Span();
  private final FormLayout metadataForm = new FormLayout();
  private final TextArea previewField = new TextArea();

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel(String previewLabel, String previewAriaLabel) {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();

    contextLine.setWidthFull();
    contextLine.setVisible(false);
    contextLine.addClassName("stitch-inspector-context");

    metadataForm.setWidthFull();
    metadataForm.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("46em", 2));
    metadataForm.addClassName("stitch-inspector-metadata");

    previewField.setLabel(Strings.trimToNull(previewLabel) == null ? "Preview" : previewLabel.trim());
    previewField.setWidthFull();
    previewField.setMinHeight("20rem");
    previewField.setReadOnly(true);
    previewField.setAriaLabel(
        Strings.trimToNull(previewAriaLabel) == null ? "Inspector preview" : previewAriaLabel.trim());
    previewField.getStyle().set("font-family", "monospace");
    previewField.addClassName("stitch-inspector-preview");

    add(contextLine, metadataForm, previewField);
  }

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel setContext(String label, String value) {
    String normalizedValue = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalizedValue == null) {
      contextLine.setText("");
      contextLine.setVisible(false);
      return this;
    }
    String prefix = Strings.trimToNull(label);
    contextLine.setText((prefix == null ? "Selection" : prefix) + ": " + normalizedValue);
    contextLine.setVisible(true);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel setMetadata(Map<String, String> fields) {
    metadataForm.removeAll();
    Map<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (fields != null) {
      normalized.putAll(fields);
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : normalized.entrySet()) {
      String label = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      if (label == null) {
        continue;
      }
      TextField field = readOnlyField(label);
      field.setValue(Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue()) == null ? "-" : entry.getValue().trim());
      metadataForm.add(field);
    }
    metadataForm.setVisible(metadataForm.getChildren().findAny().isPresent());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel setPreviewValue(String value) {
    previewField.setValue(Strings.trimToEmpty(value));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel setPreviewReadOnly(boolean value) {
    previewField.setReadOnly(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel setPreviewAriaLabel(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    previewField.setAriaLabel(normalized == null ? "Inspector preview" : normalized);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchInspectorPreviewPanel setPreviewVisible(boolean value) {
    previewField.setVisible(value);
    return this;
  }

  public TextArea previewField() {
    return previewField;
  }

  public Button createJsonAction(Runnable onClick, String ariaLabel) {
    Button json = blueAction("JSON", ariaLabel);
    if (onClick != null) {
      json.addClickListener(event -> onClick.run());
    }
    return json;
  }

  public Button createCopyAction(String copiedMessage, String emptyMessage, String ariaLabel) {
    Button copy = blueAction("COPY", ariaLabel);
    copy.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (!StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell.copyText(this, previewField.getValue())) {
            String empty = Strings.trimToNull(emptyMessage);
            if (empty != null) {
              Notification.show(empty, 1200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            }
            return;
          }
          String copied = Strings.trimToNull(copiedMessage);
          if (copied != null) {
            Notification.show(copied, 1200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
          }
        });
    return copy;
  }

  public Button createCloseAction(Runnable onClose, String ariaLabel) {
    Button close = new Button("CLOSE");
    if (onClose != null) {
      close.addClickListener(event -> onClose.run());
    }
    close.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(close);
    close.addClassName("stitch-dialog-close-action");
    close.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", normalizeAria(ariaLabel, "Close inspector"));
    return close;
  }

  private static Button blueAction(String text, String ariaLabel) {
    Button button = new Button(text);
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(button);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", normalizeAria(ariaLabel, text));
    return button;
  }

  private static TextField readOnlyField(String label) {
    TextField field = new TextField(label);
    field.setReadOnly(true);
    field.setWidthFull();
    field.addClassName("stitch-inspector-readonly-field");
    return field;
  }

  private static String normalizeAria(String value, String fallback) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? fallback : normalized;
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchJsonDiffPanel.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.GridVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.workflow.ConfigJsonDiff;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;

/** Shared left-json / diff-summary / right-json panel for read-only payload comparisons. */
public final class StitchJsonDiffPanel extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final Span leftHeader = new Span("Left");
  private final Span rightHeader = new Span("Right");
  private final TextArea leftJson = readOnlyJson("Left JSON payload");
  private final TextArea rightJson = readOnlyJson("Right JSON payload");
  private final Span summary = new Span("No differences found.");
  private final Grid<DiffRowView> diffGrid = new Grid<>(DiffRowView.class, false);
  private List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> rows = List.of();

  public StitchJsonDiffPanel() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    setHeight("28rem");

    VerticalLayout left = sidePanel(leftHeader, leftJson);
    VerticalLayout center = centerPanel();
    VerticalLayout right = sidePanel(rightHeader, rightJson);

    setFlexGrow(1.0, left);
    setFlexGrow(1.2, center);
    setFlexGrow(1.0, right);
    add(left, center, right);
  }

  public StitchJsonDiffPanel setComparison(
      String leftLabel, JsonNode leftPayload, String rightLabel, JsonNode rightPayload) {
    String safeLeftLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(leftLabel), "Left");
    String safeRightLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rightLabel), "Right");
    leftHeader.setText(safeLeftLabel);
    rightHeader.setText(safeRightLabel);
    leftJson.setAriaLabel(safeLeftLabel + " JSON payload");
    rightJson.setAriaLabel(safeRightLabel + " JSON payload");
    leftJson.setValue(prettyJson(leftPayload));
    rightJson.setValue(prettyJson(rightPayload));

    rows = ConfigJsonDiff.diff(safePayload(leftPayload), safePayload(rightPayload));
    summary.setText(rows.isEmpty() ? "No differences found." : "Changed fields: " + rows.size());
    diffGrid.setItems(
        rows.stream()
            .map(
                row ->
                    new DiffRowView(
                        Strings.firstNonBlank(row.path(), "<root>"),
                        row.change(),
                        row.oldValue() == null ? "-" : ConfigJsonDiff.formatJsonScalar(row.oldValue()),
                        row.newValue() == null ? "-" : ConfigJsonDiff.formatJsonScalar(row.newValue())))
            .toList());
    return this;
  }

  public List<ConfigJsonDiff.DiffRow> rows() {
    return rows;
  }

  private VerticalLayout centerPanel() {
    Span header = new Span("Diff Summary");
    header.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");

    summary.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    diffGrid.setWidthFull();
    diffGrid.setHeightFull();
    diffGrid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_ROW_STRIPES);
    diffGrid.addColumn(DiffRowView::path).setHeader("Path").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    diffGrid
        .addComponentColumn(row -> changeBadge(row.change()))
        .setHeader("Change")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    diffGrid.addColumn(DiffRowView::leftValue).setHeader("Left").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    diffGrid.addColumn(DiffRowView::rightValue).setHeader("Right").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    diffGrid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "JSON diff summary table");

    VerticalLayout panel = new VerticalLayout(header, summary, diffGrid);
    panel.setPadding(false);
    panel.setSpacing(true);
    panel.setWidthFull();
    panel.setHeightFull();
    panel.setAlignItems(Alignment.STRETCH);
    return panel;
  }

  private static VerticalLayout sidePanel(Span header, TextArea area) {
    header.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");
    VerticalLayout panel = new VerticalLayout(header, area);
    panel.setPadding(false);
    panel.setSpacing(true);
    panel.setWidthFull();
    panel.setHeightFull();
    panel.setAlignItems(Alignment.STRETCH);
    panel.setFlexGrow(1.0, area);
    return panel;
  }

  private static TextArea readOnlyJson(String ariaLabel) {
    TextArea area = new TextArea();
    area.setReadOnly(true);
    area.setWidthFull();
    area.setHeightFull();
    area.setAriaLabel(ariaLabel);
    area.getStyle().set("font-family", "monospace");
    return area;
  }

  private static Component changeBadge(ConfigJsonDiff.Change change) {
    ConfigJsonDiff.Change safe = change == null ? ConfigJsonDiff.Change.MODIFIED : change;
    StitchStatusBadge.Tone tone =
        switch (safe) {
          case ADDED -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.SUCCESS;
          case REMOVED -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.ERROR;
          case MODIFIED -> StitchStatusBadge.Tone.WARNING;
        };
    return new StitchStatusBadge(safe.name(), tone);
  }

  private static JsonNode safePayload(JsonNode value) {
    return value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
  }

  private static String prettyJson(JsonNode value) {
    JsonNode normalized = value == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : value;
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(normalized);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return normalized.toString();
    }
  }

  private record DiffRowView(
      String path, ConfigJsonDiff.Change change, String leftValue, String rightValue) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchResultsPagination.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.Icon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.function.SerializableConsumer;
import com.vaadin.flow.function.SerializableRunnable;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchResultsPagination extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final Button previous = new Button(new Icon(VaadinIcon.CHEVRON_LEFT_SMALL));
  private final Button next = new Button(new Icon(VaadinIcon.CHEVRON_RIGHT_SMALL));
  private final Span pageInfo = new Span();
  private final Select<Integer> pageSize = new Select<>();

  private SerializableRunnable onPrevious = () -> {};
  private SerializableRunnable onNext = () -> {};
  private SerializableConsumer<Integer> onPageSizeChanged = value -> {};
  private List<Integer> pageSizeOptions = List.of(25, 50, 100);
  private int pageSizeValue = 25;

  public StitchResultsPagination() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.35rem");
    addClassName("stitch-results-pagination");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Pagination");

    configureNavButton(previous, "Previous page");
    configureNavButton(next, "Next page");
    previous.addClickListener(event -> onPrevious.run());
    next.addClickListener(event -> onNext.run());

    pageInfo.setText("Page 1 of 1");
    pageInfo.addClassName("stitch-results-page-info");
    pageInfo.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    pageSize.addClassName("stitch-results-page-size");
    pageSize.setAriaLabel("Rows per page");
    pageSize.setItems(pageSizeOptions);
    pageSize.setValue(pageSizeValue);
    pageSize.setWidth("4.75rem");
    pageSize.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Rows per page");
    pageSize.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          Integer value = event.getValue();
          if (value == null || value <= 0) {
            return;
          }
          pageSizeValue = value;
          onPageSizeChanged.accept(pageSizeValue);
        });

    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_PAGINATION);
    StitchComponents.withCode(pageInfo, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_PAGE_INFO);
    StitchComponents.withCode(pageSize, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_PAGE_SIZE);

    add(previous, next, pageInfo, pageSize);
    setPageState(0, 1, 0);
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination onPrevious(SerializableRunnable callback) {
    onPrevious = callback == null ? () -> {} : callback;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination onNext(SerializableRunnable callback) {
    onNext = callback == null ? () -> {} : callback;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination onPageSizeChange(SerializableConsumer<Integer> callback) {
    onPageSizeChanged = callback == null ? value -> {} : callback;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination setPageSizeOptions(int... options) {
    LinkedHashSet<Integer> unique = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (options != null) {
      for (int option : options) {
        if (option > 0) {
          unique.add(option);
        }
      }
    }
    if (unique.isEmpty()) {
      unique.add(25);
      unique.add(50);
      unique.add(100);
    }
    pageSizeOptions = new ArrayList<>(unique);
    pageSize.setItems(pageSizeOptions);
    if (!pageSizeOptions.contains(pageSizeValue)) {
      pageSizeValue = pageSizeOptions.getFirst();
    }
    pageSize.setValue(pageSizeValue);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination setPageSize(int value) {
    if (value <= 0) {
      return this;
    }
    if (!pageSizeOptions.contains(value)) {
      List<Integer> expanded = new ArrayList<>(pageSizeOptions);
      expanded.add(value);
      pageSizeOptions = expanded;
      pageSize.setItems(pageSizeOptions);
    }
    pageSizeValue = value;
    pageSize.setValue(pageSizeValue);
    return this;
  }

  public int pageSize() {
    return pageSizeValue;
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination setPageState(int zeroBasedPage, int totalPages, int totalItems) {
    int pageCount = Math.max(1, totalPages);
    int pageIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(zeroBasedPage, pageCount - 1));
    pageInfo.setText("Page " + (pageIndex + 1) + " of " + pageCount + " (" + Math.max(0, totalItems) + ")");
    previous.setEnabled(pageIndex > 0 && totalItems > 0);
    next.setEnabled(pageIndex + 1 < pageCount && totalItems > 0);
    return this;
  }

  private void configureNavButton(Button button, String label) {
    button.addThemeVariants(
        ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE, ButtonVariant.LUMO_ICON);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", label);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchResultsSearch.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextFieldVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.data.value.ValueChangeMode;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/**
 * Reusable Stitch search field for live results filtering.
 *
 * <p>Behavior is shared by default:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>small compact variant
 *   <li>clear button
 *   <li>eager value changes while typing
 *   <li>consistent accessibility defaults
 * </ul>
 */
public class StitchResultsSearch extends TextField {
  public StitchResultsSearch() {
    this("Search", "Search results");
  }

  public StitchResultsSearch(String placeholder, String ariaLabel) {
    addClassName("stitch-results-search");
    setPlaceholder(placeholder == null || placeholder.isBlank() ? "Search" : placeholder.trim());
    setAriaLabel(ariaLabel == null || ariaLabel.isBlank() ? "Search results" : ariaLabel.trim());
    setClearButtonVisible(true);
    addThemeVariants(TextFieldVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    setValueChangeMode(ValueChangeMode.EAGER);
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_SEARCH);
  }

  public String normalizedQuery() {
    return normalize(getValue());
  }

  public boolean matches(String value) {
    String query = normalizedQuery();
    if (query.isBlank()) {
      return true;
    }
    return normalize(value).contains(query);
  }

  public Registration onQueryChange(Consumer<String> listener) {
    Consumer<String> callback = Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    return addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.accept(normalizedQuery()));
  }

  public static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

  public StitchResultsToolbar addLabeledFilter(String label, Component component) {

    field.setPadding(false);
    field.setSpacing(false);
    field.setWidth(null);
    field.getStyle().set("gap", "0.2rem");
    field.getStyle().set("flex", "0 0 auto");
    field.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    field.addClassName("stitch-results-filter-field");

    String normalizedLabel = label == null ? "" : label.trim();
    Span caption = new Span(normalizedLabel.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
    caption.addClassName("stitch-results-filter-label");
    caption.setVisible(!caption.getText().isBlank());
    if (!normalizedLabel.isBlank()) {
      String labelId = "stitch-results-filter-label-" + FILTER_LABEL_SEQUENCE.incrementAndGet();
      caption.getElement().setAttribute("id", labelId);
      if (!component.getElement().hasAttribute("aria-label")) {
        component.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", normalizedLabel);
      }
      if (!component.getElement().hasAttribute("aria-labelledby")) {
        component.getElement().setAttribute("aria-labelledby", labelId);
      }
    }

    field.add(caption, component);
    filters.add(field);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsToolbar addEnd(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      end.add(components);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public static void stylePrimaryAction(Button button) {
    if (button == null) {
      return;
    }
    button.removeClassName("stitch-action-primary");
    button.removeClassName("stitch-action-secondary");
    button.removeClassName("stitch-action-neutral");
    button.removeClassName("stitch-action-danger");
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
  }

  public static void styleSecondaryAction(Button button) {
    if (button == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(button);
  }

  public static Button createRefreshAction() {
    Button refresh =
        new Button("REFRESH", event -> event.getSource().getUI().ifPresent(ui -> ui.getPage().reload()));
    StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(refresh);
    refresh.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh results");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh results");
    return refresh;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchSectionHeader.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.stream.Stream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/** Shared split header with LEFT / RIGHT slots for section and panel headers. */
public final class StitchSectionHeader extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final HorizontalLayout left = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout right = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final Span title = new Span();

  public StitchSectionHeader(String titleText) {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    setJustifyContentMode(JustifyContentMode.BETWEEN);
    addClassName("stitch-section-header");

    left.setPadding(false);
    left.setSpacing(false);
    left.setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    left.addClassName("stitch-section-header-left");

    right.setPadding(false);
    right.setSpacing(false);
    right.setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    right.addClassName("stitch-section-header-right");

    title.addClassName("stitch-section-header-title");
    title.getElement().setAttribute("role", "heading");
    title.getElement().setAttribute("aria-level", "2");

    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_HEADER);
    StitchComponents.withCode(left, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_HEADER_LEFT);
    StitchComponents.withCode(right, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_HEADER_RIGHT);
    StitchComponents.withCode(title, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_HEADER_TITLE);

    left.add(title);
    add(left, right);
    expand(left);
    withTitle(titleText);
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader withTitle(String value) {
    title.setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    title.setVisible(!title.getText().isBlank());
    if (title.getParent().isEmpty()) {
      left.addComponentAsFirst(title);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader withLeft(Component... components) {
    clearLeft();
    addLeft(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader withRight(Component... components) {
    clearRight();
    addRight(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader addLeft(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      Stream.of(components).filter(Objects::nonNull).forEach(left::add);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader addRight(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      Stream.of(components).filter(Objects::nonNull).forEach(right::add);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader clearLeft() {
    left.removeAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSectionHeader clearRight() {
    right.removeAll();
    return this;
  }

  public HorizontalLayout left() {
    return left;
  }

  public HorizontalLayout right() {
    return right;
  }

  public Span title() {
    return title;
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchShellUserArea.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchSettings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/** Standard shell user-area widget for Stitch applications. */
public final class StitchShellUserArea {

  private StitchShellUserArea() {}

  public static Component create(StitchRuntimeContext context) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    StitchSettings settings = context.settings();
    boolean spoofControlEnabled =
        settings.sso().spoofControlVisible()
            && settings.sso().enabled()
            && settings.sso().spoofEnabled();
    if (spoofControlEnabled) {
      return spoofSelect(settings);
    }
    String subject = StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(settings.sso().fallbackSubject());
    Span label = new Span(displayUser(subject));
    label.addClassName("stitch-user-label");
    label.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Signed in user");
    return label;
  }

  private static Select<UserOption> spoofSelect(StitchSettings settings) {
    Select<UserOption> select = new Select<>();
    select.addClassName("stitch-sso-subject");
    select.setAriaLabel("Signed in user");
    select.setItemLabelGenerator(value -> value == null ? "" : value.label());
    List<UserOption> options = options(settings);
    select.setItems(options);
    UserOption current = resolveCurrent(options, settings);
    if (current != null) {
      select.setValue(current);
    } else if (!options.isEmpty()) {
      select.setValue(options.get(0));
    } else {
      select.setPlaceholder("No users");
      select.setEnabled(false);
    }
    select.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient()) {
            return;
          }
          String user = event.getValue() == null ? "" : event.getValue().id();
          event.getSource()
              .getUI()
              .ifPresent(
                  ui ->
                      ui.getPage()
                          .executeJs(
                              "fetch('/api/stitch/sso/spoof',{method:'POST',credentials:'same-origin',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','Accept':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify({user:$0})}).finally(() => window.location.reload());",
                              user));
        });
    StitchComponents.withCode(select, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_SSO_SPOOF);
    return select;
  }

  private static List<UserOption> options(StitchSettings settings) {
    List<UserOption> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : settings.sso().spoofUsers()) {
      String id = normalizeUserId(value);
      if (id == null) {
        continue;
      }
      options.add(new UserOption(id, id + " (" + id + ")"));
    }
    String current = normalizeUserId(StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(settings.sso().fallbackSubject()));
    if (current != null) {
      options.add(new UserOption(current, current + " (" + current + ")"));
    }
    return options.stream()
        .distinct()
        .sorted(
            Comparator.<UserOption, String>comparing(
                    value -> value.id() == null ? "" : value.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
                .thenComparing(value -> value.label() == null ? "" : value.label().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)))
        .toList();
  }

  private static UserOption resolveCurrent(List<UserOption> options, StitchSettings settings) {
    String current = normalizeUserId(StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(settings.sso().fallbackSubject()));
    if (current == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (UserOption option : options) {
      if (option != null && current.equals(option.id())) {
        return option;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String displayUser(String subject) {
    String username = normalizeUserId(subject);
    if (username == null) {
      return "Anonymous";
    }
    return username;
  }

  private static String normalizeUserId(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    if (normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("user:")) {
      String id = normalized.substring("user:".length()).trim();
      return id.isEmpty() ? null : id;
    }
    if (normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("service:")) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private record UserOption(String id, String label) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchSummaryStrip.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Shared compact summary row for list/detail and inspector surfaces. */
public final class StitchSummaryStrip extends HorizontalLayout {
  public StitchSummaryStrip() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
    getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    addClassName("stitch-summary-strip");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Summary strip");
  }

  public StitchSummaryStrip setItems(Map<String, String> values) {
    removeAll();
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return this;
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>(values);
    normalized.forEach(
        (label, value) -> {
          String resolvedLabel = Strings.trimToNull(label);
          if (resolvedLabel == null) {
            return;
          }
          Div item = new Div();
          item.addClassName("stitch-summary-item");

          Span labelText = new Span(resolvedLabel);
          labelText.addClassName("stitch-summary-label");
          Span valueText = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "-"));
          valueText.addClassName("stitch-summary-value");

          item.add(labelText, valueText);
          add(item);
        });
    return this;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/component/StitchTabbedDetailsPanel.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.tabs.Tab;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;

/** Shared tabs + detail host composition for structured inspector/detail surfaces. */
public final class StitchTabbedDetailsPanel extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchTabs tabs = new StitchTabs();
  private final Div contentHost = new Div();
  private final LinkedHashMap<String, Tab> tabsByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final LinkedHashMap<String, Component> contentByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private Consumer<String> onTabChanged = key -> {};

  public StitchTabbedDetailsPanel() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.6rem");
    addClassName("stitch-tabbed-details");

    tabs.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Detail tabs");
    tabs.addSelectedChangeListener(event -> renderSelectedAndNotify());

    contentHost.setWidthFull();
    contentHost.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    contentHost.addClassName("stitch-tabbed-details-content");

    add(tabs, contentHost);
  }

  public StitchTabbedDetailsPanel addTab(String key, String label, Component content) {
    String resolvedKey = requireKey(key);
    String resolvedLabel = label == null || label.isBlank() ? resolvedKey : label.trim();
    Tab tab = tabsByKey.get(resolvedKey);
    if (tab == null) {
      tab = new Tab(resolvedLabel);
      tab.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", resolvedLabel + " tab");
      tabsByKey.put(resolvedKey, tab);
      tabs.add(tab);
    } else {
      tab.setLabel(resolvedLabel);
    }
    contentByKey.put(resolvedKey, content == null ? new Div() : content);
    if (tabs.getSelectedTab() == null) {
      tabs.setSelectedTab(tab);
    }
    renderSelected();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTabbedDetailsPanel setTabContent(String key, Component content) {
    String resolvedKey = requireKey(key);
    if (!tabsByKey.containsKey(resolvedKey)) {
      return addTab(resolvedKey, resolvedKey, content);
    }
    contentByKey.put(resolvedKey, content == null ? new Div() : content);
    renderSelected();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTabbedDetailsPanel selectTab(String key) {
    Tab tab = tabsByKey.get(requireKey(key));
    if (tab != null) {
      tabs.setSelectedTab(tab);
      renderSelectedAndNotify();
    }
    return this;
  }

  public String selectedTabKey() {
    Tab selected = (Tab) tabs.getSelectedTab();
    if (selected == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, Tab> entry : tabsByKey.entrySet()) {
      if (entry.getValue() == selected) {
        return entry.getKey();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public boolean isSelected(String key) {
    String selected = selectedTabKey();
    return selected != null && selected.equals(requireKey(key));
  }

  public StitchTabbedDetailsPanel onTabChanged(Consumer<String> callback) {
    onTabChanged = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, key -> {});
    return this;
  }

  private void renderSelectedAndNotify() {
    renderSelected();
    onTabChanged.accept(selectedTabKey());
  }

  private void renderSelected() {
    contentHost.removeAll();
    String selected = selectedTabKey();
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    Component content = contentByKey.get(selected);
    if (content != null) {
      contentHost.add(content);
    }
  }

  private static String requireKey(String key) {
    String resolved = key == null ? "" : key.trim();
    if (resolved.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("tab key is required");
    }
    return resolved;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;

/** Shared queue/list + detail shell for workflow review screens. */
public final class StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final SplitLayout split = new SplitLayout();
  private final StitchResultsView<T> queue = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final VerticalLayout right = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchSectionHeader leftHeader = new StitchSectionHeader("Queue");
  private final StitchSectionHeader rightHeader = new StitchSectionHeader("Details");
  private final HorizontalLayout detailActions = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final Div detailHost = new Div();
  private final StitchEmptyState noSelection =
      new StitchEmptyState("No submission selected", "Select a queue item to inspect details.");

  private Consumer<T> selectionListener = value -> {};

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel(String queueTitle, String detailTitle) {
    setWidthFull();
    setHeight(null);
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");

    split.setWidthFull();
    split.setHeight(null);
    split.setSplitterPosition(44);
    split.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Workflow queue and detail layout");
    split.addClassName("stitch-workflow-queue-split");

    VerticalLayout left = new VerticalLayout();
    left.setWidthFull();
    left.setHeight(null);
    left.setPadding(false);
    left.setSpacing(false);
    left.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    left.addClassName("stitch-workflow-queue-pane");
    leftHeader.withTitle(queueTitle == null ? "Queue" : queueTitle.trim());
    leftHeader.addClassName("stitch-workflow-queue-header");
    this.queue.setWidthFull();
    this.queue.setHeight(null);
    this.queue.toolbar().setVisible(false);
    this.queue.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    this.queue.setPageSizeOptions(10, 25, 50, 100);
    this.queue.setPageSize(10);
    this.queue.setResultCountVisible(false);
    this.queue.emptyState().setTitle("Queue is empty");
    this.queue.emptyState().setMessage("No pending workflow submissions were found.");
    this.queue.grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Workflow queue");
    this.queue.addClassName("stitch-workflow-queue-results");
    left.add(leftHeader, this.queue);

    right.setWidthFull();
    right.setHeight(null);
    right.setPadding(false);
    right.setSpacing(false);
    right.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    right.addClassName("stitch-workflow-detail-pane");
    rightHeader.withTitle(detailTitle == null ? "Details" : detailTitle.trim());
    detailActions.setPadding(false);
    detailActions.setSpacing(true);
    detailActions.addClassName("stitch-workflow-detail-actions");
    rightHeader.withRight(detailActions);

    detailHost.setWidthFull();
    detailHost.setHeight(null);
    detailHost.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    detailHost.addClassName("stitch-workflow-detail-host");
    detailHost.getElement().setAttribute("role", "region");
    detailHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Selected workflow submission details");
    right.add(rightHeader, detailHost);
    setDetailContent(noSelection);

    split.addToPrimary(left);
    split.addToSecondary(right);
    add(split);

    queue.grid()
        .asSingleSelect()
        .addValueChangeListener(event -> selectionListener.accept(event.getValue()));
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> onSelectionChange(Consumer<T> listener) {
    this.selectionListener = listener == null ? value -> {} : listener;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> setItems(Collection<? extends T> items) {
    queue.setItems(items == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(items));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> setQueueEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    queue.emptyState().setTitle(Objects.requireNonNullElse(title, ""));
    queue.emptyState().setMessage(Objects.requireNonNullElse(message, ""));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> setQueueTitle(String value) {
    leftHeader.withTitle(Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, ""));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> setDetailTitle(String value) {
    rightHeader.withTitle(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> setDetailContent(Component content) {
    detailHost.removeAll();
    detailHost.add(content == null ? noSelection : content);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> setDetailActions(Component... actions) {
    detailActions.removeAll();
    if (actions != null) {
      for (Component action : actions) {
        if (action != null) {
          detailActions.add(action);
        }
      }
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchWorkflowQueuePanel<T> clearSelection() {
    queue.grid().deselectAll();
    return this;
  }

  public T selectedItem() {
    return queue.grid().asSingleSelect().getValue();
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> queueView() {
    return queue;
  }

  public StitchGrid<T> queueGrid() {
    return queue.grid();
  }

  public SplitLayout split() {
    return split;
  }

  public HorizontalLayout detailActions() {
    return detailActions;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/controller/StitchDocsResourceController.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.controller;

import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import java.net.URLDecoder;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.docs.StitchDocsBrowserProvider;
import org.springframework.http.CacheControl;
import org.springframework.http.MediaType;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
import org.springframework.web.server.ResponseStatusException;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/stitch/docs")
public class StitchDocsResourceController {

  private static final String RESOURCE_PREFIX = "/api/stitch/docs/resources/";

  private final StitchDocsBrowserProvider provider;

  public StitchDocsResourceController(StitchDocsBrowserProvider provider) {
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
  }

  @GetMapping("/resources/**")
  public ResponseEntity<byte[]> resource(HttpServletRequest request) {
    String path = extractResourcePath(request);
    StitchDocsBrowserProvider.DocResource resource = provider.loadResource(path);
    if (resource == null || resource.bytes() == null) {
      throw new ResponseStatusException(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND, "Docs resource not found");
    }
    MediaType mediaType = parseMediaType(resource.contentType());
    return ResponseEntity.ok()
        .cacheControl(CacheControl.noCache())
        .contentType(mediaType)
        .body(resource.bytes());
  }

  private static String extractResourcePath(HttpServletRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      throw new ResponseStatusException(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND, "Docs resource not found");
    }
    String contextPath = Strings.trimToEmpty(request.getContextPath());
    String uri = Strings.trimToEmpty(request.getRequestURI());
    String prefix = contextPath + RESOURCE_PREFIX;
    if (!uri.startsWith(prefix)) {
      throw new ResponseStatusException(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND, "Docs resource not found");
    }
    String relativePath = uri.substring(prefix.length());
    String decoded = URLDecoder.decode(relativePath, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    if (Strings.isBlank(decoded)) {
      throw new ResponseStatusException(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND, "Docs resource not found");
    }
    return decoded;
  }

  private static MediaType parseMediaType(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return MediaType.APPLICATION_OCTET_STREAM;
    }
    try {
      return MediaType.parseMediaType(normalized);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return MediaType.APPLICATION_OCTET_STREAM;
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/controller/StitchSsoController.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.controller;

import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchSettings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.ServletSsoRequestAdapter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.ServletSsoResponseAdapter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchSsoFilter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchSsoUsers;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PostMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestBody;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
import org.springframework.web.server.ResponseStatusException;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/stitch/sso")
public class StitchSsoController {

  private final SsoService ssoService;
  private final SsoConfig ssoConfig;
  private final StitchSsoUsers users;
  private final StitchSettings settings;

  public StitchSsoController(
      SsoService ssoService, SsoConfig ssoConfig, StitchSsoUsers users, StitchSettings settings) {
    this.ssoService = Objects.requireNonNull(ssoService, "ssoService");
    this.ssoConfig = Objects.requireNonNull(ssoConfig, "ssoConfig");
    this.users = Objects.requireNonNull(users, "users");
    this.settings = Objects.requireNonNull(settings, "settings");
  }

  @GetMapping("/whoami")
  public Map<String, Object> whoami(HttpServletRequest request) {
    SsoContext context = resolveContext(request);
    return withFallbackSubject(ssoService.buildCurrentUserPayload(context));
  }

  @GetMapping("/users")
  public List<String> users() {
    ensureSpoofEnabled();
    return users.listUsers();
  }

  @PostMapping("/spoof")
  public Map<String, Object> spoof(
      @RequestBody(required = false) SpoofRequest body,
      HttpServletRequest request,
      HttpServletResponse response) {
    ensureSpoofEnabled();
    String requestedUser = body == null ? null : body.user();
    FabricSsoRequest ssoRequest =
        new ServletSsoRequestAdapter(request, ssoConfig.forwardedHeadersEnabled());
    ServletSsoResponseAdapter ssoResponse = new ServletSsoResponseAdapter(response);
    SsoResult result = ssoService.handleSpoof(ssoRequest, ssoResponse, requestedUser);
    if (response.getStatus() >= 400) {
      throw new ResponseStatusException(HttpStatus.valueOf(response.getStatus()), "Spoof update failed");
    }
    if (result != null && result.context() != null && result.context().authenticated()) {
      return withFallbackSubject(ssoService.buildCurrentUserPayload(result.context()));
    }
    return withFallbackSubject(ssoService.buildCurrentUserPayload(fallbackContext()));
  }

  @GetMapping("/login")
  public void login(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) {
    FabricSsoRequest ssoRequest =
        new ServletSsoRequestAdapter(request, ssoConfig.forwardedHeadersEnabled());
    ssoService.handleLogin(ssoRequest, new ServletSsoResponseAdapter(response));
  }

  @GetMapping("/callback")
  public void callback(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) {
    FabricSsoRequest ssoRequest =
        new ServletSsoRequestAdapter(request, ssoConfig.forwardedHeadersEnabled());
    ssoService.handleCallback(ssoRequest, new ServletSsoResponseAdapter(response));
  }

  private void ensureSpoofEnabled() {
    if (!ssoConfig.spoofEnabled()) {
      throw new ResponseStatusException(HttpStatus.FORBIDDEN, "Spoof mode disabled");
    }
  }

  private SsoContext resolveContext(HttpServletRequest request) {
    Object fromRequest = request == null ? null : request.getAttribute(StitchSsoFilter.ATTR_CONTEXT);
    if (fromRequest instanceof SsoContext context) {
      return context;
    }
    return SsoContext.current().orElseGet(this::fallbackContext);
  }

  private SsoContext fallbackContext() {
    String fallback = Strings.trimToNull(settings.sso().fallbackSubject());
    if (fallback == null) {
      fallback = "service:stitch";
    }
    return new SsoContext(null, ssoService.mode(), false, fallback, null);
  }

  private Map<String, Object> withFallbackSubject(Map<String, Object> payload) {
    Map<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (payload != null && !payload.isEmpty()) {
      values.putAll(payload);
    }
    Object subject = values.get("subject");
    if (!(subject instanceof String text) || text.isBlank()) {
      values.put("subject", settings.sso().fallbackSubject());
    }
    if (!values.containsKey("mode")) {
      values.put("mode", ssoService.mode().name());
    }
    return Collections.unmodifiableMap(values);
  }

  private record SpoofRequest(String user) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

@FunctionalInterface
public interface StitchDashboardActionHandler {
  StitchDashboardActionResult execute(StitchDashboardActionRequest request) throws Exception;
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardActionRequest.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public record StitchDashboardActionRequest(
    StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
    StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard,
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget,
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action action,
    Map<String, String> payload,
    Map<String, String> sharedFilters,
    Map<String, String> linkedFilters,
    Map<String, String> parameters) {

  public StitchDashboardActionRequest {
    runtimeContext = runtimeContext;
    dashboard = dashboard;
    widget = widget;
    action = action;
    payload = normalize(payload);
    sharedFilters = normalize(sharedFilters);
    linkedFilters = normalize(linkedFilters);
    parameters = normalize(parameters);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> normalize(Map<String, String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      if (key != null && value != null) {
        normalized.put(key, value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardActionResult.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record StitchDashboardActionResult(
    boolean success, String message, String detail, boolean refreshRequested) {

  public static StitchDashboardActionResult success(String message) {
    return new StitchDashboardActionResult(true, Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), "Action completed."), null, true);
  }

  public static StitchDashboardActionResult success(String message, boolean refreshRequested) {
    return new StitchDashboardActionResult(
        true, Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), "Action completed."), null, refreshRequested);
  }

  public static StitchDashboardActionResult failure(String message) {
    return new StitchDashboardActionResult(false, Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), "Action failed."), null, false);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardActions.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Action registry/executor for interactive dashboard actions. */
public final class StitchDashboardActions {
  private final Map<String, StitchDashboardActionHandler> byTarget;
  private final Map<StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType, StitchDashboardActionHandler> byType;
  private final StitchDashboardActionHandler defaultHandler;

  private StitchDashboardActions(Builder builder) {
    this.byTarget = Map.copyOf(builder.byTarget);
    this.byType = Map.copyOf(builder.byType);
    this.defaultHandler = builder.defaultHandler;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public StitchDashboardActionResult execute(StitchDashboardActionRequest request) {
    if (request == null || request.action() == null) {
      return StitchDashboardActionResult.failure("No dashboard action defined.");
    }
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action action = request.action();
    StitchDashboardActionHandler handler = byTarget.get(normalizeKey(action.target()));
    if (handler == null) {
      handler = byType.get(action.type());
    }
    if (handler == null) {
      handler = defaultHandler;
    }
    if (handler == null) {
      return StitchDashboardActionResult.failure("No handler registered for action " + action.id());
    }
    try {
      StitchDashboardActionResult result = handler.execute(request);
      return result == null ? StitchDashboardActionResult.success("Action completed.") : result;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      String message = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Action failed.");
      return new StitchDashboardActionResult(false, message, error.getClass().getSimpleName(), false);
    }
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final LinkedHashMap<String, StitchDashboardActionHandler> byTarget = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    private final LinkedHashMap<StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType, StitchDashboardActionHandler> byType =
        new LinkedHashMap<>();
    private StitchDashboardActionHandler defaultHandler =
        request -> StitchDashboardActionResult.failure("No handler for action target/type.");

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder registerTarget(String target, StitchDashboardActionHandler handler) {
      String key = normalizeKey(target);
      if (key != null && handler != null) {
        byTarget.put(key, handler);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder registerType(
        StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType type, StitchDashboardActionHandler handler) {
      if (type != null && handler != null) {
        byType.put(type, handler);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDefaultHandler(StitchDashboardActionHandler handler) {
      this.defaultHandler = Objects.requireNonNull(handler, "handler");
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDashboardActions build() {
      return new StitchDashboardActions(this);
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardAuthoringBrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;

import java.util.Objects;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDashboard;

import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

/** Productized dashboard browser with create/open/edit actions. */
public class StitchDashboardAuthoringBrowserScreen extends StitchPage {
  private static final String FILTER_ALL = "__all__";
  private static final String SCOPE_ALL = "all";
  private static final String SCOPE_PUBLIC_SHARED = "public_shared";
  private static final String SCOPE_GROUP = "group";
  private static final String SCOPE_MY = "my";

  private final StitchDashboardDefinitionStore store;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchResultsView<DefinitionDashboard> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final Select<String> groupFilter = new Select<>();
  private final Select<String> scopeFilter = new Select<>();
  private final TextField searchField = new TextField();
  private final Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH");
  private final Button createAction = new Button("CREATE");

  private List<DefinitionDashboard> dashboards = List.of();
  private Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> openHandler;
  private Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> editHandler;
  private Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> createdHandler;

  public StitchDashboardAuthoringBrowserScreen(StitchDashboardDefinitionStore store) {
    super("Dashboards", "Browse, create, and edit discovery-backed dashboards.");
    this.store = Objects.requireNonNull(store, "store");

    addClassName("stitch-dashboard-authoring-browser");
    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    body().getStyle().set("gap", "0.7rem");

    configureFilters();
    configureResults();
    reload();

    addToBody(filtersBar, results);
  }

  public StitchDashboardAuthoringBrowserScreen onOpen(Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> handler) {
    this.openHandler = handler;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDashboardAuthoringBrowserScreen onEdit(Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> handler) {
    this.editHandler = handler;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDashboardAuthoringBrowserScreen onCreated(Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> handler) {
    this.createdHandler = handler;
    return this;
  }

  public void reload() {
    dashboards = store.list();
    refreshGroupOptions();
    applyFilters();
  }

  private void configureFilters() {
    groupFilter.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-browser-group");
    groupFilter.setWidth("12rem");
    groupFilter.setItemLabelGenerator(value -> FILTER_ALL.equals(value) ? "All Groups" : value);
    groupFilter.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          String selected = Strings.trimToNull(groupFilter.getValue());
          if (selected != null && !FILTER_ALL.equals(selected)) {
            StitchGroupSelectionContext.remember(selected);
          }
          applyFilters();
        });

    scopeFilter.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-browser-scope");
    scopeFilter.setWidth("13rem");
    scopeFilter.setItems(SCOPE_ALL, SCOPE_PUBLIC_SHARED, SCOPE_GROUP, SCOPE_MY);
    scopeFilter.setValue(SCOPE_ALL);
    scopeFilter.setItemLabelGenerator(
        value ->
            switch (Strings.firstNonBlank(value, SCOPE_ALL)) {
              case SCOPE_PUBLIC_SHARED -> "Public / Shared";
              case SCOPE_GROUP -> "Group Dashboards";
              case SCOPE_MY -> "My Dashboards";
              default -> "All Visibility";
            });
    scopeFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyFilters());

    searchField.setPlaceholder("Search dashboards");
    searchField.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    searchField.setWidth("18rem");
    searchField.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyFilters());

    refreshAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
    refreshAction.addClickListener(event -> reload());

    createAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    createAction.addClickListener(event -> openCreateDialog());

    filtersBar
        .withFilter(groupFilter)
        .withFilter(scopeFilter)
        .withFilter(searchField)
        .withRightAction(createAction)
        .withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  private void configureResults() {
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(10, 25, 50);
    results.setPageSize(10);
    results.setResultCountVisible(false);
    results.setEmptyState("No dashboards found", "Adjust filters or create a new dashboard.");

    results.grid().addColumn(d -> envelopeValue(d, true)).setHeader("GROUP").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    results.grid().addColumn(d -> envelopeValue(d, false)).setHeader("NAME").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    results.grid().addColumn(d -> safe(d == null ? null : d.title())).setHeader("TITLE").setAutoWidth(true);
    results.grid().addColumn(d -> safe(d == null ? null : d.description())).setHeader("DESCRIPTION");
    results.grid().addColumn(d -> safe(d == null ? null : d.category())).setHeader("CATEGORY").setAutoWidth(true);
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(d -> d == null || d.tags() == null ? "" : String.join(", ", d.tags()))
        .setHeader("TAGS");
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(d -> enumName(d == null ? null : d.visibility(), "GROUP"))
        .setHeader("VISIBILITY")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(d -> enumName(d == null ? null : d.executionMode(), "SHARED"))
        .setHeader("EXECUTION")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(d -> enumName(d == null ? null : d.mode(), "STANDARD"))
        .setHeader("MODE")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(this::owner)
        .setHeader("OWNER")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            d -> {
              DefinitionEnvelope envelope = d == null ? null : d.envelope();
              return envelope != null && Boolean.FALSE.equals(envelope.enabled()) ? "NO" : "YES";
            })
        .setHeader("ENABLED")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setFlexGrow(0);

    StitchRowActions<DefinitionDashboard> actions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    actions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.<DefinitionDashboard>icon(VaadinIcon.ARROW_RIGHT, "Open", this::openDashboard));
    actions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.<DefinitionDashboard>icon(VaadinIcon.EDIT, "Edit", this::editDashboard));
    actions.addColumn(results.grid());

    results.grid().addItemDoubleClickListener(event -> openDashboard(event.getItem()));
  }

  private void refreshGroupOptions() {
    String selected = Strings.trimToNull(groupFilter.getValue());
    List<String> options = new ArrayList<>();
    options.add(FILTER_ALL);
    options.addAll(availableGroups());
    groupFilter.setItems(options);

    if (selected != null && options.contains(selected)) {
      groupFilter.setValue(selected);
      return;
    }
    String remembered = Strings.trimToNull(StitchGroupSelectionContext.current());
    if (remembered != null && options.contains(remembered)) {
      groupFilter.setValue(remembered);
      return;
    }
    groupFilter.setValue(FILTER_ALL);
  }

  private List<String> availableGroups() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard dashboard : dashboards) {
      String group = Strings.trimToNull(envelopeValue(dashboard, true));
      if (group != null) {
        groups.add(group);
      }
    }
    return groups.isEmpty() ? List.of("lab") : List.copyOf(groups);
  }

  private void applyFilters() {
    String selectedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(groupFilter.getValue());
    String selectedScope = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(scopeFilter.getValue()), SCOPE_ALL);
    String query = normalize(searchField.getValue());
    String subject = normalizeSubject(StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject());
    String groupContext = resolveGroupContext(selectedGroup);

    ArrayList<DefinitionDashboard> filtered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard dashboard : dashboards) {
      if (dashboard == null || dashboard.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (selectedGroup != null
          && !FILTER_ALL.equals(selectedGroup)
          && !selectedGroup.equalsIgnoreCase(dashboard.envelope().group())) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!isVisibleToCurrentSubject(dashboard, groupContext, subject)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!matchesScope(selectedScope, dashboard, subject)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!query.isEmpty() && !matches(dashboard, query)) {
        continue;
      }
      filtered.add(dashboard);
    }
    results.setItems(filtered);
    results.setEmpty(filtered.isEmpty());
  }

  private void openDashboard(DefinitionDashboard dashboard) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.envelope() == null || openHandler == null) {
      return;
    }
    openHandler.accept(StitchDashboardDefinitionRef.of(dashboard.envelope().group(), dashboard.envelope().name()));
  }

  private void editDashboard(DefinitionDashboard dashboard) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.envelope() == null || editHandler == null) {
      return;
    }
    editHandler.accept(StitchDashboardDefinitionRef.of(dashboard.envelope().group(), dashboard.envelope().name()));
  }

  private void openCreateDialog() {
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Create Dashboard");
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setWidthFull();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("42em", 2));

    TextField group = new TextField("Group");
    group.setRequired(true);
    group.setWidthFull();
    group.setValue(defaultGroup());

    TextField name = new TextField("Name");
    name.setRequired(true);
    name.setWidthFull();

    TextField title = new TextField("Title");
    title.setWidthFull();

    TextArea description = new TextArea("Description");
    description.setWidthFull();
    description.setMinHeight("5.2rem");
    description.getStyle().set("grid-column", "1 / -1");

    TextField category = new TextField("Category");
    category.setWidthFull();
    category.setValue("General");

    TextField tags = new TextField("Tags (comma-separated)");
    tags.setWidthFull();

    Select<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode> mode = new Select<>();
    mode.setLabel("Mode");
    mode.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode.values());
    mode.setValue(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode.STANDARD);
    mode.setWidthFull();

    Select<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility> visibility = new Select<>();
    visibility.setLabel("Visibility");
    visibility.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.values());
    visibility.setValue(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.GROUP);
    visibility.setWidthFull();

    Select<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode> executionMode = new Select<>();
    executionMode.setLabel("Execution");
    executionMode.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.values());
    executionMode.setValue(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED);
    executionMode.setWidthFull();
    visibility.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (event.getValue() == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.USER) {
            executionMode.setValue(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.PER_USER);
          } else if (executionMode.getValue() == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.PER_USER) {
            executionMode.setValue(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED);
          }
        });

    Checkbox enabled = new Checkbox("Enabled", true);
    enabled.setWidthFull();
    enabled.getStyle().set("grid-column", "1 / -1");

    form.add(group, name, title, category, mode, visibility, executionMode, tags, enabled, description);
    dialog.body().add(form);
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "Create",
        () -> {
          String resolvedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group.getValue());
          String resolvedName = Strings.trimToNull(name.getValue());
          String resolvedTitle = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title.getValue()), resolvedName);
          if (resolvedGroup == null || resolvedName == null) {
            toast("Group and Name are required.", false);
            return;
          }
          if (store.exists(resolvedGroup, resolvedName)) {
            toast("Dashboard already exists: " + resolvedGroup + "/" + resolvedName, false);
            return;
          }

          Instant now = Instant.now();
          String actor = Strings.firstNonBlank(StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject(), "service:stitch");
          DefinitionDashboard dashboard =
              new DefinitionDashboard(
                  new DefinitionEnvelope(
                      resolvedGroup,
                      DefinitionType.DASHBOARD,
                      resolvedName,
                      UUID.randomUUID().toString(),
                      enabled.getValue(),
                      "ACTIVE",
                      now.toString(),
                      actor,
                      now.toString(),
                      actor),
                  resolvedTitle,
                  Strings.trimToNull(description.getValue()),
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(category.getValue()), "General"),
                  parseTags(tags.getValue()),
                  mode.getValue(),
                  visibility.getValue(),
                  executionMode.getValue(),
                  new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout(12, "md", List.of()),
                  List.of(),
                  List.of(),
                  new DefinitionDashboard.RefreshPolicy(DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode.MANUAL, null),
                  null);

          store.save(dashboard);
          StitchGroupSelectionContext.remember(resolvedGroup);
          dialog.close();
          reload();
          StitchDashboardDefinitionRef ref = StitchDashboardDefinitionRef.of(resolvedGroup, resolvedName);
          if (createdHandler != null) {
            createdHandler.accept(ref);
          } else if (editHandler != null) {
            editHandler.accept(ref);
          }
          toast("Created dashboard " + resolvedGroup + "/" + resolvedName, true);
        });
    dialog.open();
  }

  private String defaultGroup() {
    String remembered = Strings.trimToNull(StitchGroupSelectionContext.current());
    if (remembered != null) {
      return remembered;
    }
    String selected = Strings.trimToNull(groupFilter.getValue());
    if (selected != null && !FILTER_ALL.equals(selected)) {
      return selected;
    }
    for (DefinitionDashboard dashboard : dashboards) {
      String group = envelopeValue(dashboard, true);
      if (Strings.trimToNull(group) != null) {
        return group;
      }
    }
    return "lab";
  }

  private String resolveGroupContext(String selectedGroup) {
    if (selectedGroup != null && !FILTER_ALL.equals(selectedGroup)) {
      return selectedGroup;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(StitchGroupSelectionContext.current());
  }

  private boolean isVisibleToCurrentSubject(
      DefinitionDashboard dashboard, String groupContext, String normalizedSubject) {
    DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility visibility = visibilityOf(dashboard);
    if (visibility == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.PUBLIC) {
      return true;
    }
    if (visibility == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.GROUP) {
      String dashboardGroup = Strings.trimToNull(envelopeValue(dashboard, true));
      if (Strings.trimToNull(groupContext) == null) {
        return true;
      }
      return dashboardGroup != null && dashboardGroup.equalsIgnoreCase(groupContext);
    }
    String owner = normalizeSubject(owner(dashboard));
    return owner != null && owner.equals(normalizedSubject);
  }

  private boolean matchesScope(
      String selectedScope, DefinitionDashboard dashboard, String normalizedSubject) {
    String scope = Strings.firstNonBlank(selectedScope, SCOPE_ALL);
    DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility visibility = visibilityOf(dashboard);
    DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode execution = executionModeOf(dashboard);
    return switch (scope) {
      case SCOPE_PUBLIC_SHARED ->
          visibility == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.PUBLIC
              || execution == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED;
      case SCOPE_GROUP -> visibility == DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.GROUP;
      case SCOPE_MY -> {
        if (visibility != DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.USER) {
          yield false;
        }
        String owner = normalizeSubject(owner(dashboard));
        yield owner != null && owner.equals(normalizedSubject);
      }
      default -> true;
    };
  }

  private static DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility visibilityOf(DefinitionDashboard dashboard) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.visibility() == null) {
      return DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.GROUP;
    }
    return dashboard.visibility();
  }

  private static DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode executionModeOf(DefinitionDashboard dashboard) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.executionMode() == null) {
      return DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED;
    }
    return dashboard.executionMode();
  }

  private String owner(DefinitionDashboard dashboard) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = dashboard == null ? null : dashboard.envelope();
    if (envelope == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(
        Strings.trimToNull(envelope.updatedBy()),
        Strings.trimToNull(envelope.createdBy()),
        "");
  }

  private static String normalizeSubject(String subject) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static boolean matches(DefinitionDashboard dashboard, String query) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.envelope() == null || Strings.isBlank(query)) {
      return true;
    }
    String text =
        (safe(dashboard.envelope().group())
                + " "
                + safe(dashboard.envelope().name())
                + " "
                + safe(dashboard.title())
                + " "
                + safe(dashboard.description())
                + " "
                + safe(dashboard.category())
                + " "
                + safe(enumName(dashboard.visibility(), "GROUP"))
                + " "
                + safe(enumName(dashboard.executionMode(), "SHARED"))
                + " "
                + String.join(" ", dashboard.tags() == null ? List.of() : dashboard.tags()))
            .toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return text.contains(query);
  }

  private static List<String> parseTags(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> tags = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String token : normalized.split(",")) {
      String item = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (item != null) {
        tags.add(item);
      }
    }
    return tags.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(tags);
  }

  private static String envelopeValue(DefinitionDashboard dashboard, boolean group) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.envelope() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return safe(group ? dashboard.envelope().group() : dashboard.envelope().name());
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToEmpty(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String enumName(Enum<?> value, String fallback) {
    return value == null ? fallback : value.name();
  }

  private static String safe(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }

  private static void toast(String message, boolean success) {
    String text = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), success ? "Saved." : "Action failed.");
    Notification notification = Notification.show(text, 2800, Notification.Position.BOTTOM_END);
    notification.addThemeVariants(success ? NotificationVariant.LUMO_SUCCESS : NotificationVariant.LUMO_ERROR);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardBrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

/** Dashboard landing/browser screen using registry metadata. */
public class StitchDashboardBrowserScreen extends StitchPage {
  private static final String FILTER_ALL = "__all__";

  private final StitchDashboardRegistry registry;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchResultsView<StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final Select<String> categoryFilter = new Select<>();
  private final TextField searchFilter = new TextField();
  private final Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH");
  private Consumer<StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry> openHandler;
