  public StitchDashboardBrowserScreen(StitchDashboardRegistry registry) {
    super("Dashboards", "Browse and open available operational dashboards.");
    this.registry = registry == null ? StitchDashboardRegistry.builder().build() : registry;

    addClassName("stitch-dashboard-browser");
    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    body().getStyle().set("gap", "0.7rem");

    configureFilters();
    configureResults();
    applyFilters();

    addToBody(filtersBar, results);
  }

  public StitchDashboardBrowserScreen onOpen(Consumer<StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry> handler) {
    this.openHandler = handler;
    return this;
  }

  private void configureFilters() {
    List<String> categories = collectCategories();
    List<String> options = new ArrayList<>();
    options.add(FILTER_ALL);
    options.addAll(categories);

    categoryFilter.setItems(options);
    categoryFilter.setItemLabelGenerator(value -> FILTER_ALL.equals(value) ? "All Categories" : value);
    categoryFilter.setValue(FILTER_ALL);
    categoryFilter.setWidth("14rem");
    categoryFilter.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-browser-category");
    categoryFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyFilters());

    searchFilter.setPlaceholder("Search dashboards");
    searchFilter.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    searchFilter.setWidth("18rem");
    searchFilter.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-browser-search");
    searchFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyFilters());

    refreshAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
    refreshAction.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-browser-refresh");
    refreshAction.addClickListener(event -> applyFilters());

    filtersBar.withFilter(categoryFilter);
    filtersBar.withFilter(searchFilter);
    filtersBar.withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  private void configureResults() {
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setResultCountVisible(false);
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(10, 25, 50);
    results.setPageSize(10);
    results.setEmptyState("No dashboards found", "Adjust search or category filters.");

    results.grid().addColumn(entry -> safe(entry == null ? null : entry.category())).setHeader("CATEGORY");
    results.grid().addColumn(entry -> safe(entry == null ? null : entry.title())).setHeader("TITLE");
    results.grid().addColumn(entry -> safe(entry == null ? null : entry.description())).setHeader("DESCRIPTION");
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(entry -> entry == null || entry.tags().isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(", ", entry.tags()))
        .setHeader("TAGS");
    results
        .grid()
        .addColumn(entry -> entry == null || entry.sourceType() == null ? "" : entry.sourceType().name())
        .setHeader("SOURCE");

    StitchRowActions<StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.<StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry>icon(
            VaadinIcon.ARROW_RIGHT, "Open", this::openDashboard));
    rowActions.addColumn(results.grid());

    results.grid().addItemClickListener(event -> openDashboard(event.getItem()));
  }

  private void applyFilters() {
    String category = Strings.trimToNull(categoryFilter.getValue());
    String query = normalize(searchFilter.getValue());
    List<StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry> filtered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry entry : registry.entries()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (category != null && !FILTER_ALL.equals(category) && !category.equalsIgnoreCase(entry.category())) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!query.isEmpty() && !matches(entry, query)) {
        continue;
      }
      filtered.add(entry);
    }
    results.setItems(filtered);
    results.setEmpty(filtered.isEmpty());
  }

  private void openDashboard(StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry entry) {
    if (entry == null || openHandler == null) {
      return;
    }
    openHandler.accept(entry);
  }

  private List<String> collectCategories() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry entry : registry.entries()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String category = Strings.trimToNull(entry.category());
      if (category != null) {
        values.add(category);
      }
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? List.of("General") : List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static boolean matches(StitchDashboardRegistry.Entry entry, String query) {
    if (entry == null || Strings.isBlank(query)) {
      return true;
    }
    String text =
        (safe(entry.id())
                + " "
                + safe(entry.title())
                + " "
                + safe(entry.description())
                + " "
                + safe(entry.category())
                + " "
                + String.join(" ", entry.tags()))
            .toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return text.contains(query);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToEmpty(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String safe(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardCatalog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Immutable dashboard descriptor catalog. */
public final class StitchDashboardCatalog {
  private final Map<String, StitchDashboardDescriptor> byId;
  private final List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> dashboards;

  private StitchDashboardCatalog(List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> descriptors) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchDashboardDescriptor> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (descriptors != null) {
      for (StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor : descriptors) {
        if (descriptor == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String id = normalizeKey(descriptor.id());
        if (id != null && !indexed.containsKey(id)) {
          indexed.put(id, descriptor);
        }
      }
    }
    this.byId = Map.copyOf(indexed);
    this.dashboards = List.copyOf(indexed.values());
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static StitchDashboardCatalog of(List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> descriptors) {
    return new StitchDashboardCatalog(descriptors);
  }

  public List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> dashboards() {
    return dashboards;
  }

  public StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard(String id) {
    String normalized = normalizeKey(id);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return byId.get(normalized);
  }

  public boolean isEmpty() {
    return dashboards.isEmpty();
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> descriptors = new ArrayList<>();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder add(StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor) {
      if (descriptor != null) {
        descriptors.add(descriptor);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addAll(List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> values) {
      if (values != null) {
        for (StitchDashboardDescriptor value : values) {
          add(value);
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder loadFromClasspath(String resourcePath, Class<?> anchor) {
      return addAll(StitchDashboardDescriptorLoader.loadFromClasspath(resourcePath, anchor));
    }

    public StitchDashboardCatalog build() {
      return StitchDashboardCatalog.of(descriptors);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDataRequest.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record StitchDashboardDataRequest(
    StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard,
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget,
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source,
    Map<String, String> parameters,
    Map<String, String> sharedFilters,
    Map<String, String> linkedFilters) {

  public StitchDashboardDataRequest {
    dashboard = dashboard;
    widget = widget;
    source = source;
    parameters = normalize(parameters);
    sharedFilters = normalize(sharedFilters);
    linkedFilters = normalize(linkedFilters);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> normalize(Map<String, String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      if (key != null && value != null) {
        normalized.put(key, value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDataSource.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

@FunctionalInterface
public interface StitchDashboardDataSource {
  List<Map<String, Object>> fetch(StitchDashboardDataRequest request) throws Exception;
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDataSources.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.LocalTime;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.time.format.DateTimeParseException;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Source registry and default filtering behavior for descriptor-driven dashboard widgets. */
public final class StitchDashboardDataSources {
  private final Map<String, StitchDashboardDataSource> byId;
  private final Map<String, StitchDashboardDataSource> byResourceId;
  private final Map<StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType, StitchDashboardDataSource> byType;

  private StitchDashboardDataSources(Builder builder) {
    this.byId = Map.copyOf(builder.byId);
    this.byResourceId = Map.copyOf(builder.byResourceId);
    this.byType = Map.copyOf(builder.byType);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public List<Map<String, Object>> query(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget,
      Map<String, String> sharedFilters,
      Map<String, String> linkedFilters) {
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source =
        dashboard == null || widget == null ? null : dashboard.source(widget.sourceId());
    if (source == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    if (source.type() == StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STREAM) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dashboard.widget["
              + (widget == null ? "<unknown>" : widget.id())
              + "] stream source must be handled by live stream runtime, not snapshot query");
    }
    Map<String, String> parameters = resolveParameters(dashboard, widget, source, sharedFilters, linkedFilters);
    StitchDashboardDataRequest request =
        new StitchDashboardDataRequest(dashboard, widget, source, parameters, sharedFilters, linkedFilters);
    return fetchRawRows(request);
  }

  private List<Map<String, Object>> fetchRawRows(StitchDashboardDataRequest request) {
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source = request.source();
    if (source == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    if (source.staticRows() != null && !source.staticRows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.copyOf(source.staticRows());
    }
    StitchDashboardDataSource bySourceId = byId.get(normalizeKey(source.id()));
    if (bySourceId != null) {
      return safeFetch(bySourceId, request);
    }
    StitchDashboardDataSource byResource = byResourceId.get(normalizeKey(source.resourceId()));
    if (byResource != null) {
      return safeFetch(byResource, request);
    }
    StitchDashboardDataSource bySourceType = byType.get(source.type());
    if (bySourceType != null) {
      return safeFetch(bySourceType, request);
    }
    return List.of();
  }

  private static List<Map<String, Object>> safeFetch(
      StitchDashboardDataSource source, StitchDashboardDataRequest request) {
    try {
      List<Map<String, Object>> rows = source.fetch(request);
      if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      return List.copyOf(rows);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to load dashboard source: "
              + (request.source() == null ? "<unknown>" : request.source().id()),
          error);
    }
  }

  public static Map<String, String> resolveParameters(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source,
      Map<String, String> sharedFilters,
      Map<String, String> linkedFilters) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> parameters = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (source != null && source.parameters() != null) {
      parameters.putAll(source.parameters());
    }
    int appliedBindingCount = 0;
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalizedSharedFilters = normalizeMap(sharedFilters);
    Map<String, String> dashboardFilterIds = dashboardFilterIds(dashboard);
    if (widget != null && widget.filterBindings() != null) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> binding : widget.filterBindings().entrySet()) {
        if (binding == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String filterKey = requireNonBlank(binding.getKey(), "widget.filterBindings.filterId");
        String parameterKey = Strings.trimToNull(binding.getValue());
        if (parameterKey == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] filter binding '" + filterKey + "' is missing parameter mapping");
        }
        if (!dashboardFilterIds.isEmpty() && !dashboardFilterIds.containsKey(normalizeKey(filterKey))) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] references unknown dashboard filter '" + filterKey + "'");
        }
        String filterValue = normalizedSharedFilters.get(normalizeKey(filterKey));
        if (filterValue != null) {
          parameters.put(parameterKey, filterValue);
          appliedBindingCount++;
        }
      }
    }
    int linkedParameterCount = 0;
    if (linkedFilters != null && !linkedFilters.isEmpty()) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : linkedFilters.entrySet()) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
        if (key != null && value != null) {
          parameters.put(key, value);
          linkedParameterCount++;
        }
      }
    }
    Map<String, String> resolved = parameters.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(parameters);
    validateSourceParameterization(source, widget, appliedBindingCount, linkedParameterCount, resolved);
    return resolved;
  }

  private static void validateSourceParameterization(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget,
      int appliedBindingCount,
      int linkedParameterCount,
      Map<String, String> parameters) {
    if (source == null || source.type() == null) {
      return;
    }
    String widgetId = widget == null ? "<unknown>" : Strings.firstNonBlank(widget.id(), "<unknown>");
    switch (source.type()) {
      case STATIC -> {
        if (appliedBindingCount > 0 || linkedParameterCount > 0) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "dashboard.widget[" + widgetId + "] cannot apply filters/links to " + source.type() + " source");
        }
      }
      case STREAM -> {
        if (appliedBindingCount > 0) {
          LoggerHolder.LOGGER.warn(
              "[StitchDashboard] widget={} stream source ignores {} shared filter bindings (server-side filtering not supported)",
              widgetId,
              appliedBindingCount);
        }
      }
      case SERVICE_QUERY -> {
        String query = Strings.trimToNull(parameters == null ? null : parameters.get("query"));
        if (query == null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "dashboard.widget[" + widgetId + "] service source requires explicit query parameter");
        }
      }
      case DATASET_QUERY, MATERIALIZED_VIEW -> {
        // No additional constraints here.
      }
    }
  }

  private static Map<String, String> dashboardFilterIds(StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard) {
    if (dashboard == null || dashboard.sharedFilters() == null || dashboard.sharedFilters().isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> filterIds = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter filter : dashboard.sharedFilters()) {
      if (filter == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String filterId = Strings.trimToNull(filter.id());
      if (filterId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      filterIds.put(normalizeKey(filterId), filterId);
    }
    return filterIds.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(filterIds);
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalizeMap(Map<String, String> values) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return normalized;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      if (key == null || value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.put(normalizeKey(key), value);
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String requireNonBlank(String value, String name) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(name + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static final class LoggerHolder {
    private static final org.slf4j.Logger LOGGER =
        org.slf4j.LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchDashboardDataSources.class);
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final LinkedHashMap<String, StitchDashboardDataSource> byId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    private final LinkedHashMap<String, StitchDashboardDataSource> byResourceId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    private final LinkedHashMap<StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType, StitchDashboardDataSource> byType =
        new LinkedHashMap<>();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder register(String sourceId, StitchDashboardDataSource source) {
      String key = normalizeKey(sourceId);
      if (key != null && source != null) {
        byId.put(key, source);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder registerResource(String resourceId, StitchDashboardDataSource source) {
      String key = normalizeKey(resourceId);
      if (key != null && source != null) {
        byResourceId.put(key, source);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder register(StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType type, StitchDashboardDataSource source) {
      if (type != null && source != null) {
        byType.put(type, source);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder registerDefaultIdentitySources() {
      StitchDashboardDataSource identity =
          request -> request.source() == null ? List.of() : request.source().staticRows();
      register(StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STATIC, identity);
      register(StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.DATASET_QUERY, identity);
      register(StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.MATERIALIZED_VIEW, identity);
      register(StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.SERVICE_QUERY, identity);
      register(StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STREAM, identity);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDashboardDataSources build() {
      Objects.requireNonNull(byId, "byId");
      Objects.requireNonNull(byResourceId, "byResourceId");
      Objects.requireNonNull(byType, "byType");
      return new StitchDashboardDataSources(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDefinitionRef.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Canonical group/name identifier for DefinitionDashboard records. */
public record StitchDashboardDefinitionRef(String group, String name) {
  public StitchDashboardDefinitionRef {
    group = require(group, "group");
    name = require(name, "name");
  }

  public String key() {
    return normalize(group) + "/" + normalize(name);
  }

  public static StitchDashboardDefinitionRef of(String group, String name) {
    return new StitchDashboardDefinitionRef(group, name);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard." + field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDefinitionStore.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDashboard;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Discovery-backed CRUD access for DefinitionDashboard records. */
public final class StitchDashboardDefinitionStore {
  private static final Comparator<DefinitionDashboard> DASHBOARD_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing(
              StitchDashboardDefinitionStore::definitionGroup,
              String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
          .thenComparing(
              StitchDashboardDefinitionStore::definitionName,
              String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;

  public StitchDashboardDefinitionStore(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
  }

  public List<DefinitionDashboard> list() {
    ArrayList<DefinitionDashboard> dashboards = new ArrayList<>(discoveryCache().list(DefinitionDashboard.class));
    dashboards.sort(DASHBOARD_ORDER);
    return dashboards.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(dashboards);
  }

  public List<DefinitionDashboard> list(String group) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    if (normalizedGroup == null) {
      return list();
    }
    ArrayList<DefinitionDashboard> dashboards =
        new ArrayList<>(discoveryCache().list(DefinitionDashboard.class, normalizedGroup));
    dashboards.sort(DASHBOARD_ORDER);
    return dashboards.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(dashboards);
  }

  public Optional<DefinitionDashboard> get(String group, String name) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedName == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return discoveryCache().get(DefinitionDashboard.class, normalizedGroup, normalizedName);
  }

  public boolean exists(String group, String name) {
    return get(group, name).isPresent();
  }

  public void save(DefinitionDashboard definition) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    if (definition.envelope() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard envelope is required");
    }
    if (definition.envelope().type() != DefinitionType.DASHBOARD) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard envelope.type must be DASHBOARD");
    }
    discoveryCache().upsert(definition);
  }

  public void delete(String group, String name) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard group/name are required");
    }
    discoveryCache().delete(DefinitionType.DASHBOARD, normalizedGroup, normalizedName);
  }

  private DiscoveryCache discoveryCache() {
    Fabric.Session session = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(session instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    DiscoveryCache cache = resolved.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private static String definitionGroup(DefinitionDashboard definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(definition.envelope().group());
    return value == null ? "" : value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String definitionName(DefinitionDashboard definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(definition.envelope().name());
    return value == null ? "" : value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDefinitionSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDashboard;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/**
 * Bridges discovery DefinitionDashboard records into Stitch dashboard runtime descriptors.
 */
public final class StitchDashboardDefinitionSupport {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchDashboardDefinitionSupport.class);

  private StitchDashboardDefinitionSupport() {}

  public static StitchDashboardCatalog loadCatalog(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    return loadCatalog(runtimeContext, null);
  }

  public static StitchDashboardCatalog loadCatalog(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, String group) {
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache(runtimeContext);
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    List<DefinitionDashboard> definitions =
        normalizedGroup == null
            ? safe(cache.list(DefinitionDashboard.class))
            : safe(cache.list(DefinitionDashboard.class, normalizedGroup));
    if (definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return StitchDashboardCatalog.of(List.of());
    }

    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> descriptors = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard definition : definitions) {
      if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (Boolean.FALSE.equals(definition.envelope().enabled())) {
        continue;
      }
      try {
        descriptors.add(toDescriptor(definition));
      } catch (RuntimeException error) {
        LOGGER.warn(
            "[StitchDashboard][Definition] skipping invalid dashboard group={} name={} message={}",
            definition.envelope().group(),
            definition.envelope().name(),
            error.getMessage());
      }
    }
    return StitchDashboardCatalog.of(descriptors);
  }

  public static StitchDashboardRegistry loadRegistry(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    return loadRegistry(runtimeContext, null);
  }

  public static StitchDashboardRegistry loadRegistry(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, String group) {
    StitchDashboardCatalog catalog = loadCatalog(runtimeContext, group);
    return StitchDashboardRegistry.builder()
        .registerCatalog(catalog, StitchDashboardRegistry.SourceType.CONFIG)
        .build();
  }

  public static StitchDashboardDescriptor toDescriptor(DefinitionDashboard definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("DefinitionDashboard envelope is required");
    }
    Map<String, DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> filtersById = indexFilters(definition.filters());
    Conversion conversion = convertWidgets(definition.widgets(), filtersById);

    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor(
        definition.envelope().name(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(definition.title()), definition.envelope().name()),
        null,
        Strings.trimToNull(definition.description()),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(definition.category()), "General"),
        definition.tags(),
        convertFilters(definition.filters()),
        conversion.sources(),
        conversion.widgets(),
        convertLayoutRows(definition.layout(), conversion.widgets()),
        conversion.links(),
        convertRefreshPolicy(definition.refreshPolicy()),
        mapDashboardMode(definition.mode()),
        mapDashboardVisibility(definition.visibility()),
        mapDashboardExecutionMode(definition.executionMode()),
        convertSemantic(definition.semantic()),
        convertLayout(definition.layout()));
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter> convertFilters(
      List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> filters) {
    if (filters == null || filters.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter> converted = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter filter : filters) {
      if (filter == null || Strings.trimToNull(filter.id()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      boolean groupFilter = isGroupFilter(filter);
      List<String> options = filterOptions(filter.options());
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType type =
          mapFilterType(filter.type(), groupFilter);
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType filterSourceType =
          filter.source() == null ? null : mapSourceType(filter.source().type());
      converted.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter(
              filter.id(),
              Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.title()), filter.id()),
              type,
              isAdvancedFilter(type, groupFilter),
              options,
              Strings.trimToNull(filter.defaultValue()),
              filter.defaultValues(),
              filterSourceType,
              Strings.trimToNull(filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().ref()),
              Strings.trimToNull(filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().valueField()),
              Strings.trimToNull(filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().labelField())));
    }
    return converted.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(converted);
  }

  private static Conversion convertWidgets(
      List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget> widgets,
      Map<String, DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> filtersById) {
    if (widgets == null || widgets.isEmpty()) {
      return new Conversion(List.of(), List.of(), List.of());
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source> sources = new ArrayList<>();
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget> converted = new ArrayList<>();
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link> links = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget : widgets) {
      if (widget == null || Strings.trimToNull(widget.id()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source = convertSource(widget);
      if (source != null) {
        sources.add(source);
      }
      converted.add(convertWidget(widget, source, filtersById));
      links.addAll(convertLinks(widget));
    }
    return new Conversion(
        sources.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sources),
        converted.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(converted),
        links.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(links));
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget convertWidget(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source,
      Map<String, DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> filtersById) {
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType widgetType = mapWidgetType(widget);
    if (source == null && widgetType != StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.ACTION_PANEL) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] source is required");
    }
    if (source != null
        && source.type() == StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STREAM
        && widgetType == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.ACTION_PANEL) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] action widget cannot bind stream source");
    }
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget(
        widget.id(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(widget.title()), widget.id()),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(widget.subtitle()), Strings.trimToNull(widget.description())),
        widgetType,
        source == null ? null : source.id(),
        widgetColumns(widget),
        widgetKeyField(widget, widgetType),
        widgetLabelField(widget, widgetType),
        widgetValueField(widget, widgetType),
        widgetToneField(widget, widgetType),
        convertFilterBindings(widget.filterBindings(), filtersById),
        convertActions(widget),
        convertDrilldowns(widget, widgetType),
        convertRefreshPolicy(widget.refreshPolicy()),
        null,
        Strings.trimToNull(widget.description()),
        convertWidgetLayout(widget.layout()),
        convertColumnSpecs(widget),
        mapChartType(widget.chart() == null ? null : widget.chart().chartType()),
        Strings.trimToNull(widget.chart() == null ? null : widget.chart().seriesField()),
        widget.chart() == null ? Boolean.TRUE : widget.chart().clickable(),
        mapStreamMode(widget.stream() == null ? null : widget.stream().mode()));
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source convertSource(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget) {
    if (widget == null || Strings.trimToNull(widget.id()) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionDashboard.WidgetSource source = widget.source();
    if (source == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (source.type() == DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.STREAM
        && Strings.trimToNull(source.stream()) == null
        && Strings.trimToNull(source.ref()) == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] stream source requires source.stream or source.ref");
    }
    if (source.type() == DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.SERVICE
        && Strings.trimToNull(source.query()) == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] service source requires source.query (service/method dispatch is not supported yet)");
    }
    if (source.type() == DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.STREAM
        && source.mode() == DefinitionDashboard.SourceMode.SNAPSHOT) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] stream source mode SNAPSHOT is not supported; use LIVE");
    }
    if ((source.type() == DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.DATASET
            || source.type() == DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.MATERIALIZED_VIEW)
        && Strings.trimToNull(source.ref()) == null
        && Strings.trimToNull(source.query()) == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] dataset source requires source.ref or source.query");
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> parameters = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (source.parameters() != null) {
      parameters.putAll(source.parameters());
    }
    addParameter(parameters, "query", source.query());
    addParameter(parameters, "stream", source.stream());
    addParameter(parameters, "service", source.service());
    addParameter(parameters, "method", source.method());
    addParameter(parameters, "ref", source.ref());
    addParameter(parameters, "streamId", source.stream());
    addParameter(parameters, "sourceMode", enumName(accessor(source, "mode")));
    addParameter(parameters, "limit", integerText(accessor(source, "limit")));

    DefinitionDashboard.StreamWidget streamWidget = widget.stream();
    addParameter(parameters, "streamMode", enumName(accessor(streamWidget, "mode")));
    addParameter(
        parameters,
        "streamMaxRows",
        integerText(streamWidget == null ? null : streamWidget.maxRows()));
    addParameter(
        parameters,
        "streamAutoStart",
        booleanText(streamWidget == null ? null : streamWidget.autoStart()));

    String sourceId = widget.id() + ".source";
    String resourceId =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(source.ref()),
            Strings.trimToNull(source.stream()),
            Strings.trimToNull(source.service()),
            Strings.trimToNull(source.method()));
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source(
        sourceId,
        mapSourceType(source.type()),
        null,
        resourceId,
        parameters.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(parameters),
        List.of());
  }

  private static Map<String, String> convertFilterBindings(
      List<String> bindings, Map<String, DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> filtersById) {
    if (bindings == null || bindings.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    if (filtersById == null || filtersById.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard.widget.filterBindings requires dashboard filters");
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> mapped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String binding : bindings) {
      String filterId = Strings.trimToNull(binding);
      if (filterId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter filter = filtersById.get(normalizeKey(filterId));
      if (filter == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "dashboard.widget.filterBindings references unknown filter id '" + filterId + "'");
      }
      String parameter = Strings.trimToNull(filter.field());
      if (parameter == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "dashboard.filter[" + filterId + "] is missing required field mapping");
      }
      mapped.put(filterId, parameter);
    }
    return mapped.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(mapped);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action> convertActions(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget) {
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    if (widget == null) {
      return List.of();
    }

    DefinitionDashboard.ActionWidget actionWidget = widget.action();
    if (actionWidget != null) {
      String target =
          Strings.trimToNull(actionWidget.inputs() == null ? null : actionWidget.inputs().get("target"));
      if (target == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] action widget requires action.inputs.target");
      }
      if (actionWidget.actionType() == DefinitionDashboard.ActionType.NAVIGATE) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] actionType NAVIGATE is not supported in Stitch action panel");
      }
      actions.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action(
              widget.id() + ".action",
              Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(actionWidget.label()), "ACTION"),
              null,
              mapActionType(actionWidget.actionType()),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionScope.WIDGET,
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.PRIMARY,
              target,
              actionWidget.inputs() == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(actionWidget.inputs()),
              Boolean.TRUE.equals(actionWidget.confirm()),
              Strings.trimToNull(actionWidget.confirmMessage()),
              null,
              null,
              true));
    }

    DefinitionDashboard.TableWidget table = widget.table();
    if (table != null && table.rowActions() != null && !table.rowActions().isEmpty()) {
      for (DefinitionDashboard.RowAction rowAction : table.rowActions()) {
        if (rowAction == null) {
          continue;
        }
        DefinitionDashboard.WidgetAction rowWidgetAction = rowAction.action();
        String target =
            Strings.firstNonBlank(
                rowWidgetAction == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(rowWidgetAction.targetWidgetId()),
                rowAction.drilldown() == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(rowAction.drilldown().target()));
        if (target == null) {
          continue;
        }
        Map<String, String> parameters =
            rowWidgetAction == null || rowWidgetAction.parameterMappings() == null
                ? Map.of()
                : Map.copyOf(rowWidgetAction.parameterMappings());
        actions.add(
            new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action(
                Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rowAction.id()), widget.id() + ".row.action"),
                Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rowAction.label()), "OPEN"),
                null,
                mapActionType(rowAction.type()),
                StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionScope.ROW,
                mapActionTone(rowAction.style()),
                target,
                parameters,
                false,
                null,
                null,
                null,
                true));
      }
    }

    return actions.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Drilldown> convertDrilldowns(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget, StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType widgetType) {
    if (widget == null || widget.drilldown() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    DefinitionDashboard.Drilldown drilldown = widget.drilldown();
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType event =
        widgetType == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.TABLE
                || widgetType == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.STREAM_LOG
            ? StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ROW_SELECTED
            : StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ITEM_SELECTED;
    return List.of(
        new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Drilldown(
            event,
            mapDrilldownType(drilldown.type()),
            Strings.trimToNull(drilldown.target()),
            drilldown.parameterMappings() == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(drilldown.parameterMappings()),
            true));
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link> convertLinks(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget) {
    if (widget == null || widget.actions() == null || widget.actions().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link> links = new ArrayList<>();
    int index = 0;
    for (DefinitionDashboard.WidgetAction action : widget.actions()) {
      if (action == null || Strings.trimToNull(action.targetWidgetId()) == null) {
        index++;
        continue;
      }
      links.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link(
              Strings.firstNonBlank(
                  Strings.trimToNull(action.id()), widget.id() + ".link." + index),
              widget.id(),
              mapEventForLink(widget.type()),
              List.of(action.targetWidgetId()),
              action.parameterMappings() == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(action.parameterMappings())));
      index++;
    }
    return links.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(links);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow> convertLayoutRows(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout layout, List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget> widgets) {
    if (layout != null && layout.sections() != null && !layout.sections().isEmpty()) {
      List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
      for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardSection section : layout.sections()) {
        if (section == null || section.placements() == null || section.placements().isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        List<String> widgetIds = new ArrayList<>();
        for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement placement : section.placements()) {
          if (placement == null) {
            continue;
          }
          String widgetId = Strings.trimToNull(placement.widgetId());
          if (widgetId != null) {
            widgetIds.add(widgetId);
          }
        }
        if (!widgetIds.isEmpty()) {
          rows.add(new StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow(widgetIds));
        }
      }
      if (!rows.isEmpty()) {
        return List.copyOf(rows);
      }
    }
    if (widgets == null || widgets.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> widgetIds = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget : widgets) {
      if (widget == null || Strings.trimToNull(widget.id()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      widgetIds.add(widget.id());
    }
    return widgetIds.isEmpty()
        ? List.of()
        : List.of(new StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow(List.copyOf(widgetIds)));
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy convertRefreshPolicy(
      DefinitionDashboard.RefreshPolicy refreshPolicy) {
    if (refreshPolicy == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy(
        mapRefreshMode(refreshPolicy.mode()), refreshPolicy.intervalSeconds());
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardLayout convertLayout(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout layout) {
    if (layout == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardLayout.empty();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutSection> sections = new ArrayList<>();
    if (layout.sections() != null) {
      for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardSection section : layout.sections()) {
        if (section == null || section.placements() == null || section.placements().isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutPlacement> placements = new ArrayList<>();
        for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement placement : section.placements()) {
          if (placement == null || Strings.trimToNull(placement.widgetId()) == null) {
            continue;
          }
          placements.add(
              new StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutPlacement(
                  placement.widgetId(), placement.colSpan(), placement.rowSpan()));
        }
        if (!placements.isEmpty()) {
          sections.add(
              new StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutSection(
                  section.id(), section.title(), section.columns(), List.copyOf(placements)));
        }
      }
    }
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardLayout(
        layout.columns(), layout.gap(), sections.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sections));
  }

  private static Map<String, DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> indexFilters(
      List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> filters) {
    if (filters == null || filters.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter filter : filters) {
      if (filter == null || Strings.trimToNull(filter.id()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      indexed.putIfAbsent(normalizeKey(filter.id()), filter);
    }
    return indexed.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(indexed);
  }

  private static List<String> filterOptions(List<DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption> options) {
    if (options == null || options.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption option : options) {
      if (option == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String value = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(option.value()), Strings.trimToNull(option.label()));
      if (value != null) {
        values.add(value);
      }
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static List<String> widgetColumns(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget) {
    if (widget == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> columns = new ArrayList<>();
    DefinitionDashboard.TableWidget table = widget.table();
    if (table != null && table.columns() != null) {
      for (DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn column : table.columns()) {
        if (column == null || Strings.trimToNull(column.field()) == null) {
          continue;
        }
        columns.add(column.field());
      }
    }
    DefinitionDashboard.StreamWidget stream = widget.stream();
    if (columns.isEmpty() && stream != null && stream.columns() != null) {
      for (DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn column : stream.columns()) {
        if (column == null || Strings.trimToNull(column.field()) == null) {
          continue;
        }
        columns.add(column.field());
      }
    }
    return columns.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(columns);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.ColumnSpec> convertColumnSpecs(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget) {
    if (widget == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> sourceColumns = null;
    if (widget.table() != null && widget.table().columns() != null && !widget.table().columns().isEmpty()) {
      sourceColumns = widget.table().columns();
    } else if (widget.stream() != null
        && widget.stream().columns() != null
        && !widget.stream().columns().isEmpty()) {
      sourceColumns = widget.stream().columns();
    }
    if (sourceColumns == null || sourceColumns.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.ColumnSpec> specs = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn column : sourceColumns) {
      if (column == null || Strings.trimToNull(column.field()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      specs.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.ColumnSpec(
              column.field(),
              Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(column.title()), Strings.trimToNull(column.field())),
              column.width(),
              column.visible(),
              Strings.trimToNull(column.format())));
    }
    return specs.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(specs);
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetLayout convertWidgetLayout(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement placement) {
    if (placement == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetLayout.singleCell();
    }
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetLayout(placement.colSpan(), placement.rowSpan());
  }

  private static String widgetKeyField(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget, StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType type) {
    if (widget == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.BAR_CHART && widget.chart() != null) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(widget.chart().categoryField());
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.KPI_TILES) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(
          widget.kpi() == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(widget.kpi().secondaryField()),
          "status");
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String widgetLabelField(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget, StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType type) {
    if (widget == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.BAR_CHART && widget.chart() != null) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(widget.chart().categoryField());
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.KPI_TILES) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(
          widget.kpi() == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(widget.kpi().secondaryField()),
          "label");
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String widgetValueField(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget, StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType type) {
    if (widget == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.BAR_CHART && widget.chart() != null) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(widget.chart().valueField());
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.KPI_TILES && widget.kpi() != null) {
      return Strings.trimToNull(widget.kpi().valueField());
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String widgetToneField(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget, StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType type) {
    if (widget == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.KPI_TILES) {
      return "tone";
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType mapFilterType(
      DefinitionDashboard.FilterType type,
      boolean groupFilter) {
    if (groupFilter) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.SELECT;
    }
    if (type == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.SELECT;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case GROUP -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.SELECT;
      case SELECT -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.SELECT;
      case MULTI_SELECT -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.MULTI_SELECT;
      case TEXT -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.TEXT;
      case DATE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.DATE;
      case TIME -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.TIME;
      case DATE_RANGE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.DATE_TIME_RANGE;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType mapWidgetType(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget) {
    DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType type = widget == null ? null : widget.type();
    if (type == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.TABLE;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case KPI -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.KPI_TILES;
      case TABLE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.TABLE;
      case CHART -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.BAR_CHART;
      case STREAM -> {
        DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode streamMode = widget == null || widget.stream() == null ? null : widget.stream().mode();
        if (streamMode == DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode.HYBRID) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] stream.mode HYBRID is not supported yet");
        }
        if (streamMode == DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode.TABLE) {
          yield StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.TABLE;
        }
        yield StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.STREAM_LOG;
      }
      case STATUS ->
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "dashboard.widget[" + widget.id() + "] STATUS widgets are not supported yet");
      case ACTION -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.ACTION_PANEL;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType mapChartType(DefinitionDashboard.ChartType type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case BAR -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType.BAR;
      case LINE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType.LINE;
      case AREA -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType.AREA;
      case DONUT -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType.DONUT;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.StreamMode mapStreamMode(DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return switch (mode) {
      case EVENT -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.StreamMode.EVENT;
      case TABLE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.StreamMode.TABLE;
      case HYBRID -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.StreamMode.HYBRID;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType mapSourceType(DefinitionDashboard.SourceType type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STATIC;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case DATASET -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.DATASET_QUERY;
      case MATERIALIZED_VIEW -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.MATERIALIZED_VIEW;
      case STREAM -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STREAM;
      case SERVICE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.SERVICE_QUERY;
      case INLINE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STATIC;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType mapActionType(DefinitionDashboard.ActionType type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType.CUSTOM_CALLBACK;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case SERVICE_CALL -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType.SERVICE_ACTION;
      case DATA_UPDATE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType.DATA_ACTION;
      case NAVIGATE, CUSTOM -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType.CUSTOM_CALLBACK;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone mapActionTone(String style) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(style);
    if (value == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.PRIMARY;
    }
    String normalized = value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (normalized.contains("danger") || normalized.contains("error") || normalized.contains("destructive")) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.DANGER;
    }
    if (normalized.contains("success")) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.SUCCESS;
    }
    if (normalized.contains("info")) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.INFO;
    }
    if (normalized.contains("neutral")) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.NEUTRAL;
    }
    return StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.PRIMARY;
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType mapDrilldownType(
      DefinitionDashboard.DrilldownType type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType.DIALOG;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case DASHBOARD -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType.DASHBOARD;
      case DIALOG -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType.DIALOG;
      case FILTER -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType.FILTER;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType mapEventForLink(DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType sourceType) {
    if (sourceType == DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.TABLE || sourceType == DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.STREAM) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ROW_SELECTED;
    }
    if (sourceType == DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.CHART) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.POINT_CLICKED;
    }
    if (sourceType == DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.KPI) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.TILE_CLICKED;
    }
    return StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ITEM_SELECTED;
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode mapRefreshMode(
      DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.ON_FILTER_CHANGE;
    }
    return switch (mode) {
      case MANUAL -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.MANUAL;
      case INTERVAL -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.INTERVAL;
      case LIVE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.LIVE;
      case ON_FILTER_CHANGE -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.ON_FILTER_CHANGE;
      case ON_LINK_EVENT -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.ON_LINK_EVENT;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardMode mapDashboardMode(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardMode.STANDARD;
    }
    return switch (mode) {
      case STANDARD -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardMode.STANDARD;
      case FULL_SCREEN -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardMode.FULL_SCREEN;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardVisibility mapDashboardVisibility(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility visibility) {
    if (visibility == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardVisibility.GROUP;
    }
    return switch (visibility) {
      case PUBLIC -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardVisibility.PUBLIC;
      case GROUP -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardVisibility.GROUP;
      case USER -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardVisibility.USER;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardExecutionMode mapDashboardExecutionMode(
      DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode mode) {
    if (mode == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED;
    }
    return switch (mode) {
      case SHARED -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED;
      case PER_USER -> StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardExecutionMode.PER_USER;
    };
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardSemantic convertSemantic(
      org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common.Semantic semantic) {
    if (semantic == null) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardSemantic.empty();
    }
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardSemantic(
        semantic.title(), semantic.description(), semantic.domain(), semantic.subdomain(), semantic.tags());
  }

  private static boolean isGroupFilter(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter filter) {
    if (filter == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return "group".equalsIgnoreCase(
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(filter.id()), Strings.trimToNull(filter.field()), ""));
  }

  private static boolean isAdvancedFilter(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType type, boolean groupFilter) {
    if (groupFilter) {
      return false;
    }
    return type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.DATE
        || type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.TIME
        || type == StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.DATE_TIME_RANGE;
  }

  private static void addParameter(Map<String, String> parameters, String key, String value) {
    String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    String normalizedValue = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalizedKey != null && normalizedValue != null) {
      parameters.putIfAbsent(normalizedKey, normalizedValue);
    }
  }

  private static String enumName(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof Enum<?> enumValue) {
      return enumValue.name();
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(value == null ? null : String.valueOf(value));
  }

  private static String integerText(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof Number number) {
      return String.valueOf(number.intValue());
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String booleanText(Object value) {
    if (value instanceof Boolean flag) {
      return String.valueOf(flag);
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static Object accessor(Object target, String method) {
    if (target == null || Strings.trimToNull(method) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return target.getClass().getMethod(method).invoke(target);
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static DiscoveryCache requireCache(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    if (runtimeContext == null || runtimeContext.session() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Stitch runtime session is not available");
    }
    Fabric.Session session = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(session instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    DiscoveryCache cache = resolved.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private static List<DefinitionDashboard> safe(List<DefinitionDashboard> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private record Conversion(
      List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source> sources,
      List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget> widgets,
      List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link> links) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDescriptor.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/**
 * Opinionated Stitch dashboard descriptor model.
 */
public record StitchDashboardDescriptor(
    String id,
    String title,
    String subtitle,
    String description,
    String category,
    List<String> tags,
    List<SharedFilter> sharedFilters,
    List<Source> sources,
    List<Widget> widgets,
    List<LayoutRow> layoutRows,
    List<Link> links,
    RefreshPolicy refreshPolicy,
    DashboardMode mode,
    DashboardVisibility visibility,
    DashboardExecutionMode executionMode,
    DashboardSemantic semantic,
    DashboardLayout layout) {

  public StitchDashboardDescriptor {
    id = require(id, "id");
    title = normalizeTitle(title, id);
    subtitle = Strings.trimToNull(subtitle);
    description = Strings.trimToNull(description);
    category = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(category), "General");
    tags = normalizeStrings(tags);
    sharedFilters = sharedFilters == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sharedFilters);
    sources = sources == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sources);
    widgets = normalizeWidgets(widgets);
    layoutRows = normalizeLayoutRows(layoutRows, widgets);
    links = links == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(links);
    refreshPolicy = refreshPolicy == null ? RefreshPolicy.defaultPolicy() : refreshPolicy.normalized();
    mode = mode == null ? DashboardMode.STANDARD : mode;
    visibility = visibility == null ? DashboardVisibility.GROUP : visibility;
    executionMode = executionMode == null ? DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED : executionMode;
    semantic = semantic == null ? DashboardSemantic.empty() : semantic.normalized();
    layout = layout == null ? DashboardLayout.empty() : layout.normalized();
  }

  // Backward-compatible constructor used by legacy descriptor loading paths.
  public StitchDashboardDescriptor(
      String id,
      String title,
      String subtitle,
      String description,
      String category,
      List<String> tags,
      List<SharedFilter> sharedFilters,
      List<Source> sources,
      List<Widget> widgets,
      List<LayoutRow> layoutRows,
      List<Link> links,
      RefreshPolicy refreshPolicy) {
    this(
        id,
        title,
        subtitle,
        description,
        category,
        tags,
        sharedFilters,
        sources,
        widgets,
        layoutRows,
        links,
        refreshPolicy,
        DashboardMode.STANDARD,
        DashboardVisibility.GROUP,
        DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED,
        DashboardSemantic.empty(),
        DashboardLayout.empty());
  }

  public Widget widget(String widgetId) {
    String normalized = normalizedKey(widgetId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (Widget widget : widgets) {
      if (widget != null && normalized.equals(normalizedKey(widget.id()))) {
        return widget;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public Source source(String sourceId) {
    String normalized = normalizedKey(sourceId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (Source source : sources) {
      if (source != null && normalized.equals(normalizedKey(source.id()))) {
        return source;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public enum DashboardMode {
    STANDARD,
    FULL_SCREEN;

    public static DashboardMode from(String value, DashboardMode fallback) {
      String normalized = normalizedKey(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return fallback;
      }
      for (DashboardMode candidate : values()) {
        if (normalized.equals(normalizedKey(candidate.name()))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  public enum DashboardVisibility {
    PUBLIC,
    GROUP,
    USER;

    public static DashboardVisibility from(String value, DashboardVisibility fallback) {
      String normalized = normalizedKey(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return fallback;
      }
      for (DashboardVisibility candidate : values()) {
        if (normalized.equals(normalizedKey(candidate.name()))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  public enum DashboardExecutionMode {
    SHARED,
    PER_USER;

    public static DashboardExecutionMode from(String value, DashboardExecutionMode fallback) {
      String normalized = normalizedKey(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return fallback;
      }
      for (DashboardExecutionMode candidate : values()) {
        if (normalized.equals(normalizedKey(candidate.name()))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  public enum FilterType {
    SELECT,
    MULTI_SELECT,
    TEXT,
    TOGGLE,
    NUMBER,
    DATE,
    TIME,
    DATE_TIME_RANGE;

    public static FilterType from(String value, FilterType fallback) {
      String normalized = normalizedKey(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return fallback;
      }
      for (FilterType candidate : values()) {
        if (normalized.equals(normalizedKey(candidate.name()))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  public enum WidgetType {
    KPI_TILES,
    BAR_CHART,
    TABLE,
    STREAM_LOG,
    ACTION_PANEL,
    STATUS;

    public static WidgetType from(String value, WidgetType fallback) {
      String normalized = normalizedKey(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return fallback;
      }
      for (WidgetType candidate : values()) {
        if (normalized.equals(normalizedKey(candidate.name()))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  public enum ChartType {
    BAR,
    LINE,
    AREA,
    DONUT;

    public static ChartType from(String value, ChartType fallback) {
      String normalized = normalizedKey(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return fallback;
      }
      for (ChartType candidate : values()) {
        if (normalized.equals(normalizedKey(candidate.name()))) {
          return candidate;
        }
      }
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  public record DashboardSemantic(

  public record SharedFilter(

    }

  public record Widget(
      String id,
      String title,
      String subtitle,
      WidgetType type,
      String sourceId,
      List<String> columns,
      String keyField,
      String labelField,
      String valueField,
      String toneField,
      Map<String, String> filterBindings,
      List<Action> actions,
      List<Drilldown> drilldowns,
      RefreshPolicy refreshPolicy,
      String emptyTitle,
      String emptyMessage,
      WidgetLayout layout,
      List<ColumnSpec> columnSpecs,
      ChartType chartType,
      String chartSeriesField,
      Boolean chartClickable,
      StreamMode streamMode) {
    public Widget {
      id = require(id, "widget.id");
      title = normalizeTitle(title, id);
      subtitle = Strings.trimToNull(subtitle);
      type = type == null ? WidgetType.TABLE : type;
      sourceId = Strings.trimToNull(sourceId);
      columns = normalizeStrings(columns);
      keyField = Strings.trimToNull(keyField);
      labelField = Strings.trimToNull(labelField);
      valueField = Strings.trimToNull(valueField);
      toneField = Strings.trimToNull(toneField);
      filterBindings = normalizeMap(filterBindings);
      actions = actions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(actions);
      drilldowns = drilldowns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(drilldowns);
      refreshPolicy = refreshPolicy == null ? null : refreshPolicy.normalized();
      emptyTitle = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(emptyTitle), "No data");
      emptyMessage =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(emptyMessage), "No records match current dashboard context.");
      layout = layout == null ? WidgetLayout.singleCell() : layout;
      columnSpecs = normalizeColumnSpecs(columnSpecs, columns);
      chartType = chartType == null ? null : chartType;
      chartSeriesField = Strings.trimToNull(chartSeriesField);
      chartClickable = chartClickable == null ? Boolean.TRUE : chartClickable;
      streamMode = streamMode == null ? null : streamMode;
    }

    // Backward-compatible constructor used by legacy descriptor loading paths.
    public Widget(
        String id,
        String title,
        String subtitle,
        WidgetType type,
        String sourceId,
        List<String> columns,
        String keyField,
        String labelField,
        String valueField,
        String toneField,
        Map<String, String> filterBindings,
        List<Action> actions,
        List<Drilldown> drilldowns,
        RefreshPolicy refreshPolicy,

      this(
          id,

          toneField,

          actions,
          drilldowns,
          refreshPolicy,
          emptyTitle,
          emptyMessage,
          WidgetLayout.singleCell(),
          List.of(),
          null,
          null,
          Boolean.TRUE,
          null);
    }
  }

  public record Drilldown(
      EventType event,
      DrilldownType type,
      String target,
      Map<String, String> payloadToParameter,
      boolean includeSharedFilters) {
    public Drilldown {
      event = event == null ? EventType.ITEM_SELECTED : event;
      type = type == null ? DrilldownType.DIALOG : type;
      target = Strings.trimToNull(target);
      payloadToParameter = normalizeMap(payloadToParameter);
    }
  }

  public record Action(
      String id,
      String label,
      String icon,
      ActionType type,
      ActionScope scope,
      ActionTone tone,
      String target,
      Map<String, String> parameters,
      boolean confirmationRequired,
      String confirmationMessage,
      String successMessage,
      String failureMessage,
      boolean includeSharedFilters) {
    public Action {
      id = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(id), "action");
      label = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), "ACTION");
      icon = Strings.trimToNull(icon);
      type = type == null ? ActionType.CUSTOM_CALLBACK : type;
      scope = scope == null ? ActionScope.WIDGET : scope;
      tone = tone == null ? ActionTone.PRIMARY : tone;
      target = Strings.trimToNull(target);
      parameters = normalizeMap(parameters);
      confirmationMessage = Strings.trimToNull(confirmationMessage);
      successMessage = Strings.trimToNull(successMessage);
      failureMessage = Strings.trimToNull(failureMessage);
