  public record Link(
      String id,
      String sourceWidgetId,
      EventType event,
      List<String> targetWidgetIds,
      Map<String, String> payloadToTargetParameter) {
    public Link {
      id = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(id), "link");
      sourceWidgetId = require(sourceWidgetId, "link.sourceWidgetId");
      event = event == null ? EventType.ITEM_SELECTED : event;
      targetWidgetIds = normalizeStrings(targetWidgetIds);
      payloadToTargetParameter = normalizeMap(payloadToTargetParameter);
    }
  }

  public record LayoutRow(List<String> widgetIds) {
    public LayoutRow {
      widgetIds = normalizeStrings(widgetIds);
    }
  }

  private static List<Widget> normalizeWidgets(List<Widget> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Widget> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> seen = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Widget value : values) {
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = normalizedKey(value.id());
      if (key == null || seen.contains(key)) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.add(value);
      seen.add(key);
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static List<LayoutRow> normalizeLayoutRows(List<LayoutRow> rows, List<Widget> widgets) {
    if (rows != null && !rows.isEmpty()) {
      List<LayoutRow> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
      for (LayoutRow row : rows) {
        if (row == null || row.widgetIds().isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        normalized.add(row);
      }
      if (!normalized.isEmpty()) {
        return List.copyOf(normalized);
      }
    }
    if (widgets == null || widgets.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<LayoutRow> singleColumn = new ArrayList<>(widgets.size());
    for (Widget widget : widgets) {
      singleColumn.add(new LayoutRow(List.of(widget.id())));
    }
    return List.copyOf(singleColumn);
  }

  private static List<LayoutSection> normalizeLayoutSections(List<LayoutSection> sections) {
    if (sections == null || sections.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<LayoutSection> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (LayoutSection section : sections) {
      if (section == null || section.placements().isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.add(section);
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static List<LayoutPlacement> normalizeLayoutPlacements(List<LayoutPlacement> placements) {
    if (placements == null || placements.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<LayoutPlacement> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (LayoutPlacement placement : placements) {
      if (placement == null || Strings.trimToNull(placement.widgetId()) == null) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.add(placement);
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static List<ColumnSpec> normalizeColumnSpecs(List<ColumnSpec> specs, List<String> columns) {
    List<ColumnSpec> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    if (specs != null) {
      LinkedHashSet<String> seen = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (ColumnSpec spec : specs) {
        if (spec == null || Strings.trimToNull(spec.field()) == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = normalizedKey(spec.field());
        if (key == null || seen.contains(key)) {
          continue;
        }
        normalized.add(spec);
        seen.add(key);
      }
    }
    if (!normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return List.copyOf(normalized);
    }
    if (columns == null || columns.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ColumnSpec> derived = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String column : columns) {
      String field = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (field == null) {
        continue;
      }
      derived.add(new ColumnSpec(field, field, null, Boolean.TRUE, null));
    }
    return derived.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(derived);
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeStrings(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String item = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (item != null) {
        normalized.add(item);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> normalizeMap(Map<String, String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      if (key != null && value != null) {
        normalized.put(key, value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static List<Map<String, Object>> normalizeRows(List<Map<String, Object>> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map<String, Object> row : values) {
      if (row == null || row.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      rows.add(Map.copyOf(row));
    }
    return rows.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String normalizeTitle(String title, String fallback) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title), Strings.trimToNull(fallback), "Dashboard");
  }

  private static String normalizedKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardDescriptorLoader.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Io;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Loads Stitch dashboard descriptors from JSON config resources. */
public final class StitchDashboardDescriptorLoader {
  private StitchDashboardDescriptorLoader() {}

  public static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> loadFromClasspath(String resourcePath, Class<?> anchor) {
    try {
      byte[] bytes = Io.readClasspathBytes(resourcePath, anchor == null ? StitchDashboardDescriptorLoader.class : anchor);
      String json = new String(bytes, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
      return parseJson(json);
    } catch (IOException error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to load dashboard descriptor resource: " + resourcePath, error);
    }
  }

  public static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> parseJson(String json) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(json);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    try {
      JsonNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(normalized);
      ArrayNode dashboards = dashboardsNode(root);
      if (dashboards == null || dashboards.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      Map<String, JsonNode> sourceTemplates = parseTemplates(root, "sourceTemplates");
      Map<String, JsonNode> widgetTemplates = parseTemplates(root, "widgetTemplates");
      List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> parsed = new ArrayList<>();
      for (JsonNode node : dashboards) {
        if (node == null || !node.isObject()) {
          continue;
        }
        parsed.add(parseDashboard(node, sourceTemplates, widgetTemplates));
      }
      return parsed.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(parsed);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to parse dashboard descriptor JSON", error);
    }
  }

  private static ArrayNode dashboardsNode(JsonNode root) {
    if (root == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (root instanceof ArrayNode array) {
      return array;
    }
    JsonNode dashboards = root.get("dashboards");
    return dashboards instanceof ArrayNode array ? array : null;
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor parseDashboard(
      JsonNode node,
      Map<String, JsonNode> sourceTemplates,
      Map<String, JsonNode> widgetTemplates) {
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor(
        text(node, "id"),
        text(node, "title"),
        text(node, "subtitle"),
        text(node, "description"),
        text(node, "category"),
        strings(node.get("tags")),
        parseFilters(node.get("sharedFilters")),
        parseSources(node.get("sources"), sourceTemplates),
        parseWidgets(node.get("widgets"), widgetTemplates),
        parseLayout(node.get("layoutRows")),
        parseLinks(node.get("links")),
        parseRefreshPolicy(node.get("refreshPolicy")));
  }

  private static Map<String, JsonNode> parseTemplates(JsonNode root, String field) {
    if (root == null || Strings.trimToNull(field) == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    JsonNode node = root.get(field);
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array) || array.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, JsonNode> templates = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (!(value instanceof ObjectNode object)) {
        continue;
      }
      String id = normalizeTemplateKey(text(value, "id"));
      if (id == null || templates.containsKey(id)) {
        continue;
      }
      templates.put(id, object.deepCopy());
    }
    return templates.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(templates);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter> parseFilters(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter> filters = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      filters.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.SharedFilter(
              text(value, "id"),
              text(value, "label"),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.from(
                  text(value, "type"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.FilterType.SELECT),
              bool(value, "advanced"),
              strings(value.get("options")),
              text(value, "defaultValue"),
              strings(value.get("defaultValues")),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.from(
                  text(value.get("source"), "type"), null),
              text(value.get("source"), "ref"),
              text(value.get("source"), "valueField"),
              text(value.get("source"), "labelField")));
    }
    return filters.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(filters);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source> parseSources(
      JsonNode node, Map<String, JsonNode> templates) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source> sources = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      JsonNode resolved = applyTemplate(value, templates);
      sources.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source(
              text(resolved, "id"),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.from(
                  text(resolved, "type"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.SourceType.STATIC),
              text(resolved, "namespace"),
              text(resolved, "resourceId"),
              stringMap(resolved.get("parameters")),
              rows(resolved.get("staticRows"))));
    }
    return sources.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sources);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget> parseWidgets(
      JsonNode node, Map<String, JsonNode> templates) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget> widgets = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      JsonNode resolved = applyTemplate(value, templates);
      widgets.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget(
              text(resolved, "id"),
              text(resolved, "title"),
              text(resolved, "subtitle"),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.from(
                  text(resolved, "type"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.WidgetType.TABLE),
              text(resolved, "sourceId"),
              strings(resolved.get("columns")),
              text(resolved, "keyField"),
              text(resolved, "labelField"),
              text(resolved, "valueField"),
              text(resolved, "toneField"),
              stringMap(resolved.get("filterBindings")),
              parseActions(resolved.get("actions")),
              parseDrilldowns(resolved.get("drilldowns")),
              parseRefreshPolicy(resolved.get("refreshPolicy")),
              text(resolved, "emptyTitle"),
              text(resolved, "emptyMessage")));
    }
    return widgets.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(widgets);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Drilldown> parseDrilldowns(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Drilldown> drilldowns = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      drilldowns.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Drilldown(
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.from(
                  text(value, "event"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ITEM_SELECTED),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType.from(
                  text(value, "type"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.DrilldownType.DIALOG),
              text(value, "target"),
              stringMap(value.get("payloadToParameter")),
              bool(value, "includeSharedFilters")));
    }
    return drilldowns.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(drilldowns);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action> parseActions(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      actions.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action(
              text(value, "id"),
              text(value, "label"),
              text(value, "icon"),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType.from(
                  text(value, "type"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionType.CUSTOM_CALLBACK),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionScope.from(
                  text(value, "scope"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionScope.WIDGET),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.from(
                  text(value, "tone"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.ActionTone.PRIMARY),
              text(value, "target"),
              stringMap(value.get("parameters")),
              bool(value, "confirmationRequired"),
              text(value, "confirmationMessage"),
              text(value, "successMessage"),
              text(value, "failureMessage"),
              bool(value, "includeSharedFilters")));
    }
    return actions.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow> parseLayout(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      rows.add(new StitchDashboardDescriptor.LayoutRow(strings(value.get("widgetIds"))));
    }
    return rows.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link> parseLinks(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link> links = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      links.add(
          new StitchDashboardDescriptor.Link(
              text(value, "id"),
              text(value, "sourceWidgetId"),
              StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.from(
                  text(value, "event"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ITEM_SELECTED),
              strings(value.get("targetWidgetIds")),
              stringMap(value.get("payloadToTargetParameter"))));
    }
    return links.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(links);
  }

  private static StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy parseRefreshPolicy(JsonNode node) {
    if (node == null || !node.isObject()) {
      return StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy.defaultPolicy();
    }
    return new StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy(
        StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.from(
            text(node, "mode"), StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshMode.ON_FILTER_CHANGE),
        intValue(node, "intervalSeconds"));
  }

  private static List<String> strings(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      String text = value == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(value.asText(null));
      if (text != null) {
        values.add(text);
      }
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static Map<String, String> stringMap(JsonNode node) {
    if (node == null || !node.isObject()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    node.fields()
        .forEachRemaining(
            entry -> {
              String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
              String value = entry.getValue() == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue().asText(null));
              if (key != null && value != null) {
                values.put(key, value);
              }
            });
    return values.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  private static List<Map<String, Object>> rows(JsonNode node) {
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode value : array) {
      if (value == null || !value.isObject()) {
        continue;
      }
      @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
      Map<String, Object> row =
          DiscoveryCodec.mapper().convertValue(value, LinkedHashMap.class);
      if (row != null && !row.isEmpty()) {
        rows.add(Map.copyOf(row));
      }
    }
    return rows.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static JsonNode applyTemplate(JsonNode value, Map<String, JsonNode> templates) {
    if (!(value instanceof ObjectNode object) || templates == null || templates.isEmpty()) {
      return value;
    }
    String templateId = normalizeTemplateKey(text(value, "template"));
    if (templateId == null) {
      return value;
    }
    JsonNode template = templates.get(templateId);
    if (!(template instanceof ObjectNode templateObject)) {
      return value;
    }
    ObjectNode merged = templateObject.deepCopy();
    merged.setAll(object);
    merged.remove("template");
    return merged;
  }

  private static String normalizeTemplateKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String text(JsonNode node, String key) {
    if (node == null || Strings.trimToNull(key) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode value = node.get(key);
    return value == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(value.asText(null));
  }

  private static boolean bool(JsonNode node, String key) {
    if (node == null || Strings.trimToNull(key) == null) {
      return false;
    }
    JsonNode value = node.get(key);
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return false;
    }
    if (value.isBoolean()) {
      return value.asBoolean();
    }
    return "true".equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.trimToEmpty(value.asText()));
  }

  private static Integer intValue(JsonNode node, String key) {
    if (node == null || Strings.trimToNull(key) == null) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode value = node.get(key);
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (value.isInt()) {
      return value.asInt();
    }
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(value.asText(null));
    if (text == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return Integer.parseInt(text);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }
}

  public StitchDashboardEditorScreen(StitchDashboardDefinitionStore store) {
    super("Dashboard Editor", "View and edit DefinitionDashboard records.");
    this.store = Objects.requireNonNull(store, "store");

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    body().getStyle().set("gap", "0.7rem");
    addClassName("stitch-dashboard-editor");

    configureHeaderActions();
    configureMetadataSection();
    configureFilterSection();
    configureWidgetSection();
    configureLayoutSection();
    setEditMode(false);

    addToBody(summary, metadataSection, filtersSection, widgetsSection, layoutSection);
  }

  public StitchDashboardEditorScreen onOpen(Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> handler) {
    this.openHandler = handler;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDashboardEditorScreen onSaved(Consumer<StitchDashboardDefinitionRef> handler) {
    this.savedHandler = handler;
    return this;
  }

  public void load(String group, String name) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String resolvedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    if (resolvedGroup == null || resolvedName == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("dashboard group/name are required");
    }
    DefinitionDashboard definition =
        store.get(resolvedGroup, resolvedName)
            .orElseThrow(
                () -> new IllegalStateException("Dashboard not found: " + resolvedGroup + "/" + resolvedName));
    apply(definition);
    setEditMode(false);
  }

  private void configureHeaderActions() {
    primary(editAction);
    primary(saveAction);
    neutral(cancelAction);
    neutral(jsonAction);
    neutral(openAction);

    editAction.addClickListener(event -> setEditMode(true));
    saveAction.addClickListener(event -> save());
    cancelAction.addClickListener(event -> cancel());
    jsonAction.addClickListener(event -> new StitchJsonDialog("Dashboard JSON", buildDefinition()).open());
    openAction.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (openHandler != null && currentRef != null) {
            openHandler.accept(currentRef);
          }
        });

    addPageAction(editAction, saveAction, cancelAction, jsonAction, openAction);
  }

  private void configureMetadataSection() {
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setWidthFull();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("44em", 2),
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("72em", 3));

    groupField.setRequired(true);
    nameField.setRequired(true);
    titleField.setRequired(true);
    descriptionField.setMinHeight("5rem");
    descriptionField.getStyle().set("grid-column", "1 / -1");

    modeField.setLabel("Mode");
    modeField.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode.values());
    visibilityField.setLabel("Visibility");
    visibilityField.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.values());
    executionModeField.setLabel("Execution");
    executionModeField.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.values());
    refreshModeField.setLabel("Refresh");
    refreshModeField.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode.values());

    layoutColumnsField.setMin(1);
    layoutColumnsField.setStepButtonsVisible(true);
    refreshIntervalField.setMin(1);
    refreshIntervalField.setStepButtonsVisible(true);

    HorizontalLayout enabledWrap = new HorizontalLayout(enabledField);
    enabledWrap.setPadding(false);
    enabledWrap.setSpacing(false);
    enabledWrap.getStyle().set("grid-column", "1 / -1");

    form.add(
        groupField,
        nameField,
        titleField,
        categoryField,
        tagsField,
        modeField,
        visibilityField,
        executionModeField,
        layoutColumnsField,
        layoutGapField,
        refreshModeField,
        refreshIntervalField,
        enabledWrap,
        descriptionField);
    metadataSection.addToBody(form);
  }

  private void configureFilterSection() {
    neutral(addFilterAction);
    neutral(editFilterAction);
    neutral(removeFilterAction);
    filtersSection.addSectionAction(addFilterAction, editFilterAction, removeFilterAction);

    addFilterAction.addClickListener(event -> openFilterDialog(null, -1));
    editFilterAction.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          FilterDraft selected = filtersGrid.asSingleSelect().getValue();
          int index = selected == null ? -1 : filters.indexOf(selected);
          openFilterDialog(selected, index);
        });
    removeFilterAction.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (!editMode) {
            return;
          }
          FilterDraft selected = filtersGrid.asSingleSelect().getValue();
          if (selected == null) {
            return;
          }
          filters.remove(selected);
          refreshFilters();
        });

    filtersGrid.setWidthFull();
    filtersGrid.addColumn(FilterDraft::id).setHeader("ID").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    filtersGrid.addColumn(FilterDraft::title).setHeader("TITLE");
    filtersGrid.addColumn(d -> d.type().name()).setHeader("TYPE").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    filtersGrid.addColumn(FilterDraft::field).setHeader("FIELD").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    filtersGrid.addColumn(FilterDraft::sourceSummary).setHeader("SOURCE");
    filtersGrid.addItemDoubleClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (!editMode) {
            return;
          }
          FilterDraft selected = event.getItem();
          openFilterDialog(selected, filters.indexOf(selected));
        });

    filtersSection.addToBody(filtersGrid);
  }

  private void configureWidgetSection() {
    neutral(addWidgetAction);
    neutral(editWidgetAction);
    neutral(removeWidgetAction);
    widgetsSection.addSectionAction(addWidgetAction, editWidgetAction, removeWidgetAction);

    addWidgetAction.addClickListener(event -> openWidgetDialog(null, -1));
    editWidgetAction.addClickListener(

          int index = selected == null ? -1 : widgets.indexOf(selected);
          openWidgetDialog(selected, index);
        });
    removeWidgetAction.addClickListener(

            return;

          WidgetDraft selected = widgetsGrid.asSingleSelect().getValue();
          if (selected == null) {
            return;
          }
          widgets.remove(selected);
          refreshWidgets();

    widgetsGrid.setWidthFull();
    widgetsGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::id).setHeader("ID").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    widgetsGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::title).setHeader("TITLE");
    widgetsGrid.addColumn(d -> d.type().name()).setHeader("TYPE").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    widgetsGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::sourceSummary).setHeader("SOURCE");
    widgetsGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::sectionSummary).setHeader("SECTION");
    widgetsGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::orderSummary).setHeader("ORDER").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    widgetsGrid.addItemDoubleClickListener(
        event -> {

  }

  private void configureLayoutSection() {
    neutral(editPlacementAction);
    neutral(placementUpAction);
    neutral(placementDownAction);
    layoutSection.addSectionAction(editPlacementAction, placementUpAction, placementDownAction);

    editPlacementAction.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          WidgetDraft selected = layoutGrid.asSingleSelect().getValue();
          int index = selected == null ? -1 : widgets.indexOf(selected);
          openPlacementDialog(selected, index);
        });
    placementUpAction.addClickListener(event -> movePlacement(-1));
    placementDownAction.addClickListener(event -> movePlacement(1));

    layoutGrid.setWidthFull();
    layoutGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::sectionSummary).setHeader("SECTION");
    layoutGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::id).setHeader("WIDGET").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    layoutGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::orderSummary).setHeader("ORDER").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    layoutGrid.addColumn(WidgetDraft::spanSummary).setHeader("SPAN").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    layoutGrid.addItemDoubleClickListener(
        event -> {
          if (!editMode) {
            return;
          }
          WidgetDraft selected = event.getItem();
          openPlacementDialog(selected, widgets.indexOf(selected));
        });

    layoutSection.addToBody(layoutGrid);
  }

  private void apply(DefinitionDashboard definition) {
    this.baseline = definition;
    this.currentRef = StitchDashboardDefinitionRef.of(definition.envelope().group(), definition.envelope().name());
    setPageTitle(Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.title(), definition.envelope().name()));
    setPageSubtitle(Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.description(), "Definition-backed dashboard."));

    groupField.setValue(definition.envelope().group());
    nameField.setValue(definition.envelope().name());
    titleField.setValue(Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.title(), definition.envelope().name()));
    descriptionField.setValue(Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.description(), ""));
    categoryField.setValue(Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.category(), "General"));
    tagsField.setValue(String.join(", ", definition.tags() == null ? List.of() : definition.tags()));
    modeField.setValue(definition.mode() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode.STANDARD : definition.mode());
    visibilityField.setValue(
        definition.visibility() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.GROUP : definition.visibility());
    executionModeField.setValue(
        definition.executionMode() == null
            ? DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED
            : definition.executionMode());
    enabledField.setValue(!Boolean.FALSE.equals(definition.envelope().enabled()));
    layoutColumnsField.setValue(
        definition.layout() == null || definition.layout().columns() == null
            ? 12d
            : definition.layout().columns().doubleValue());
    layoutGapField.setValue(definition.layout() == null ? "" : Strings.firstNonBlank(definition.layout().gap(), ""));
    refreshModeField.setValue(
        definition.refreshPolicy() == null || definition.refreshPolicy().mode() == null
            ? DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode.MANUAL
            : definition.refreshPolicy().mode());
    refreshIntervalField.setValue(
        definition.refreshPolicy() == null || definition.refreshPolicy().intervalSeconds() == null
            ? null
            : definition.refreshPolicy().intervalSeconds().doubleValue());

    filters.clear();
    if (definition.filters() != null) {
      for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter filter : definition.filters()) {
        if (filter != null) {
          filters.add(FilterDraft.from(filter));
        }
      }
    }

    widgets.clear();
    Map<String, PlacementDraft> placements = placementByWidget(definition.layout());
    int order = 1;
    if (definition.widgets() != null) {
      for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget : definition.widgets()) {
        if (widget == null || Strings.trimToNull(widget.id()) == null) {
          continue;
        }
        widgets.add(WidgetDraft.from(widget, placements.get(normalizeKey(widget.id())), order));
        order++;
      }
    }
    normalizeWidgetOrder();
    refreshFilters();
    refreshWidgets();
  }

  private void setEditMode(boolean enabled) {
    this.editMode = enabled;
    editAction.setVisible(!enabled);
    saveAction.setVisible(enabled);
    cancelAction.setVisible(enabled);

    groupField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    nameField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    titleField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    descriptionField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    categoryField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    tagsField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    modeField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    visibilityField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    executionModeField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    enabledField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    layoutColumnsField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    layoutGapField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    refreshModeField.setReadOnly(!enabled);
    refreshIntervalField.setReadOnly(!enabled);

    setEnabled(addFilterAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(editFilterAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(removeFilterAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(addWidgetAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(editWidgetAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(removeWidgetAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(editPlacementAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(placementUpAction, enabled);
    setEnabled(placementDownAction, enabled);
    refreshSummary();
  }

  private void cancel() {
    if (baseline == null) {
      return;
    }
    apply(baseline);
    setEditMode(false);
  }

  private void save() {
    try {
      DefinitionDashboard definition = buildDefinition();
      StitchDashboardDefinitionRef previous = currentRef;
      StitchDashboardDefinitionRef next =
          StitchDashboardDefinitionRef.of(definition.envelope().group(), definition.envelope().name());
      store.save(definition);
      if (previous != null && !previous.key().equals(next.key())) {
        store.delete(previous.group(), previous.name());
      }
      apply(definition);
      setEditMode(false);
      if (savedHandler != null) {
        savedHandler.accept(next);
      }
      toast("Saved dashboard " + next.group() + "/" + next.name(), true);
    } catch (RuntimeException error) {
      toast(Strings.firstNonBlank(error.getMessage(), "Save failed."), false);
    }
  }

  private void openFilterDialog(FilterDraft existing, int index) {
    if (!editMode) {
      return;
    }
    FilterDraft base = existing == null ? FilterDraft.empty() : existing.copy();
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog(existing == null ? "Add Filter" : "Edit Filter");
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("40em", 2));

    TextField id = new TextField("Id");
    id.setRequired(true);
    id.setValue(base.id());
    TextField title = new TextField("Title");
    title.setValue(base.title());
    Select<DefinitionDashboard.FilterType> type = new Select<>();
    type.setLabel("Type");
    type.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.FilterType.values());
    type.setValue(base.type());
    TextField field = new TextField("Field");
    field.setRequired(true);
    field.setValue(base.field());
    Checkbox required = new Checkbox("Required", base.required());
    TextField defaultValue = new TextField("Default Value");
    defaultValue.setValue(base.defaultValue());
    TextField options = new TextField("Options (comma-separated)");
    options.setValue(base.optionsCsv());
    Select<DefinitionDashboard.SourceType> sourceType = new Select<>();
    sourceType.setLabel("Source Type");
    sourceType.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.values());
    sourceType.setValue(base.sourceType());
    TextField sourceRef = new TextField("Source Ref");
    sourceRef.setValue(base.sourceRef());
    TextField sourceValueField = new TextField("Source Value Field");
    sourceValueField.setValue(base.sourceValueField());
    TextField sourceLabelField = new TextField("Source Label Field");
    sourceLabelField.setValue(base.sourceLabelField());

    form.add(id, title, type, field, required, defaultValue, options, sourceType, sourceRef, sourceValueField, sourceLabelField);
    dialog.body().add(form);
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "Save",
        () -> {
          String filterId = Strings.trimToNull(id.getValue());
          String filterField = Strings.trimToNull(field.getValue());
          if (filterId == null || filterField == null) {
            toast("Filter id/field are required.", false);
            return;
          }
          FilterDraft next =
              new FilterDraft(
                  filterId,
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title.getValue()), filterId),
                  type.getValue() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.FilterType.SELECT : type.getValue(),
                  filterField,
                  required.getValue(),
                  Strings.trimToNull(defaultValue.getValue()),
                  parseOptions(options.getValue()),
                  sourceType.getValue(),
                  Strings.trimToNull(sourceRef.getValue()),
                  Strings.trimToNull(sourceValueField.getValue()),
                  Strings.trimToNull(sourceLabelField.getValue()));
          if (index >= 0 && index < filters.size()) {
            filters.set(index, next);
          } else {
            filters.add(next);
          }
          dialog.close();
          refreshFilters();
        });
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void openWidgetDialog(WidgetDraft existing, int index) {
    if (!editMode) {
      return;
    }
    WidgetDraft base = existing == null ? WidgetDraft.empty() : existing.copy();
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog(existing == null ? "Add Widget" : "Edit Widget");
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("42em", 2));

    TextField id = new TextField("Id");
    id.setRequired(true);
    id.setValue(base.id());
    TextField title = new TextField("Title");
    title.setValue(base.title());
    Select<DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType> type = new Select<>();
    type.setLabel("Type");
    type.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.values());
    type.setValue(base.type());
    TextField subtitle = new TextField("Subtitle");
    subtitle.setValue(base.subtitle());
    TextArea description = new TextArea("Description");
    description.setValue(base.description());
    description.getStyle().set("grid-column", "1 / -1");
    TextField filterBindings = new TextField("Filter Bindings (comma-separated)");
    filterBindings.setValue(String.join(", ", base.filterBindings()));

    Select<DefinitionDashboard.SourceType> sourceType = new Select<>();
    sourceType.setLabel("Source Type");
    sourceType.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.values());
    sourceType.setValue(base.sourceType());
    Select<DefinitionDashboard.SourceMode> sourceMode = new Select<>();
    sourceMode.setLabel("Source Mode");
    sourceMode.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.SourceMode.values());
    sourceMode.setValue(base.sourceMode());
    TextField sourceRef = new TextField("Source Ref");
    sourceRef.setValue(base.sourceRef());
    TextField sourceQuery = new TextField("Source Query");
    sourceQuery.setValue(base.sourceQuery());
    TextField sourceStream = new TextField("Source Stream");
    sourceStream.setValue(base.sourceStream());
    NumberField sourceLimit = new NumberField("Source Limit");
    sourceLimit.setMin(1);
    sourceLimit.setStepButtonsVisible(true);
    sourceLimit.setValue(base.sourceLimit() == null ? null : base.sourceLimit().doubleValue());

    Select<DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode> refreshMode = new Select<>();
    refreshMode.setLabel("Refresh");
    refreshMode.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode.values());
    refreshMode.setValue(base.refreshMode());
    NumberField refreshInterval = new NumberField("Refresh Interval");
    refreshInterval.setMin(1);
    refreshInterval.setStepButtonsVisible(true);
    refreshInterval.setValue(base.refreshInterval() == null ? null : base.refreshInterval().doubleValue());

    TextField sectionId = new TextField("Section Id");
    sectionId.setValue(base.sectionId());
    TextField sectionTitle = new TextField("Section Title");
    sectionTitle.setValue(base.sectionTitle());
    NumberField sectionOrder = new NumberField("Section Order");
    sectionOrder.setMin(1);
    sectionOrder.setValue((double) base.sectionOrder());
    NumberField widgetOrder = new NumberField("Widget Order");
    widgetOrder.setMin(1);
    widgetOrder.setValue((double) base.widgetOrder());
    NumberField colSpan = new NumberField("Col Span");
    colSpan.setMin(1);
    colSpan.setValue((double) base.colSpan());
    NumberField rowSpan = new NumberField("Row Span");
    rowSpan.setMin(1);
    rowSpan.setValue((double) base.rowSpan());

    TextField kpiValueField = new TextField("KPI Value Field");
    kpiValueField.setValue(base.kpiValueField());
    TextField tableColumns = new TextField("Table Columns (comma-separated)");
    tableColumns.setValue(base.tableColumnsCsv());
    Select<DefinitionDashboard.ChartType> chartType = new Select<>();
    chartType.setLabel("Chart Type");
    chartType.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.ChartType.values());
    chartType.setValue(base.chartType());
    TextField chartCategoryField = new TextField("Chart Category Field");
    chartCategoryField.setValue(base.chartCategoryField());
    TextField chartValueField = new TextField("Chart Value Field");
    chartValueField.setValue(base.chartValueField());
    Select<DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode> streamMode = new Select<>();
    streamMode.setLabel("Stream Mode");
    streamMode.setItems(DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode.values());
    streamMode.setValue(base.streamMode());
    TextField streamColumns = new TextField("Stream Columns (comma-separated)");
    streamColumns.setValue(base.streamColumnsCsv());

    form.add(
        id, title, type, subtitle, filterBindings, sourceType, sourceMode, sourceRef, sourceQuery, sourceStream,
        sourceLimit, refreshMode, refreshInterval, sectionId, sectionTitle, sectionOrder, widgetOrder, colSpan,
        rowSpan, kpiValueField, tableColumns, chartType, chartCategoryField, chartValueField, streamMode,
        streamColumns, description);
    dialog.body().add(form);
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "Save",
        () -> {
          String widgetId = Strings.trimToNull(id.getValue());
          if (widgetId == null) {
            toast("Widget id is required.", false);
            return;
          }
          WidgetDraft next = base.copy();
          next.id(widgetId);
          next.title(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title.getValue()), widgetId));
          next.type(type.getValue());
          next.subtitle(Strings.trimToNull(subtitle.getValue()));
          next.description(Strings.trimToNull(description.getValue()));
          next.filterBindings(parseCsv(filterBindings.getValue()));
          next.sourceType(sourceType.getValue());
          next.sourceMode(sourceMode.getValue());
          next.sourceRef(Strings.trimToNull(sourceRef.getValue()));
          next.sourceQuery(Strings.trimToNull(sourceQuery.getValue()));
          next.sourceStream(Strings.trimToNull(sourceStream.getValue()));
          next.sourceLimit(intValue(sourceLimit.getValue()));
          next.refreshMode(refreshMode.getValue());
          next.refreshInterval(intValue(refreshInterval.getValue()));
          next.sectionId(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sectionId.getValue()), DEFAULT_SECTION));
          next.sectionTitle(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sectionTitle.getValue()), next.sectionId()));
          next.sectionOrder(intOrDefault(sectionOrder.getValue(), 1));
          next.widgetOrder(intOrDefault(widgetOrder.getValue(), 1));
          next.colSpan(intOrDefault(colSpan.getValue(), 1));
          next.rowSpan(intOrDefault(rowSpan.getValue(), 1));
          next.kpiValueField(Strings.trimToNull(kpiValueField.getValue()));
          next.tableColumns(parseTableColumns(tableColumns.getValue(), next.tableColumns()));
          next.chartType(chartType.getValue());
          next.chartCategoryField(Strings.trimToNull(chartCategoryField.getValue()));
          next.chartValueField(Strings.trimToNull(chartValueField.getValue()));
          next.streamMode(streamMode.getValue());
          next.streamColumns(parseTableColumns(streamColumns.getValue(), next.streamColumns()));
          if (index >= 0 && index < widgets.size()) {
            widgets.set(index, next);
          } else {
            widgets.add(next);
          }
          normalizeWidgetOrder();
          dialog.close();
          refreshWidgets();
        });
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void openPlacementDialog(WidgetDraft existing, int index) {
    if (!editMode || existing == null || index < 0) {
      return;
    }
    WidgetDraft base = existing.copy();
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Edit Placement");
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    NumberField sectionOrder = new NumberField("Section Order");
    sectionOrder.setMin(1);
    sectionOrder.setValue((double) base.sectionOrder());
    NumberField widgetOrder = new NumberField("Widget Order");
    widgetOrder.setMin(1);
    widgetOrder.setValue((double) base.widgetOrder());
    NumberField colSpan = new NumberField("Col Span");
    colSpan.setMin(1);
    colSpan.setValue((double) base.colSpan());
    NumberField rowSpan = new NumberField("Row Span");
    rowSpan.setMin(1);
    rowSpan.setValue((double) base.rowSpan());
    form.add(sectionOrder, widgetOrder, colSpan, rowSpan);
    dialog.body().add(form);
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "Save",
        () -> {
          WidgetDraft next = widgets.get(index);
          next.sectionOrder(intOrDefault(sectionOrder.getValue(), 1));
          next.widgetOrder(intOrDefault(widgetOrder.getValue(), 1));
          next.colSpan(intOrDefault(colSpan.getValue(), 1));
          next.rowSpan(intOrDefault(rowSpan.getValue(), 1));
          normalizeWidgetOrder();
          dialog.close();
          refreshWidgets();
        });
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void movePlacement(int delta) {
    if (!editMode) {
      return;
    }
    WidgetDraft selected = layoutGrid.asSingleSelect().getValue();
    if (selected == null) {
      return;
    }
    List<WidgetDraft> sorted = sortedWidgets();
    int index = sorted.indexOf(selected);
    int next = index + delta;
    if (index < 0 || next < 0 || next >= sorted.size()) {
      return;
    }
    WidgetDraft target = sorted.get(next);
    int selectedOrder = selected.widgetOrder();
    selected.widgetOrder(target.widgetOrder());
    target.widgetOrder(selectedOrder);
    normalizeWidgetOrder();
    refreshWidgets();
  }

  private DefinitionDashboard buildDefinition() {
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(groupField.getValue());
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(nameField.getValue());
    String title = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(titleField.getValue()), name);
    if (group == null || name == null || title == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Group, Name, and Title are required.");
    }

    DefinitionEnvelope previous = baseline == null ? null : baseline.envelope();
    String now = Instant.now().toString();
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            group,
            DefinitionType.DASHBOARD,
            name,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.uuid(), UUID.randomUUID().toString()),
            enabledField.getValue(),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.lifecycleStatus(), "ACTIVE"),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.createdTimeUtc(), now),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previous == null ? null : previous.createdBy(), "stitch"),
            now,
            "stitch");

    List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter> nextFilters = new ArrayList<>();
    for (FilterDraft draft : filters) {
      nextFilters.add(draft.toDefinition());
    }

    List<WidgetDraft> sortedWidgets = sortedWidgets();
    List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget> nextWidgets = new ArrayList<>();
    for (WidgetDraft draft : sortedWidgets) {
      nextWidgets.add(draft.toDefinition());
    }

    DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout layout = buildLayout(sortedWidgets);
    DefinitionDashboard.RefreshPolicy refresh =
        new DefinitionDashboard.RefreshPolicy(
            refreshModeField.getValue() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode.MANUAL : refreshModeField.getValue(),
            intValue(refreshIntervalField.getValue()));

    return new DefinitionDashboard(
        envelope,
        title,
        Strings.trimToNull(descriptionField.getValue()),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(categoryField.getValue()), "General"),
        parseCsv(tagsField.getValue()),
        modeField.getValue() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.DashboardMode.STANDARD : modeField.getValue(),
        visibilityField.getValue() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.DashboardVisibility.GROUP : visibilityField.getValue(),
        executionModeField.getValue() == null
            ? DefinitionDashboard.DashboardExecutionMode.SHARED
            : executionModeField.getValue(),
        layout,
        nextFilters.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(nextFilters),
        nextWidgets.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(nextWidgets),
        refresh,
        baseline == null ? null : baseline.semantic());
  }

  private DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout buildLayout(List<WidgetDraft> sortedWidgets) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, List<WidgetDraft>> bySection = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (WidgetDraft widget : sortedWidgets) {
      String sectionKey = normalizeKey(widget.sectionId());
      if (sectionKey == null) {
        sectionKey = DEFAULT_SECTION;
      }
      bySection.computeIfAbsent(sectionKey, ignored -> new ArrayList<>()).add(widget);
    }
    List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardSection> sections = new ArrayList<>();
    for (List<WidgetDraft> sectionWidgets : bySection.values()) {
      if (sectionWidgets.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      WidgetDraft head = sectionWidgets.getFirst();
      List<DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement> placements = new ArrayList<>();
      for (WidgetDraft widget : sectionWidgets) {
        placements.add(new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement(widget.id(), widget.colSpan(), widget.rowSpan()));
      }
      sections.add(
          new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardSection(
              head.sectionId(),
              head.sectionTitle(),
              12,
              List.copyOf(placements)));
    }
    return new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout(
        intValue(layoutColumnsField.getValue()),
        Strings.trimToNull(layoutGapField.getValue()),
        sections.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(sections));
  }

  private void refreshFilters() {
    filtersGrid.setItems(List.copyOf(filters));
    refreshSummary();
  }

  private void refreshWidgets() {
    List<WidgetDraft> sorted = sortedWidgets();
    widgetsGrid.setItems(sorted);
    layoutGrid.setItems(sorted);
    refreshSummary();
  }

  private void refreshSummary() {
    summary.setItems(
        Map.of(
            "Group", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(groupField.getValue()), "-"),
            "Name", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(nameField.getValue()), "-"),
            "Mode", modeField.getValue() == null ? "-" : modeField.getValue().name(),
            "Filters", String.valueOf(filters.size()),
            "Widgets", String.valueOf(widgets.size()),
            "Edit", editMode ? "ON" : "OFF"));
  }

  private List<WidgetDraft> sortedWidgets() {
    List<WidgetDraft> sorted = new ArrayList<>(widgets);
    sorted.sort(
        (left, right) -> {
          int cmp = Integer.compare(left.sectionOrder(), right.sectionOrder());
          if (cmp != 0) {
            return cmp;
          }
          cmp = Integer.compare(left.widgetOrder(), right.widgetOrder());
          if (cmp != 0) {
            return cmp;
          }
          return left.id().compareToIgnoreCase(right.id());
        });
    return sorted;
  }

  private void normalizeWidgetOrder() {
    List<WidgetDraft> sorted = sortedWidgets();
    int order = 1;
    for (WidgetDraft widget : sorted) {
      widget.widgetOrder(order);
      order++;
    }
  }

  private static Map<String, PlacementDraft> placementByWidget(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardLayout layout) {
    if (layout == null || layout.sections() == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, PlacementDraft> placements = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    int sectionOrder = 1;
    for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardSection section : layout.sections()) {
      int widgetOrder = 1;
      if (section != null && section.placements() != null) {
        for (DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement placement : section.placements()) {
          if (placement == null || Strings.trimToNull(placement.widgetId()) == null) {
            continue;
          }
          placements.put(
              normalizeKey(placement.widgetId()),
              new PlacementDraft(
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(section.id(), DEFAULT_SECTION),
                  Strings.firstNonBlank(section.title(), Strings.firstNonBlank(section.id(), DEFAULT_SECTION)),
                  sectionOrder,
                  widgetOrder,
                  placement.colSpan(),
                  placement.rowSpan()));
          widgetOrder++;
        }
      }
      sectionOrder++;
    }
    return placements.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(placements);
  }

  private static List<String> parseCsv(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> items = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String token : normalized.split(",")) {
      String next = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (next != null) {
        items.add(next);
      }
    }
    return items.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(items);
  }

  private static List<DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption> parseOptions(String value) {
    List<String> values = parseCsv(value);
    if (values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String item : values) {
      options.add(new DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption(item, item));
    }
    return List.copyOf(options);
  }

  private static List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> parseTableColumns(
      String value, List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> fallback) {
    List<String> fields = parseCsv(value);
    if (fields.isEmpty()) {
      return fallback == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(fallback);
    }
    List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> columns = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String field : fields) {
      columns.add(new DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn(field, field, null, true, null));
    }
    return List.copyOf(columns);
  }

  private static Integer intValue(Double value) {
    return value == null ? null : Math.max(1, value.intValue());
  }

  private static int intOrDefault(Double value, int fallback) {
    Integer next = intValue(value);
    return next == null ? fallback : next;
  }

  private static void primary(Button button) {
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
  }

  private static void neutral(Button button) {
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
  }

  private static void setEnabled(Component component, boolean enabled) {
    if (component instanceof com.vaadin.flow.component.HasEnabled target) {
      target.setEnabled(enabled);
    }
  }

  private static void toast(String message, boolean success) {
    Notification notification =
        Notification.show(
            Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), success ? "Saved." : "Failed."),
            3000,
            Notification.Position.BOTTOM_END);
    notification.addThemeVariants(success ? NotificationVariant.LUMO_SUCCESS : NotificationVariant.LUMO_ERROR);
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private record PlacementDraft(
      String sectionId,
      String sectionTitle,
      int sectionOrder,
      int widgetOrder,
      Integer colSpan,
      Integer rowSpan) {}

  private record FilterDraft(
      String id,
      String title,
      DefinitionDashboard.FilterType type,
      String field,
      boolean required,
      String defaultValue,
      List<DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption> options,
      DefinitionDashboard.SourceType sourceType,
      String sourceRef,
      String sourceValueField,
      String sourceLabelField) {
    static FilterDraft from(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter filter) {
      return new FilterDraft(
          filter.id(),
          Strings.firstNonBlank(filter.title(), filter.id()),
          filter.type() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.FilterType.SELECT : filter.type(),
          filter.field(),
          Boolean.TRUE.equals(filter.required()),
          filter.defaultValue(),
          filter.options() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(filter.options()),
          filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().type(),
          filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().ref(),
          filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().valueField(),
          filter.source() == null ? null : filter.source().labelField());
    }

    static FilterDraft empty() {
      String id = "filter_" + UUID.randomUUID().toString().substring(0, 8);
      return new FilterDraft(id, id, DefinitionDashboard.FilterType.SELECT, "field", false, null, List.of(), null, null, null, null);
    }

    FilterDraft copy() {
      return new FilterDraft(id, title, type, field, required, defaultValue, options, sourceType, sourceRef, sourceValueField, sourceLabelField);
    }

    DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter toDefinition() {
      DefinitionDashboard.FilterSource source =
          sourceType == null && sourceRef == null && sourceValueField == null && sourceLabelField == null
              ? null
              : new DefinitionDashboard.FilterSource(sourceType, sourceRef, sourceValueField, sourceLabelField);
      return new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardFilter(
          id, title, type, field, required, null, defaultValue, List.of(), options, source);
    }

    String sourceSummary() {
      if (sourceType == null && Strings.trimToNull(sourceRef) == null) {
        return "";
      }
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(sourceType == null ? null : sourceType.name(), "") + " " + Strings.firstNonBlank(sourceRef, "");
    }

    String optionsCsv() {
      if (options == null || options.isEmpty()) {
        return "";
      }
      List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
      for (DefinitionDashboard.FilterOption option : options) {
        if (option == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String value = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(option.value()), Strings.trimToNull(option.label()));
        if (value != null) {
          values.add(value);
        }
      }
      return values.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(", ", values);
    }
  }

  private static final class WidgetDraft {
    private String id;
    private String title;
    private DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType type;
    private String subtitle;
    private String description;
    private List<String> filterBindings;
    private DefinitionDashboard.SourceType sourceType;
    private DefinitionDashboard.SourceMode sourceMode;
    private String sourceRef;
    private String sourceQuery;
    private String sourceStream;
    private Integer sourceLimit;
    private DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode refreshMode;
    private Integer refreshInterval;
    private String sectionId;
    private String sectionTitle;
    private int sectionOrder;
    private int widgetOrder;
    private int colSpan;
    private int rowSpan;
    private String kpiValueField;
    private List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> tableColumns;
    private DefinitionDashboard.ChartType chartType;
    private String chartCategoryField;
    private String chartValueField;
    private DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode streamMode;
    private List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> streamColumns;

    static WidgetDraft from(DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget widget, PlacementDraft placement, int fallbackOrder) {
      WidgetDraft draft = new WidgetDraft();
      draft.id = widget.id();
      draft.title = Strings.firstNonBlank(widget.title(), widget.id());
      draft.type = widget.type() == null ? DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.TABLE : widget.type();
      draft.subtitle = Strings.trimToNull(widget.subtitle());
      draft.description = Strings.trimToNull(widget.description());
      draft.filterBindings = widget.filterBindings() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(widget.filterBindings());
      draft.sourceType = widget.source() == null ? null : widget.source().type();
      draft.sourceMode = widget.source() == null ? null : widget.source().mode();
      draft.sourceRef = widget.source() == null ? null : widget.source().ref();
      draft.sourceQuery = widget.source() == null ? null : widget.source().query();
      draft.sourceStream = widget.source() == null ? null : widget.source().stream();
      draft.sourceLimit = widget.source() == null ? null : widget.source().limit();
      draft.refreshMode = widget.refreshPolicy() == null ? null : widget.refreshPolicy().mode();
      draft.refreshInterval = widget.refreshPolicy() == null ? null : widget.refreshPolicy().intervalSeconds();
      draft.sectionId = placement == null ? DEFAULT_SECTION : placement.sectionId();
      draft.sectionTitle = placement == null ? "Main" : placement.sectionTitle();
      draft.sectionOrder = placement == null ? fallbackOrder : Math.max(1, placement.sectionOrder());
      draft.widgetOrder = placement == null ? fallbackOrder : Math.max(1, placement.widgetOrder());
      draft.colSpan = Math.max(1, placement == null || placement.colSpan() == null ? 1 : placement.colSpan());
      draft.rowSpan = Math.max(1, placement == null || placement.rowSpan() == null ? 1 : placement.rowSpan());
      draft.kpiValueField = widget.kpi() == null ? null : widget.kpi().valueField();
      draft.tableColumns = widget.table() == null || widget.table().columns() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(widget.table().columns());
      draft.chartType = widget.chart() == null ? null : widget.chart().chartType();
      draft.chartCategoryField = widget.chart() == null ? null : widget.chart().categoryField();
      draft.chartValueField = widget.chart() == null ? null : widget.chart().valueField();
      draft.streamMode = widget.stream() == null ? null : widget.stream().mode();
      draft.streamColumns = widget.stream() == null || widget.stream().columns() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(widget.stream().columns());
      return draft;
    }

    static WidgetDraft empty() {
      WidgetDraft draft = new WidgetDraft();
      String id = "widget_" + UUID.randomUUID().toString().substring(0, 8);
      draft.id = id;
      draft.title = id;
      draft.type = DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.TABLE;
      draft.filterBindings = List.of();
      draft.sourceType = DefinitionDashboard.SourceType.DATASET;
      draft.sourceMode = DefinitionDashboard.SourceMode.SNAPSHOT;
      draft.sectionId = DEFAULT_SECTION;
      draft.sectionTitle = "Main";
      draft.sectionOrder = 1;
      draft.widgetOrder = 1;
      draft.colSpan = 3;
      draft.rowSpan = 1;
      draft.tableColumns = List.of();
      draft.streamColumns = List.of();
      return draft;
    }

    WidgetDraft copy() { WidgetDraft n = new WidgetDraft(); n.id=id; n.title=title; n.type=type; n.subtitle=subtitle; n.description=description; n.filterBindings=filterBindings==null?List.of():List.copyOf(filterBindings); n.sourceType=sourceType; n.sourceMode=sourceMode; n.sourceRef=sourceRef; n.sourceQuery=sourceQuery; n.sourceStream=sourceStream; n.sourceLimit=sourceLimit; n.refreshMode=refreshMode; n.refreshInterval=refreshInterval; n.sectionId=sectionId; n.sectionTitle=sectionTitle; n.sectionOrder=sectionOrder; n.widgetOrder=widgetOrder; n.colSpan=colSpan; n.rowSpan=rowSpan; n.kpiValueField=kpiValueField; n.tableColumns=tableColumns==null?List.of():List.copyOf(tableColumns); n.chartType=chartType; n.chartCategoryField=chartCategoryField; n.chartValueField=chartValueField; n.streamMode=streamMode; n.streamColumns=streamColumns==null?List.of():List.copyOf(streamColumns); return n; }
    DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget toDefinition() { DefinitionDashboard.WidgetSource source = sourceType==null?null:new DefinitionDashboard.WidgetSource(sourceType,sourceMode,sourceRef,sourceQuery,sourceStream,null,null,sourceLimit,Map.of()); DefinitionDashboard.RefreshPolicy refresh = refreshMode==null&&refreshInterval==null?null:new DefinitionDashboard.RefreshPolicy(refreshMode,refreshInterval); DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement layout = new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardPlacement(id,colSpan,rowSpan); DefinitionDashboard.KpiWidget kpi = type==DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.KPI?new DefinitionDashboard.KpiWidget(kpiValueField,null,null,null):null; DefinitionDashboard.TableWidget table = type==DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.TABLE?new DefinitionDashboard.TableWidget(tableColumns==null?List.of():List.copyOf(tableColumns),25,true,true,List.of()):null; DefinitionDashboard.ChartWidget chart = type==DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.CHART?new DefinitionDashboard.ChartWidget(chartType,chartCategoryField,chartValueField,null,true):null; DefinitionDashboard.StreamWidget stream = type==DefinitionDashboard.WidgetType.STREAM?new DefinitionDashboard.StreamWidget(streamMode,500,true,streamColumns==null?List.of():List.copyOf(streamColumns)):null; return new DefinitionDashboard.DashboardWidget(id,title,type,subtitle,description,refresh,filterBindings==null?List.of():List.copyOf(filterBindings),List.of(),null,source,layout,kpi,table,chart,stream,null,null); }
    String id() { return Strings.firstNonBlank(id, ""); } void id(String v) { id = Strings.requireNonBlank(v, "widget.id"); }
    String title() { return Strings.firstNonBlank(title, id()); } void title(String v) { title = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(v), id()); }

    Integer sourceLimit() { return sourceLimit; } void sourceLimit(Integer v) { sourceLimit = v; }
    DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode refreshMode() { return refreshMode==null?DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode.ON_FILTER_CHANGE:refreshMode; } void refreshMode(DefinitionDashboard.RefreshMode v) { refreshMode = v; }
    Integer refreshInterval() { return refreshInterval; } void refreshInterval(Integer v) { refreshInterval = v; }
    String sectionId() { return Strings.firstNonBlank(sectionId, DEFAULT_SECTION); } void sectionId(String v) { sectionId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(v), DEFAULT_SECTION); }

    int widgetOrder() { return Math.max(1, widgetOrder); } void widgetOrder(int v) { widgetOrder = Math.max(1, v); }

    int rowSpan() { return Math.max(1, rowSpan); } void rowSpan(int v) { rowSpan = Math.max(1, v); }
    String kpiValueField() { return Strings.firstNonBlank(kpiValueField, ""); } void kpiValueField(String v) { kpiValueField = Strings.trimToNull(v); }
    List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> tableColumns() { return tableColumns==null?List.of():tableColumns; } void tableColumns(List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> v) { tableColumns = v==null?List.of():List.copyOf(v); }
    String tableColumnsCsv() { List<String> fields = new ArrayList<>(); for (DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn c : tableColumns()) { if (c!=null && Strings.trimToNull(c.field())!=null) fields.add(c.field()); } return fields.isEmpty()?"":String.join(", ", fields); }
    DefinitionDashboard.ChartType chartType() { return chartType; } void chartType(DefinitionDashboard.ChartType v) { chartType = v; }

    String chartValueField() { return Strings.firstNonBlank(chartValueField, ""); } void chartValueField(String v) { chartValueField = Strings.trimToNull(v); }
    DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode streamMode() { return streamMode; } void streamMode(DefinitionDashboard.StreamMode v) { streamMode = v; }
    List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> streamColumns() { return streamColumns==null?List.of():streamColumns; } void streamColumns(List<DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn> v) { streamColumns = v==null?List.of():List.copyOf(v); }
    String streamColumnsCsv() { List<String> fields = new ArrayList<>(); for (DefinitionDashboard.TableColumn c : streamColumns()) { if (c!=null && Strings.trimToNull(c.field())!=null) fields.add(c.field()); } return fields.isEmpty()?"":String.join(", ", fields); }
    String sourceSummary() { return (sourceType==null?"":sourceType.name()) + " " + Strings.firstNonBlank(sourceRef, sourceQuery, sourceStream, ""); }
    String sectionSummary() { return sectionTitle() + " (" + sectionId() + ")"; }
    String orderSummary() { return sectionOrder() + "/" + widgetOrder(); }
    String spanSummary() { return colSpan() + "x" + rowSpan(); }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dashboard/StitchDashboardRegistry.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dashboard;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Registry/discovery layer for dashboard metadata and descriptor access. */
public final class StitchDashboardRegistry {
  private final Map<String, Entry> byId;
  private final List<Entry> entries;

  private StitchDashboardRegistry(Builder builder) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Entry> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Entry entry : builder.entries) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = normalizeKey(entry.id());
      if (key != null && !indexed.containsKey(key)) {
        indexed.put(key, entry);
      }
    }
    this.byId = Map.copyOf(indexed);
    this.entries = List.copyOf(indexed.values());
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public List<Entry> entries() {
    return entries;
  }

  public boolean isEmpty() {
    return entries.isEmpty();
  }

  public Entry entry(String dashboardId) {
    String key = normalizeKey(dashboardId);
    return key == null ? null : byId.get(key);
  }

  public StitchDashboardCatalog toCatalog() {
    List<StitchDashboardDescriptor> descriptors = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Entry entry : entries) {
      if (entry != null && entry.descriptor() != null) {
        descriptors.add(entry.descriptor());
      }
    }
    return StitchDashboardCatalog.of(descriptors);
  }

  public enum SourceType {
    CODE,
    CONFIG
  }

  public record Entry(
      String id,
      String title,
      String description,
      String category,
      List<String> tags,
      String routeKey,
      SourceType sourceType,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor) {
    public Entry {
      id = require(id, "id");
      title = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title), id);
      description = Strings.trimToNull(description);
      category = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(category), "General");
      tags = normalizeTags(tags);
      routeKey = Strings.trimToNull(routeKey);
      sourceType = sourceType == null ? SourceType.CONFIG : sourceType;
      descriptor = Objects.requireNonNull(descriptor, "descriptor");
    }
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final List<Entry> entries = new ArrayList<>();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder register(Entry entry) {
      if (entry != null) {
        entries.add(entry);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder register(
        StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor, SourceType sourceType, String routeKey) {
      if (descriptor == null) {
        return this;
      }
      return register(
          new Entry(
              descriptor.id(),
              descriptor.title(),
              Strings.firstNonBlank(descriptor.subtitle(), descriptor.description()),
              descriptor.category(),
              descriptor.tags(),
              routeKey,
              sourceType,
              descriptor));
    }

    public Builder registerCatalog(StitchDashboardCatalog catalog, SourceType sourceType) {
      return registerCatalog(catalog, sourceType, descriptor -> descriptor == null ? null : descriptor.id());
    }

    public Builder registerCatalog(
        StitchDashboardCatalog catalog,
        SourceType sourceType,
        Function<StitchDashboardDescriptor, String> routeResolver) {
      if (catalog == null || catalog.isEmpty()) {
        return this;
      }
      for (StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor : catalog.dashboards()) {
        if (descriptor == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String routeKey = routeResolver == null ? descriptor.id() : routeResolver.apply(descriptor);
        register(descriptor, sourceType, routeKey);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public StitchDashboardRegistry build() {
      return new StitchDashboardRegistry(this);
    }
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeTags(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> unique = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String item = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (item == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (!unique.containsKey(key)) {
        unique.put(key, item);
      }
    }
    return unique.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(unique.values());
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? null : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

/**
 * Descriptor-driven dashboard runtime screen for Stitch.
 *
 * <p>Phase 2 scope:
 *
 * <ul>
 *   <li>Shared filters
 *   <li>Linked widgets
 *   <li>Drilldowns
 *   <li>Refresh policies
 * </ul>
 */
public class StitchDashboardScreen extends StitchPage {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchDashboardScreen.class);
  private static final String FILTER_ALL = "__all__";
  private static final int INTERVAL_DEFAULT_SECONDS = 15;
  private static final int LIVE_DEFAULT_SECONDS = 2;
  private static final ConcurrentMap<String, DashboardRuntimeState> RUNTIME_STATE =
      new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchDashboardCatalog catalog;
  private final StitchDashboardDataSources dataSources;
  private final StitchDashboardActions actions;
  private final StitchStreamsProvider streamsProvider;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final VerticalLayout advancedPanel = new VerticalLayout();
  private final FormLayout advancedFields = new FormLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout advancedActions = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout rows = new VerticalLayout();
  private final Select<DashboardOption> dashboardSelector = new Select<>();
  private final Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH");
  private final Button clearLinksAction = new Button("CLEAR LINKS");
  private final Button applyAdvancedAction = new Button("APPLY");
  private final Button clearAdvancedAction = new Button("CLEAR");
  private final ScheduledExecutorService scheduler =
      Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(
          runnable -> {
            Thread worker = new Thread(runnable, "stitch-dashboard-refresh");
            worker.setDaemon(true);
            return worker;
          });
  private final List<ScheduledFuture<?>> scheduledRefreshes = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();
  private final Map<String, SharedFilterBinding> sharedFilters = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final Map<String, WidgetController> widgets = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final Map<String, Map<String, String>> linkContextByWidget = new LinkedHashMap<>();

  private StitchDashboardDescriptor dashboard;
  private Map<String, String> dashboardContext = Map.of();
  private Map<String, String> appliedAdvancedFilters = Map.of();
  private Map<String, String> activeSharedFilters = Map.of();
  private DashboardRuntimeState runtimeState = DashboardRuntimeState.empty();
  private Consumer<String> dashboardSelectionListener;
  private BiConsumer<String, Map<String, String>> dashboardNavigationHandler;
