        Div empty = new Div();
        empty.setText(widget.emptyMessage());
        empty.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-widget-empty");
        actionLayout.add(empty);
        return;
      }
      for (StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action action : widgetActions) {
        Button button = createActionButton(action);
        button.addClickListener(event -> runAction(action, Map.of(), button));
        actionLayout.add(button);
      }
    }

    private Button createActionButton(StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action action) {
      Button button = new Button(Strings.firstNonBlank(action.label(), "ACTION"));
      button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
      button.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-action-button");
      button.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-action-tone-" + action.tone().name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      VaadinIcon icon = resolveIcon(action.icon());
      if (icon != null) {
        button.setIcon(icon.create());
      }
      button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", action.label());
      return button;
    }

    private void runAction(
        StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action action, Map<String, String> payload, Button sourceButton) {
      if (action == null) {
        return;
      }
      Runnable invoke = () -> invokeActionNow(action, payload, sourceButton);
      if (action.confirmationRequired()) {
        String message =
            Strings.firstNonBlank(
                action.confirmationMessage(),
                "Run action " + action.label() + "?");
        StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Confirm Action");
        dialog.addToBody(new Paragraph(message));
        dialog.addPrimaryAction(
            "RUN",
            () -> {
              dialog.close();
              invoke.run();
            });
        dialog.addSecondaryAction("CANCEL", dialog::close);
        dialog.open();
      } else {
        invoke.run();
      }
    }

    private void invokeActionNow(
        StitchDashboardDescriptor.Action action, Map<String, String> payload, Button sourceButton) {
      String previousText = null;
      if (sourceButton != null) {
        previousText = sourceButton.getText();
        sourceButton.setEnabled(false);
        sourceButton.setText("RUNNING...");
      }
      try {
        Map<String, String> linked = linkedFilters(widget.id());
        Map<String, String> parameters = resolveActionParameters(action, payload, linked);
        StitchDashboardActionRequest request =
            new StitchDashboardActionRequest(
                runtimeContext,
                dashboard,
                widget,
                action,
                payload,
                activeSharedFilters,
                linked,
                parameters);
        StitchDashboardActionResult result = actions.execute(request);
        if (result.success()) {
          String message = Strings.firstNonBlank(action.successMessage(), result.message(), "Action completed.");
          showActionNotification(message, true);
          if (result.refreshRequested()) {
            refreshAll(RefreshTrigger.MANUAL, true);
          }
        } else {
          String message = Strings.firstNonBlank(action.failureMessage(), result.message(), "Action failed.");
          showActionNotification(message, false);
        }
      } finally {
        if (sourceButton != null) {
          sourceButton.setEnabled(true);
          sourceButton.setText(previousText == null ? action.label() : previousText);
        }
      }
    }

    private void renderTiles(List<Map<String, Object>> rows) {
      tileLayout.removeAll();
      if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
        Div empty = new Div();
        empty.setText(widget.emptyMessage());
        empty.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-widget-empty");
        tileLayout.add(empty);
        return;
      }
      HorizontalLayout tiles = new HorizontalLayout();
      tiles.setPadding(false);
      tiles.setSpacing(false);
      tiles.setWidthFull();
      tiles.getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
      tiles.getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
      tiles.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-kpi-tiles");

      for (Map<String, Object> row : rows) {
        String label = resolveTileValue(row, widget.labelField(), "label", "name", "key");
        String value = resolveTileValue(row, widget.valueField(), "value", "count", "total");
        String tone = resolveTileValue(row, widget.toneField(), "tone", "status");

        Button tile = new Button();
        tile.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
        tile.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-kpi-tile");
        if (Strings.trimToNull(tone) != null) {
          tile.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-kpi-tone-" + tone.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
        }
        tile.setText("");
        VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout();
        content.setPadding(false);
        content.setSpacing(false);
        content.getStyle().set("gap", "0.1rem");
        content.setAlignItems(Alignment.START);
        content.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-kpi-content");

        Span labelSpan = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(label), "Item"));
        labelSpan.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-kpi-label");
        Span valueSpan = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "0"));
        valueSpan.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-kpi-value");
        content.add(labelSpan, valueSpan);

        tile.getElement().appendChild(content.getElement());
        tile.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", labelSpan.getText() + " " + valueSpan.getText());
        tile.addClickListener(
            event -> {
              Map<String, String> payload = payloadFromRow(widget, row);
              handleWidgetEvent(this, StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.TILE_CLICKED, payload);
              handleWidgetEvent(this, StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ITEM_SELECTED, payload);
            });
        tiles.add(tile);
      }

      tileLayout.add(tiles);
    }

    private void renderBars(List<Map<String, Object>> rows) {
      chartLayout.removeAll();
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType chartType =
          widget.chartType() == null ? StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType.BAR : widget.chartType();
      if (chartType != StitchDashboardDescriptor.ChartType.BAR) {
        String message =
            "Unsupported chartType '" + chartType + "' for widget '" + widget.id() + "'.";
        LOGGER.warn("[StitchDashboard] {}", message);
        Div unsupported = new Div();
        unsupported.setText(message);
        unsupported.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-widget-empty");
        chartLayout.add(unsupported);
        return;
      }
      if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
        Div empty = new Div();
        empty.setText(widget.emptyMessage());
        empty.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-widget-empty");
        chartLayout.add(empty);
        return;
      }

      long maxValue = 0L;
      for (Map<String, Object> row : rows) {
        String value = resolveTileValue(row, widget.valueField(), "value", "count", "total");
        long numeric = parseLong(value);
        if (numeric > maxValue) {
          maxValue = numeric;
        }
      }
      long safeMax = maxValue <= 0 ? 1 : maxValue;

      for (Map<String, Object> row : rows) {
        String label = resolveTileValue(row, widget.labelField(), "label", "status", "key");
        String value = resolveTileValue(row, widget.valueField(), "value", "count", "total");
        String tone = resolveTileValue(row, widget.toneField(), "tone", "status");
        long numeric = parseLong(value);
        int widthPercent = (int) Math.max(4, Math.min(100, Math.round((numeric * 100.0) / safeMax)));

        Button bar = new Button();
        bar.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE);
        bar.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-bar");
        if (Strings.trimToNull(tone) != null) {
          bar.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-tone-" + tone.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
        }
        bar.getElement().setAttribute(
            "aria-label",
            Strings.firstNonBlank(label, "Item")
                + " "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(value, "0"));

        Div rowLayout = new Div();
        rowLayout.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-row");

        Span labelSpan = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(label, "Item"));
        labelSpan.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-label");
        Span valueSpan = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(value, "0"));
        valueSpan.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-value");

        Div track = new Div();
        track.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-track");
        Div fill = new Div();
        fill.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-chart-fill");
        fill.getStyle().set("width", widthPercent + "%");
        track.add(fill);

        rowLayout.add(labelSpan, valueSpan, track);
        bar.getElement().appendChild(rowLayout.getElement());
        if (!Boolean.FALSE.equals(widget.chartClickable())) {
          bar.addClickListener(
              event -> {
                Map<String, String> payload = payloadFromRow(widget, row);
                handleWidgetEvent(this, StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.POINT_CLICKED, payload);
                handleWidgetEvent(this, StitchDashboardDescriptor.EventType.ITEM_SELECTED, payload);
              });
        }
        chartLayout.add(bar);
      }
    }

    private String resolveTileValue(
        Map<String, Object> row, String preferredField, String... fallbacks) {
      if (row == null || row.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      String preferred = Strings.trimToNull(preferredField);
      if (preferred != null) {
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(String.valueOf(row.get(preferred)));
        if (value != null) {
          return value;
        }
      }
      if (fallbacks != null) {
        for (String fallback : fallbacks) {
          String key = Strings.trimToNull(fallback);
          if (key == null) {
            continue;
          }
          String value = Strings.trimToNull(String.valueOf(row.get(key)));
          if (value != null) {
            return value;
          }
        }
      }
      return null;
    }

    private static long parseLong(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return 0L;
      }
      try {
        return Long.parseLong(normalized);
      } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
        return 0L;
      }
    }
  }

  private enum LiveStreamRenderMode {
    EVENT,
    TABLE,
    KPI
  }

  private static boolean isStreamActive(StitchRealtimeConnectionState state) {
    return state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED
        || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING
        || state == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE;
  }

  private static void safeClose(AutoCloseable handle) {
    if (handle == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      handle.close();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  private Map<String, String> resolveWidgetParameters(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget,
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source,
      Map<String, String> linked) {
    return StitchDashboardDataSources.resolveParameters(
        dashboard, widget, source, activeSharedFilters, linked);
  }

  private static String resolveStreamId(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Source source, Map<String, String> parameters) {
    if (parameters != null && !parameters.isEmpty()) {
      String value =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(parameters.get("streamId")),
              Strings.trimToNull(parameters.get("stream")),
              Strings.trimToNull(parameters.get("ref")));
      if (value != null) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    return source == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(source.resourceId());
  }

  private static int intParameter(
      Map<String, String> parameters, int fallback, String... keys) {
    if (parameters == null || parameters.isEmpty() || keys == null || keys.length == 0) {
      return Math.max(1, fallback);
    }
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(parameters.get(key));
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      try {
        return Math.max(1, Integer.parseInt(value));
      } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
        // continue
      }
    }
    return Math.max(1, fallback);
  }

  private static boolean boolParameter(
      Map<String, String> parameters, boolean fallback, String... keys) {
    if (parameters == null || parameters.isEmpty() || keys == null || keys.length == 0) {
      return fallback;
    }
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(parameters.get(key));
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(value) || "1".equals(value)) {
        return true;
      }
      if ("false".equalsIgnoreCase(value) || "0".equals(value)) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return fallback;
  }

  private List<Map<String, Object>> loadRowsForWidget(String widgetId) {
    if (dashboard == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget = dashboard.widget(widgetId);
    if (widget == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, String> linked = linkedFilters(widget.id());
    return dataSources.query(dashboard, widget, activeSharedFilters, linked);
  }

  private Map<String, String> linkedFilters(String widgetId) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> merged = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (dashboardContext != null && !dashboardContext.isEmpty()) {
      merged.putAll(dashboardContext);
    }
    if (widgetId != null) {
      Map<String, String> byWidget = linkContextByWidget.get(widgetId);
      if (byWidget != null && !byWidget.isEmpty()) {
        merged.putAll(byWidget);
      }
    }
    return merged.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(merged);
  }

  private DashboardRuntimeState resolveRuntimeState(StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor) {
    String key = runtimeStateKey(descriptor);
    if (key == null) {
      return DashboardRuntimeState.empty();
    }
    return RUNTIME_STATE.getOrDefault(key, DashboardRuntimeState.empty());
  }

  private void persistRuntimeState() {
    if (dashboard == null) {
      return;
    }
    String key = runtimeStateKey(dashboard);
    if (key == null) {
      return;
    }
    DashboardRuntimeState snapshot =
        new DashboardRuntimeState(
            collectFilterValues(false),
            collectFilterValues(true),
            copyLinkContext(linkContextByWidget));
    runtimeState = snapshot;
    RUNTIME_STATE.put(key, snapshot);
  }

  private static String runtimeStateKey(StitchDashboardDescriptor descriptor) {
    if (descriptor == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String dashboardId = normalizeKey(descriptor.id());
    if (dashboardId == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (descriptor.executionMode() == StitchDashboardDescriptor.DashboardExecutionMode.PER_USER) {
      String subject = normalizeKey(StitchIdentityContext.currentSubject());
      return dashboardId + "|user|" + Strings.firstNonBlank(subject, "anonymous");
    }
    return dashboardId + "|shared";
  }

  private static Map<String, Map<String, String>> copyLinkContext(
      Map<String, Map<String, String>> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, Map<String, String>> copied = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Map<String, String>> entry : source.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String widgetId = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      Map<String, String> context = normalizeMap(entry.getValue());
      if (widgetId != null && !context.isEmpty()) {
        copied.put(widgetId, context);
      }
    }
    return copied.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(copied);
  }

  private StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy resolvePolicy(
      StitchDashboardDescriptor.Widget widget) {
    StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy widgetPolicy = widget.refreshPolicy();
    if (widgetPolicy != null) {
      return widgetPolicy;
    }
    if (dashboard != null && dashboard.refreshPolicy() != null) {
      return dashboard.refreshPolicy();
    }
    return StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy.defaultPolicy();
  }

  private static boolean shouldRefresh(
      RefreshTrigger trigger, StitchDashboardDescriptor.RefreshPolicy policy) {
    if (policy == null || policy.mode() == null) {
      return trigger == RefreshTrigger.MANUAL || trigger == RefreshTrigger.FILTER_CHANGE;
    }
    return switch (policy.mode()) {
      case MANUAL -> trigger == RefreshTrigger.MANUAL;
      case ON_FILTER_CHANGE -> trigger == RefreshTrigger.MANUAL || trigger == RefreshTrigger.FILTER_CHANGE;
      case ON_LINK_EVENT ->
          trigger == RefreshTrigger.MANUAL
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.LINK_EVENT
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.FILTER_CHANGE;
      case INTERVAL ->
          trigger == RefreshTrigger.MANUAL
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.INTERVAL
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.FILTER_CHANGE
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.LINK_EVENT;
      case LIVE ->
          trigger == RefreshTrigger.MANUAL
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.LIVE
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.FILTER_CHANGE
              || trigger == RefreshTrigger.LINK_EVENT;
    };
  }

  private interface DashboardFilterField {
    Component component();

    Map<String, String> valueMap();

    Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context);

    void clear();

    Registration onChange(Runnable callback);
  }

  private static final class SelectFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {
    private final String key;
    private final Select<String> field = new Select<>();

    private SelectFilterField(
        String key, String label, List<String> options, String defaultValue) {
      this.key = Objects.requireNonNull(key, "key");
      field.setWidth("12.5rem");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter-select");
      field.setAriaLabel(label);

      List<String> entries = new ArrayList<>();
      entries.add(FILTER_ALL);
      if (options != null) {
        for (String option : options) {
          String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(option);
          if (normalized != null && !FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
            entries.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      field.setItems(entries);
      field.setItemLabelGenerator(value -> FILTER_ALL.equals(value) ? "All" : value);
      String candidate = Strings.trimToNull(defaultValue);
      field.setValue(candidate == null ? FILTER_ALL : candidate);
      if (!entries.contains(field.getValue())) {
        field.setValue(FILTER_ALL);
      }
    }

    @Override
    public Component component() {
      return field;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> valueMap() {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(field.getValue());
      if (value == null || FILTER_ALL.equalsIgnoreCase(value)) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      return Map.of(key, value);
    }

    @Override
    public Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context) {
      if (context == null || context.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      String value = context.get(key);
      if (Strings.trimToNull(value) == null) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      List<String> items = field.getListDataView().getItems().toList();
      for (String item : items) {
        if (item != null && item.equalsIgnoreCase(value.trim())) {
          field.setValue(item);
          return Set.of(normalizeKey(key));
        }
      }
      return Set.of();
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
      field.setValue(FILTER_ALL);
    }

    @Override
    public Registration onChange(Runnable callback) {
      return field.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
    }
  }

  private static final class MultiSelectFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {
    private final String key;
    private final MultiSelectComboBox<String> field = new MultiSelectComboBox<>();

    private MultiSelectFilterField(
        String key, String label, List<String> options, List<String> defaultValues) {
      this.key = Objects.requireNonNull(key, "key");
      field.setWidth("14rem");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter-multi");
      field.setLabel("");
      field.setPlaceholder(label);
      field.setItems(options == null ? List.of() : options);
      if (defaultValues != null && !defaultValues.isEmpty()) {
        LinkedHashSet<String> selected = new LinkedHashSet<>();
        for (String value : defaultValues) {
          String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
          if (normalized != null) {
            selected.add(normalized);
          }
        }
        field.setValue(selected);
      }
    }

    @Override
    public Component component() {
      return field;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> valueMap() {
      if (field.getValue() == null || field.getValue().isEmpty()) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      List<String> values = new ArrayList<>(field.getValue());
      values.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
      return Map.of(key, String.join("|", values));
    }

    @Override
    public Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context) {
      if (context == null || context.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      String raw = Strings.trimToNull(context.get(key));
      if (raw == null) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      String[] parts = raw.split("\\|");
      LinkedHashSet<String> selected = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String part : parts) {
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(part);
        if (value != null) {
          selected.add(value);
        }
      }
      if (selected.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      field.setValue(selected);
      return Set.of(normalizeKey(key));
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
      field.clear();
    }

    @Override
    public Registration onChange(Runnable callback) {
      return field.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
    }
  }

  private static final class TextFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {

    @Override

  private static final class ToggleFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {

      field.setLabel(label);
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter-toggle");
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(defaultValue);
      if (normalized != null) {
        field.setValue("true".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized) || "1".equals(normalized));
      }
    }

    @Override
    public Component component() {
      return field;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> valueMap() {
      return field.getValue() ? Map.of(key, "true") : Map.of();
    }

    @Override
    public Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context) {
      if (context == null || context.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(context.get(key));
      if (value == null) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      field.setValue("true".equalsIgnoreCase(value) || "1".equals(value));
      return Set.of(normalizeKey(key));
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
      field.setValue(false);
    }

    @Override
    public Registration onChange(Runnable callback) {
      return field.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
    }
  }

  private static final class NumberFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {
    private final String key;
    private final NumberField field = new NumberField();

    private NumberFilterField(String key, String label, String defaultValue) {
      this.key = Objects.requireNonNull(key, "key");
      field.setWidth("10rem");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter");
      field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter-number");
      field.setLabel("");
      field.setPlaceholder(label);
      field.setStep(1.0d);
      field.setMin(0.0d);
      field.setClearButtonVisible(true);
      field.setValueChangeMode(ValueChangeMode.LAZY);
      field.setValueChangeTimeout(350);
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(defaultValue);
      if (normalized != null) {
        try {
          field.setValue(Double.parseDouble(normalized));
        } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
          field.clear();
        }
      }
    }

    @Override
    public Component component() {
      return field;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> valueMap() {
      Double value = field.getValue();
      if (value == null) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      if (Math.floor(value) == value) {
        return Map.of(key, String.valueOf(value.longValue()));
      }
      return Map.of(key, String.valueOf(value));
    }

    @Override
    public Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context) {
      if (context == null || context.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(context.get(key));
      if (value == null) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      try {
        field.setValue(Double.parseDouble(value));
        return Set.of(normalizeKey(key));
      } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
        return Set.of();
      }
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
      field.clear();
    }

    @Override
    public Registration onChange(Runnable callback) {
      return field.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
    }
  }

  private static final class DateFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {

  private static final class DateTimeRangeFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {
    private final String keyFrom;
    private final String keyTo;
    private final HorizontalLayout layout = new HorizontalLayout();
    private final DateTimePicker from = new DateTimePicker();
    private final DateTimePicker to = new DateTimePicker();

    private DateTimeRangeFilterField(String key, String label) {
      this.keyFrom = key + "_from";
      this.keyTo = key + "_to";
      layout.setPadding(false);
      layout.setSpacing(false);
      layout.setWidthFull();
      layout.getStyle().set("gap", "0.4rem");
      layout.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter");
      layout.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter-datetime-range");

      from.setLabel(label + " from");
      from.setStep(java.time.Duration.ofMinutes(1));
      from.setWidth("15rem");

      to.setLabel(label + " to");
      to.setStep(java.time.Duration.ofMinutes(1));
      to.setWidth("15rem");

      layout.add(from, to);
      layout.setFlexGrow(1.0, from);
      layout.setFlexGrow(1.0, to);
    }

    @Override
    public Component component() {
      return layout;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> valueMap() {
      LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      if (from.getValue() != null) {
        values.put(keyFrom, from.getValue().toString());
      }
      if (to.getValue() != null) {
        values.put(keyTo, to.getValue().toString());
      }
      return values.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(values);
    }

    @Override
    public Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context) {
      if (context == null || context.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      Set<String> consumed = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      LocalDateTime fromValue = parseDateTime(context.get(keyFrom));
      if (fromValue != null) {
        from.setValue(fromValue);
        consumed.add(normalizeKey(keyFrom));
      }
      LocalDateTime toValue = parseDateTime(context.get(keyTo));
      if (toValue != null) {
        to.setValue(toValue);
        consumed.add(normalizeKey(keyTo));
      }
      return consumed.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(consumed);
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
      from.clear();
      to.clear();
    }

    @Override
    public Registration onChange(Runnable callback) {
      Registration left = from.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
      Registration right = to.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
      return () -> {
        left.remove();
        right.remove();
      };
    }
  }

  private static final class GroupFilterField implements DashboardFilterField {
    private final String key;
    private final StitchGroupFilter field;

    private GroupFilterField(String key, StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, String defaultValue) {
      this.key = Objects.requireNonNull(key, "key");
      this.field = new StitchGroupFilter(runtimeContext);
      this.field.setWidth("13rem");
      this.field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter");
      this.field.addClassName("stitch-dashboard-filter-group");
      applyDefault(defaultValue);
    }

    @Override
    public Component component() {
      return field;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> valueMap() {
      String selected = Strings.trimToNull(field.selectedGroup());
      return selected == null ? Map.of() : Map.of(key, selected);
    }

    @Override
    public Set<String> applyContext(Map<String, String> context) {
      if (context == null || context.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      String requested = Strings.trimToNull(context.get(key));
      if (requested == null) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      StitchGroupFilter.Option selected = null;
      for (StitchGroupFilter.Option option : field.getListDataView().getItems().toList()) {
        if (option != null && requested.equalsIgnoreCase(option.key())) {
          selected = option;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (selected == null) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      field.setValue(selected);
      return Set.of(normalizeKey(key));
    }

    @Override
    public void clear() {
      field.clear();
    }

    @Override
    public Registration onChange(Runnable callback) {
      return field.addValueChangeListener(event -> callback.run());
    }

    private void applyDefault(String defaultValue) {
      String requested = Strings.trimToNull(defaultValue);
      if (requested == null) {
        return;
      }
      for (StitchGroupFilter.Option option : field.getListDataView().getItems().toList()) {
        if (option != null && requested.equalsIgnoreCase(option.key())) {
          field.setValue(option);
          return;
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static LocalDate parseDate(String value) {
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (text == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return LocalDate.parse(text);
    } catch (DateTimeParseException ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static LocalTime parseTime(String value) {
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (text == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return LocalTime.parse(text);
    } catch (DateTimeParseException ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static LocalDateTime parseDateTime(String value) {
    String text = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (text == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return LocalDateTime.parse(text);
    } catch (DateTimeParseException ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  public QueryParameters toDashboardQueryParameters(String dashboardId, Map<String, String> context) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> query = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    String target = Strings.trimToNull(dashboardId);
    if (target != null) {
      query.put("dashboard", target);
    }
    if (context != null) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : context.entrySet()) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
        if (key != null && value != null) {
          query.put("ctx_" + key, value);
        }
      }
    }
    return query.isEmpty() ? QueryParameters.empty() : QueryParameters.simple(query);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.dialog.Dialog;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchDialog extends Dialog {
  private final Span headerTitle = new Span();
  private final HorizontalLayout header = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout headerActions = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final Button jsonAction = new Button("JSON");
  private final Button closeAction = new Button("CLOSE");
  private final VerticalLayout body = new VerticalLayout();
  private final boolean jsonEnabled;
  private Runnable secondaryAction = this::close;
  private Supplier<Object> jsonPayloadSupplier;

  public StitchDialog(String title) {
    this(title, true);
  }

  protected StitchDialog(String title, boolean withJsonAction) {
    addClassName("stitch-dialog");
    getElement().getThemeList().add("stitch-dialog");
    setWidth("560px");
    setMaxWidth("92vw");
    setTop("10vh");
    setCloseOnEsc(true);
    setCloseOnOutsideClick(false);

    headerTitle.setText(title == null ? "" : title.trim());
    headerTitle.addClassName("stitch-dialog-title");

    header.setPadding(false);
    header.setSpacing(false);
    header.setWidthFull();
    header.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(FlexComponent.Alignment.CENTER);
    header.addClassName("stitch-dialog-header");

    headerActions.setPadding(false);
    headerActions.setSpacing(true);
    headerActions.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(FlexComponent.Alignment.CENTER);
    headerActions.addClassName("stitch-dialog-header-actions");
    headerActions.addClassName("stitch-dialog-actions");

    this.jsonEnabled = withJsonAction;
    if (jsonEnabled) {
      configureActionButton(jsonAction, "Open raw JSON", false);
      jsonAction.addClassName("stitch-dialog-primary-action");
      jsonAction.addClassName("stitch-dialog-json-action");
      jsonAction.addClassName("stitch-btn-secondary");
      StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(jsonAction);
      jsonAction.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Open raw JSON");
      jsonAction.addClickListener(
          event -> {
            Object payload = jsonPayloadSupplier == null ? defaultJsonPayload() : jsonPayloadSupplier.get();
            new StitchJsonDialog("Raw JSON - " + headerTitle.getText(), payload).open();
          });
    }

    closeAction.addClassName("stitch-dialog-close-action");
    closeAction.addClassName("stitch-btn-tertiary");
    configureActionButton(closeAction, "Close dialog", false);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(closeAction);
    closeAction.addClickListener(event -> run(secondaryAction));

    Div spacer = new Div();
    header.add(headerTitle, spacer, headerActions);
    header.expand(spacer);
    if (jsonEnabled) {
      headerActions.add(jsonAction);
    }
    headerActions.add(closeAction);

    body.setPadding(false);
    body.setSpacing(true);
    body.setWidthFull();
    body.addClassName("stitch-dialog-body");

    StitchComponents.withCode(header, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_HEADER);
    StitchComponents.withCode(body, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_BODY);
    if (jsonEnabled) {
      StitchComponents.withCode(jsonAction, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_JSON_ACTION);
    }
    StitchComponents.withCode(closeAction, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_SECONDARY_ACTION);

    getHeader().add(header);
    add(body);
  }

  public StitchDialog setDialogTitle(String value) {
    headerTitle.setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDialog addToBody(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      body.add(components);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDialog addPrimaryAction(String label, Runnable action) {
    String resolvedLabel = label == null || label.isBlank() ? "OK" : label.trim();
    Button button = new Button(resolvedLabel);
    configureActionButton(button, resolvedLabel, false);
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-primary-action");
    button.addClassName("stitch-btn-primary");
    StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, resolvedLabel);
    StitchComponents.withCode(button, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_PRIMARY_ACTION);
    button.addClickListener(event -> run(action));
    int insertIndex =
        jsonEnabled ? Math.max(0, headerActions.indexOf(jsonAction)) : Math.max(0, headerActions.getComponentCount() - 1);
    headerActions.addComponentAtIndex(insertIndex, button);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDialog addSecondaryAction(String label, Runnable action) {
    String resolvedLabel = label == null || label.isBlank() ? "CLOSE" : label.trim().toUpperCase();
    closeAction.setText(resolvedLabel);
    secondaryAction = action == null ? this::close : action;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDialog withJsonPayload(Object payload) {
    this.jsonPayloadSupplier = () -> payload;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchDialog withJsonPayloadSupplier(Supplier<Object> supplier) {
    this.jsonPayloadSupplier = supplier;
    return this;
  }

  public VerticalLayout body() {
    return body;
  }

  public HorizontalLayout footer() {
    return headerActions;
  }

  private static void run(Runnable action) {
    Runnable safeAction = Objects.requireNonNullElse(action, () -> {});
    safeAction.run();
  }

  private Object defaultJsonPayload() {
    return java.util.Map.of("title", headerTitle.getText());
  }

  private static void configureActionButton(Button button, String ariaLabel, boolean primary) {
    if (button == null) {
      return;
    }
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-action-button");
    button.addClassName("stitch-btn");
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    if (primary) {
      button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    } else {
      button.removeThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    }
    if (ariaLabel != null && !ariaLabel.isBlank()) {
      button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel.trim());
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dialog/StitchJsonDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.JsonProcessingException;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Pre;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/** Shared JSON inspection dialog for Stitch info/details workflows. */
public class StitchJsonDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      new ObjectMapper()
          .registerModule(new JavaTimeModule())
          .disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS)
          .enable(SerializationFeature.INDENT_OUTPUT);

  private final String renderedJson;

  public StitchJsonDialog(String title, Object rawValue) {
    super(title == null || title.isBlank() ? "Raw JSON" : title.trim(), false);
    setWidth("820px");
    setMaxWidth("95vw");
    setTop("8vh");
    body().setWidthFull();

    renderedJson = prettyJson(rawValue);
    Pre content = new Pre(renderedJson);
    content.addClassName("stitch-json-dialog-content");
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Raw JSON content");
    StitchComponents.withCode(content, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_JSON_CONTENT);
    addToBody(content);
    addPrimaryAction("COPY", this::copyJsonToClipboard);
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }

  private static String prettyJson(Object rawValue) {
    Object safeValue = rawValue == null ? Map.of() : rawValue;
    try {
      return MAPPER.writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(safeValue);
    } catch (JsonProcessingException ignored) {
      Map<String, Object> fallback = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      fallback.put("value", String.valueOf(safeValue));
      try {
        return MAPPER.writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(fallback);
      } catch (JsonProcessingException nested) {
        return "{\"value\":\"" + escapeJson(String.valueOf(safeValue)) + "\"}";
      }
    }
  }

  private static String escapeJson(String value) {
    return value.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace("\"", "\\\"");
  }

  private void copyJsonToClipboard() {
    getUI()
        .ifPresent(
            ui ->
                ui.getPage()
                    .executeJs(
                        """
                        const text = $0;
                        const fallbackCopy = (value) => {
                          const area = document.createElement('textarea');
                          area.value = value;
                          area.style.position = 'fixed';
                          area.style.left = '-9999px';
                          document.body.appendChild(area);
                          area.focus();
                          area.select();
                          try { document.execCommand('copy'); } finally { document.body.removeChild(area); }
                        };
                        if (navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext) {
                          navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).catch(() => fallbackCopy(text));
                        } else {
                          fallbackCopy(text);
                        }
                        """,
                        renderedJson));
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/dialog/StitchJsonDiffDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchJsonDiffPanel;

/** Shared StitchDialog wrapper for JSON payload comparison. */
public final class StitchJsonDiffDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchJsonDiffPanel panel = new StitchJsonDiffPanel();
  private String leftLabel = "Left";
  private String rightLabel = "Right";
  private JsonNode leftPayload;
  private JsonNode rightPayload;

  public StitchJsonDiffDialog(
      String title,
      String leftLabel,
      JsonNode leftPayload,
      String rightLabel,
      JsonNode rightPayload) {
    super(title == null || title.isBlank() ? "JSON Compare" : title.trim());
    setWidth("1200px");
    setMaxWidth("98vw");
    setTop("6vh");
    body().setWidthFull();
    body().setPadding(false);
    body().setSpacing(false);
    addToBody(panel);
    setComparison(leftLabel, leftPayload, rightLabel, rightPayload);
    withJsonPayloadSupplier(this::jsonPayload);
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }

  public StitchJsonDiffDialog setComparison(
      String leftLabel, JsonNode leftPayload, String rightLabel, JsonNode rightPayload) {
    this.leftLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(leftLabel), "Left");
    this.rightLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(rightLabel), "Right");
    this.leftPayload = leftPayload;
    this.rightPayload = rightPayload;
    panel.setComparison(this.leftLabel, this.leftPayload, this.rightLabel, this.rightPayload);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchJsonDiffPanel panel() {
    return panel;
  }

  private Map<String, Object> jsonPayload() {
    Map<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("leftLabel", leftLabel);
    payload.put("rightLabel", rightLabel);
    payload.put("leftPayload", leftPayload);
    payload.put("rightPayload", rightPayload);
    payload.put("diffRows", panel.rows());
    payload.put("changedCount", panel.rows().size());
    return payload;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Paragraph;
import java.util.Objects;

/** Shared unsaved-changes guard dialog for editor workflows. */
public final class StitchUnsavedChangesDialog extends StitchDialog {
  public StitchUnsavedChangesDialog(
      String message, Runnable onSave, Runnable onDiscard, Runnable onCancel) {
    super("Unsaved Changes", false);
    addToBody(
        new Paragraph(
            message == null || message.isBlank()
                ? "Save, discard, or cancel before continuing."
                : message.trim()));
    addPrimaryAction(
        "SAVE",
        () -> {
          runAction(onSave);
          close();
        });
    addPrimaryAction(
        "DISCARD",
        () -> {
          runAction(onDiscard);
          close();
        });
    addSecondaryAction(
        "CANCEL",
        () -> {
          runAction(onCancel);
          close();
        });
  }

  public static StitchUnsavedChangesDialog open(
      String message, Runnable onSave, Runnable onDiscard, Runnable onCancel) {
    StitchUnsavedChangesDialog dialog =
        new StitchUnsavedChangesDialog(message, onSave, onDiscard, onCancel);
    dialog.open();
    return dialog;
  }

  private static void runAction(Runnable action) {
    Runnable safeAction = Objects.requireNonNullElse(action, () -> {});
    safeAction.run();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/StitchFeatureRegistry.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuContributionRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchFeatureRegistry {
  private final List<StitchFeatureSet> features;
  private final StitchMenuContributionRegistry menuContributions;

  public StitchFeatureRegistry(List<? extends StitchFeatureSet> featureSets) {
    List<StitchFeatureSet> sorted = new ArrayList<>();
    if (featureSets != null) {
      for (StitchFeatureSet feature : featureSets) {
        if (feature != null) {
          sorted.add(feature);
        }
      }
    }
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(StitchFeatureSet::order)
            .thenComparing(feature -> feature.id().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    this.features = List.copyOf(sorted);
    this.menuContributions = new StitchMenuContributionRegistry(collectMenuEntries(this.features));
  }

  public List<StitchFeatureSet> featureSets() {
    return features;
  }

  public StitchMenuContributionRegistry menuContributions() {
    return menuContributions;
  }

  public <T extends StitchFeatureSet> Optional<T> feature(Class<T> type) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(type, "type");
    for (StitchFeatureSet feature : features) {
      if (type.isInstance(feature)) {
        return Optional.of(type.cast(feature));
      }
    }
    return Optional.empty();
  }

  private static List<StitchMenuEntry> collectMenuEntries(List<StitchFeatureSet> features) {
    List<StitchMenuEntry> entries = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchFeatureSet feature : features) {
      List<StitchMenuEntry> contributed = feature.menuEntries();
      if (contributed == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (StitchMenuEntry entry : contributed) {
        if (entry != null) {
          entries.add(entry);
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(entries);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/StitchFeatures.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents.StitchAgentsFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets.StitchAssetsFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.audit.StitchAuditFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.catalog.StitchCatalogFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.configs.StitchConfigsFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data.StitchDataFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.discovery.StitchDiscoveryFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.docs.StitchDocsFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.entitlements.StitchEntitlementsFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform.StitchPlatformFeature;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status.StitchStatusFeature;

public final class StitchFeatures {
  private final StitchFeatureRegistry registry;
  private final StitchStatusFeature status;
  private final StitchAssetsFeature assets;
  private final StitchPlatformFeature platform;
  private final StitchDiscoveryFeature discovery;
  private final StitchDataFeature data;
  private final StitchConfigsFeature configs;
  private final StitchAuditFeature audit;
  private final StitchEntitlementsFeature entitlements;
  private final StitchDocsFeature docs;
  private final StitchCatalogFeature catalog;
  private final StitchAgentsFeature agents;

  private StitchFeatures(Builder builder, Set<String> activatedFeatures) {
    Set<String> active = activatedFeatures == null ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(activatedFeatures);
    List<StitchFeatureSet> featureSets = new ArrayList<>();

    if (active.contains(StitchStatusFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.status = builder.buildStatus();
      featureSets.add(status);
    } else {
      this.status = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchAssetsFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.assets = builder.buildAssets();
      featureSets.add(assets);
    } else {
      this.assets = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchPlatformFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.platform = builder.buildPlatform();
      featureSets.add(platform);
    } else {
      this.platform = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchDiscoveryFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.discovery = builder.buildDiscovery();
      featureSets.add(discovery);
    } else {
      this.discovery = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchDataFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.data = builder.buildData();
      featureSets.add(data);
    } else {
      this.data = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchConfigsFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.configs = builder.buildConfigs();
      featureSets.add(configs);
    } else {
      this.configs = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchAuditFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.audit = builder.buildAudit();
      featureSets.add(audit);
    } else {
      this.audit = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchEntitlementsFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.entitlements = builder.buildEntitlements();
      featureSets.add(entitlements);
    } else {
      this.entitlements = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchDocsFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.docs = builder.buildDocs();
      featureSets.add(docs);
    } else {
      this.docs = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchCatalogFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.catalog = builder.buildCatalog();
      featureSets.add(catalog);
    } else {
      this.catalog = null;
    }

    if (active.contains(StitchAgentsFeature.FEATURE_ID)) {
      this.agents = builder.buildAgents();
      featureSets.add(agents);
    } else {
      this.agents = null;
    }

    this.registry = new StitchFeatureRegistry(featureSets);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public StitchFeatureRegistry registry() {
    return registry;
  }

  public Optional<StitchStatusFeature> status() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(status);
  }

  public Optional<StitchAssetsFeature> assets() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(assets);
  }

  public Optional<StitchPlatformFeature> platform() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(platform);
  }

  public Optional<StitchDiscoveryFeature> discovery() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(discovery);
  }

  public Optional<StitchDataFeature> data() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(data);
  }

  public Optional<StitchConfigsFeature> configs() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(configs);
  }

  public Optional<StitchAuditFeature> audit() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(audit);
  }

  public Optional<StitchEntitlementsFeature> entitlements() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(entitlements);
  }

  public Optional<StitchDocsFeature> docs() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(docs);
  }

  public Optional<StitchCatalogFeature> catalog() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(catalog);
  }

  public Optional<StitchAgentsFeature> agents() {
    return Optional.ofNullable(agents);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private Consumer<StitchStatusFeature.Builder> statusCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchAssetsFeature.Builder> assetsCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchPlatformFeature.Builder> platformCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchDiscoveryFeature.Builder> discoveryCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchDataFeature.Builder> dataCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchConfigsFeature.Builder> configsCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchAuditFeature.Builder> auditCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchEntitlementsFeature.Builder> entitlementsCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchDocsFeature.Builder> docsCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchCatalogFeature.Builder> catalogCustomizer = noop();
    private Consumer<StitchAgentsFeature.Builder> agentsCustomizer = noop();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder configureStatus(Consumer<StitchStatusFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.statusCustomizer = this.statusCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureAssets(Consumer<StitchAssetsFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.assetsCustomizer = this.assetsCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configurePlatform(Consumer<StitchPlatformFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.platformCustomizer = this.platformCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureDiscovery(Consumer<StitchDiscoveryFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.discoveryCustomizer = this.discoveryCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureData(Consumer<StitchDataFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.dataCustomizer = this.dataCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureConfigs(Consumer<StitchConfigsFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.configsCustomizer = this.configsCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureAudit(Consumer<StitchAuditFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.auditCustomizer = this.auditCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureEntitlements(Consumer<StitchEntitlementsFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.entitlementsCustomizer = this.entitlementsCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureDocs(Consumer<StitchDocsFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.docsCustomizer = this.docsCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureCatalog(Consumer<StitchCatalogFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.catalogCustomizer = this.catalogCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder configureAgents(Consumer<StitchAgentsFeature.Builder> customizer) {
      if (customizer != null) {
        this.agentsCustomizer = this.agentsCustomizer.andThen(customizer);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public StitchFeatures build() {
      return build(Set.of());
    }

    public StitchFeatures build(Set<String> referencedEntryIds) {
      return new StitchFeatures(this, resolveActivatedFeatures(referencedEntryIds));
    }

    private StitchStatusFeature buildStatus() {
      StitchStatusFeature.Builder builder = StitchStatusFeature.builder();
      statusCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchAssetsFeature buildAssets() {
      StitchAssetsFeature.Builder builder = StitchAssetsFeature.builder();
      assetsCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchPlatformFeature buildPlatform() {
      StitchPlatformFeature.Builder builder = StitchPlatformFeature.builder();
      platformCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchDiscoveryFeature buildDiscovery() {
      StitchDiscoveryFeature.Builder builder = StitchDiscoveryFeature.builder();
      discoveryCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchDataFeature buildData() {
      StitchDataFeature.Builder builder = StitchDataFeature.builder();
      dataCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchConfigsFeature buildConfigs() {
      StitchConfigsFeature.Builder builder = StitchConfigsFeature.builder();
      configsCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchAuditFeature buildAudit() {
      StitchAuditFeature.Builder builder = StitchAuditFeature.builder();
      auditCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchEntitlementsFeature buildEntitlements() {
      StitchEntitlementsFeature.Builder builder = StitchEntitlementsFeature.builder();
      entitlementsCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchDocsFeature buildDocs() {
      StitchDocsFeature.Builder builder = StitchDocsFeature.builder();
      docsCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchCatalogFeature buildCatalog() {
      StitchCatalogFeature.Builder builder = StitchCatalogFeature.builder();
      catalogCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private StitchAgentsFeature buildAgents() {
      StitchAgentsFeature.Builder builder = StitchAgentsFeature.builder();
      agentsCustomizer.accept(builder);
      return builder.build();
    }

    private static Set<String> resolveActivatedFeatures(Set<String> referencedEntryIds) {
      if (referencedEntryIds == null || referencedEntryIds.isEmpty()) {
        return Set.of();
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> activated = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String entryId : referencedEntryIds) {
        activateFeatureForEntry(activated, entryId);
      }
      return Set.copyOf(activated);
    }

    private static void activateFeatureForEntry(Set<String> activated, String entryId) {
      if (entryId == null || entryId.isBlank()) {
        return;
      }
      String normalized = entryId.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (normalized.startsWith("status.")) {
        activated.add(StitchStatusFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("assets.")) {
        activated.add(StitchAssetsFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("data.")) {
        activated.add(StitchDataFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("configs.")) {
        activated.add(StitchConfigsFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("catalog.")) {
        activated.add(StitchCatalogFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("agents.")) {
        activated.add(StitchAgentsFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("docs.")) {
        activated.add(StitchDocsFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("admin.security.")) {
        activated.add(StitchPlatformFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("admin.discovery.")) {
        activated.add(StitchDiscoveryFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("admin.audit.")) {
        activated.add(StitchAuditFeature.FEATURE_ID);
        return;
      }
      if (normalized.startsWith("admin.entitlements")) {
        activated.add(StitchEntitlementsFeature.FEATURE_ID);
      }
    }

    private static <T> Consumer<T> noop() {
      return ignored -> {};
    }
  }
}
