package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public interface StitchFeatureSet {
  String id();

  int order();

  List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries();
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchAgentsFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "agents";
  public static final String PLAYGROUND_ROUTE = "agents";
  public static final String SCENARIOS_ROUTE = "agents/scenarios";
  public static final String TRACE_VIEWER_ROUTE = "agents/traces";
  public static final String TOOLS_ROUTE = "agents/tools";
  public static final String ENTRY_PLAYGROUND = "agents.playground";
  public static final String ENTRY_SCENARIOS = "agents.scenarios";
  public static final String ENTRY_TRACE_VIEWER = "agents.traceViewer";
  public static final String ENTRY_TOOLS = "agents.tools";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final String routePath;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchAgentsFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public String menuLabel() {
    return menuLabel;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    if (!enabled) {
      return List.of();
    }
    StitchMenuEntry playgroundItem =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_PLAYGROUND)
            .withLabel("Playground")
            .withRoutePath(routePath)
            .withOrder(10)
            .build();
    StitchMenuEntry scenariosItem =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_SCENARIOS)
            .withLabel("Scenarios")
            .withRoutePath(SCENARIOS_ROUTE)
            .withOrder(20)
            .build();
    StitchMenuEntry traceViewerItem =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_TRACE_VIEWER)
            .withLabel("Trace Viewer")
            .withRoutePath(TRACE_VIEWER_ROUTE)
            .withOrder(30)
            .build();
    StitchMenuEntry toolsItem =
        StitchMenuEntry.builder(ENTRY_TOOLS)
            .withLabel("Tools")
            .withRoutePath(TOOLS_ROUTE)
            .withOrder(40)
            .build();
    return List.of(playgroundItem, scenariosItem, traceViewerItem, toolsItem);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(field + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Agents";
    private String routePath = PLAYGROUND_ROUTE;
    private int order = 22;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchAgentsFeature build() {
      return new StitchAgentsFeature(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsListScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsSearch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

abstract class StitchAgentsListScreen<T> extends StitchPage {
  private final StitchAgentsProvider provider;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchResultsView<T> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final StitchResultsSearch search;
  private final Button refreshAction;

  protected StitchAgentsListScreen(
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchAgentsProvider provider,
      String pageTitle,
      String pageSubtitle,
      String screenClassName,
      String searchPlaceholder,
      String searchAria,
      String refreshAria,
      String sectionTitle,
      String gridAria,
      String emptyTitle,
      String emptyMessage) {
    super(pageTitle, pageSubtitle);
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.requireEnabled(stitch);
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.search = new StitchResultsSearch(searchPlaceholder, searchAria);

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    addClassName("stitch-agents-screen");
    addClassName(screenClassName);
    filtersBar.addClassName("stitch-agents-filters");

    StitchAgentsUiSupport.configureResults(results, gridAria, emptyTitle, emptyMessage);
    results.toolbar().setVisible(false);
    search.setWidth("min(100%, 24rem)");
    search.onQueryChange(query -> refreshRequested());
    configureGrid(results.grid());
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.attachOpenAction(results, this::openRow);

    refreshAction = StitchAgentsUiSupport.refreshAction(refreshAria, this::refreshRequested);
    filtersBar.withSearch(search).withRightAction(refreshAction);

    StitchSection resultsSection = StitchAgentsUiSupport.fullSection(sectionTitle, results);
    resultsSection.addClassName("stitch-agents-results-section");
    addToBody(filtersBar, resultsSection);

    refreshRequested();
  }

  protected final StitchAgentsProvider provider() {
    return provider;
  }

  protected final String query() {
    return search.normalizedQuery();
  }

  protected final void refreshList() {
    refreshRequested();
  }

  protected abstract void configureGrid(StitchGrid<T> grid);

  protected abstract List<T> loadRows(String query);

  protected abstract void openRow(T row);

  private void refreshRequested() {
    List<T> rows = loadRows(query());
    List<T> safe = rows == null ? List.of() : rows;
    results.setItems(safe);
    results.setResultCount(safe.size());
    results.setEmpty(safe.isEmpty());
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsPlaygroundScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.MultiSelectComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.IntegerField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.NumberField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchInspectorPreviewPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditorModeController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

@Route(value = StitchAgentsFeature.PLAYGROUND_ROUTE, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchAgentsPlaygroundScreen
    extends StitchPage implements BeforeLeaveObserver, BeforeEnterObserver {
  private static final String QUERY_SCENARIO = "scenario";

  private final StitchAgentsProvider provider;
  private final StitchAgentsSessionState sessionState;
  private final StitchEditorModeController inputMode = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();

  private final ComboBox<StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode> mode = new ComboBox<>("Mode");
  private final ComboBox<String> model = new ComboBox<>("Model");
  private final NumberField temperature = new NumberField("Temperature");
  private final IntegerField maxTokens = new IntegerField("Max Tokens");
  private final MultiSelectComboBox<String> tools = new MultiSelectComboBox<>("Tools");
  private final ComboBox<String> scenario = new ComboBox<>("Scenario");
  private final TextArea requestInput = new TextArea("Request");
  private final StitchSummaryStrip outputSummary = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final StitchTabbedDetailsPanel outputTabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
  private final StitchInspectorPreviewPanel resultPanel =
      new StitchInspectorPreviewPanel("Result", "Agents result output");
  private final TextArea planPanel = new TextArea("Plan");
  private final TextArea traceSummaryPanel = new TextArea("Trace Summary");
  private final TextArea jsonPanel = new TextArea("Run JSON");
  private final StitchResultsView<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep> trace = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final Button runAction;
  private final Button clearAction;
  private final Button refreshAction;

  private boolean syncingState;

  public StitchAgentsPlaygroundScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchAgentsProvider provider) {
    super("Agents Playground", "Control execution settings, run requests, and inspect trace output.");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.requireEnabled(stitch);
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.sessionState = provider.sessionState();

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    addClassName("stitch-agents-screen");
    addClassName("stitch-agents-playground-screen");
    filtersBar.addClassName("stitch-agents-filters");
    inputMode.enterEditMode();

    configureControls();
    configureInput();
    configureResult();
    configureTrace();
    runAction = StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(new Button("RUN", event -> runExecution()), "Run agents request");
    runAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    clearAction = StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(new Button("CLEAR", event -> clearRequested()), "Clear agents request");
    clearAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    refreshAction = StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshRequested()), "Refresh agents execution");
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refreshAction);
    configureControlBar();
    applyStateToControls();
    renderOutput();

    HorizontalLayout bottom = buildResults();
    addToBody(filtersBar, buildInput(), bottom);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, bottom);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeEnter(BeforeEnterEvent event) {
    String scenarioId = StitchAgentsUiSupport.firstQueryParam(event, QUERY_SCENARIO);
    if (scenarioId != null && !scenarioId.isBlank()) {
      provider.applyScenario(scenarioId);
      applyStateToControls();
      renderOutput();
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeLeave(BeforeLeaveEvent event) {
    dirtyStateSupport.guardBeforeLeave(
        event,
        inputMode::hasUnsavedChanges,
        this::saveInputState,
        this::discardInputState);
  }

  private StitchSection buildInput() {
    VerticalLayout input = new VerticalLayout(requestInput);
    input.setPadding(false);
    input.setSpacing(true);
    input.setWidthFull();

    StitchSection section = new StitchSection("Input");
    section.addToBody(input);
    return section;
  }

  private void configureControlBar() {
    mode.setWidth("8.5rem");
    model.setWidth("10.5rem");
    temperature.setWidth("8.5rem");
    maxTokens.setWidth("8.5rem");
    tools.setWidth("14rem");
    scenario.setWidth("13rem");
    filtersBar
        .withFilter(mode)
        .withFilter(model)
        .withFilter(temperature)
        .withFilter(maxTokens)
        .withFilter(tools)
        .withFilter(scenario)
        .withRightActions(runAction, clearAction, refreshAction);
  }

  private HorizontalLayout buildResults() {
    StitchSection resultSection = new StitchSection("Result");
    resultSection.setSizeFull();
    resultSection.addToBody(outputSummary, outputTabs);

    StitchSection traceSection = new StitchSection("Trace");
    traceSection.setSizeFull();
    traceSection.addToBody(trace);

    HorizontalLayout bottom = new HorizontalLayout(resultSection, traceSection);
    bottom.setPadding(false);
    bottom.setSpacing(true);
    bottom.setSizeFull();
    bottom.setWidthFull();
    bottom.setFlexGrow(3, resultSection);
    bottom.setFlexGrow(2, traceSection);
    return bottom;
  }

  private void configureControls() {
    mode.setItems(StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode.values());
    mode.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    mode.setWidth("9rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(mode, "Agents mode selector");
    mode.addValueChangeListener(event -> controlsChanged(event.isFromClient()));

    model.setItems(List.of("mock-gpt", "mock-fast", "mock-accurate"));
    model.setAllowCustomValue(true);
    model.setWidth("11rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(model, "Agents model selector");
    model.addValueChangeListener(event -> controlsChanged(event.isFromClient()));

    temperature.setMin(0.0d);
    temperature.setMax(2.0d);
    temperature.setStep(0.1d);
    temperature.setWidth("9rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(temperature, "Agents temperature");
    temperature.addValueChangeListener(event -> controlsChanged(event.isFromClient()));

    maxTokens.setMin(1);
    maxTokens.setWidth("9rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(maxTokens, "Agents max tokens");
    maxTokens.addValueChangeListener(event -> controlsChanged(event.isFromClient()));

    tools.setItems(provider.tools().stream().map(StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition::id).toList());
    tools.setWidth("15rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(tools, "Agents tools selector");
    tools.addValueChangeListener(event -> controlsChanged(event.isFromClient()));

    scenario.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    scenario.setItems(provider.scenarios().stream().map(StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition::id).toList());
    scenario.setPlaceholder("None");
    scenario.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    scenario.setWidth("14rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(scenario, "Agents scenario selector");
    scenario.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (syncingState) {
            return;
          }
          if (event.isFromClient() && event.getValue() != null) {
            provider.applyScenario(event.getValue());
            applyStateToControls();
            renderOutput();
            inputMode.markDirty();
            return;
          }
          controlsChanged(event.isFromClient());
        });
  }

  private void configureInput() {
    requestInput.setWidthFull();
    requestInput.setMinHeight("11rem");
    requestInput.setPlaceholder("Describe the task or ask for an execution plan.");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(requestInput, "Agents request input");
    requestInput.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (syncingState) {
            return;
          }
          sessionState.requestText = requestInput.getValue();
          if (event.isFromClient()) {
            inputMode.markDirty();
          }
        });
  }

  private void configureResult() {
    resultPanel.previewField().setReadOnly(true);
    resultPanel.previewField().setMinHeight("20rem");
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(resultPanel.previewField(), "Agents result output");

    planPanel.setWidthFull();
    planPanel.setMinHeight("20rem");
    planPanel.setReadOnly(true);
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(planPanel, "Agents plan output");

    traceSummaryPanel.setWidthFull();
    traceSummaryPanel.setMinHeight("20rem");
    traceSummaryPanel.setReadOnly(true);
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(traceSummaryPanel, "Agents trace summary");

    jsonPanel.setWidthFull();
    jsonPanel.setMinHeight("20rem");
    jsonPanel.setReadOnly(true);
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(jsonPanel, "Agents run JSON");

    outputTabs
        .addTab("result", "Result", resultPanel)
        .addTab("plan", "Plan", planPanel)
        .addTab("trace", "Trace Summary", traceSummaryPanel)
        .addTab("json", "JSON", jsonPanel)
        .selectTab("result");
  }

  private void configureTrace() {
    trace.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    trace.setPageSizeOptions(25, 50, 100);
    trace.setPageSize(25);
    trace.setResultCountVisible(true);
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.aria(trace.grid(), "Agents trace grid");
    trace.setEmptyState("No trace steps", "Run a request to populate execution trace steps.");
    trace.grid().addColumn(StitchGridColumn.text("Step", StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep::id).key("step").kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.NAME));
    trace.grid().addColumn(StitchGridColumn.<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep>text("Type", step -> step.type().name()).key("type").kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    trace.grid().addColumn(StitchGridColumn.text("Summary", StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep::summary).key("summary").kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    trace.grid().asSingleSelect().addValueChangeListener(event -> openTracePayload(event.getValue()));
  }

  private void controlsChanged(boolean fromClient) {
    if (syncingState) {
      return;
    }
    syncControlsToState();
    if (fromClient) {
      inputMode.markDirty();
    }
  }

  private void applyStateToControls() {
    syncingState = true;
    try {
      mode.setValue(sessionState.mode);
      model.setValue(sessionState.model);
      temperature.setValue(sessionState.temperature);
      maxTokens.setValue(sessionState.maxTokens);
      tools.select(sessionState.tools);
      scenario.setValue(sessionState.scenario.isBlank() ? null : sessionState.scenario);
      requestInput.setValue(sessionState.requestText);
    } finally {
      syncingState = false;
    }
  }

  private void syncControlsToState() {
    sessionState.mode = mode.getValue();
    sessionState.model = model.getValue();
    sessionState.temperature = Objects.requireNonNull(temperature.getValue(), "temperature is required");
    sessionState.maxTokens = Objects.requireNonNull(maxTokens.getValue(), "maxTokens is required");
    sessionState.tools = List.copyOf(tools.getSelectedItems());
    String scenarioValue = scenario.getValue();
    sessionState.scenario = scenarioValue == null ? "" : scenarioValue;
  }

  private void runExecution() {
    syncControlsToState();
    sessionState.requestText = requestInput.getValue();
    if (sessionState.requestText.isBlank()) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Request is required", "Provide request text before running.");
      return;
    }
    provider.execute(
        sessionState.requestText,
        new StitchAgentsProvider.ExecutionConfig(
            sessionState.mode,
            sessionState.model,
            sessionState.temperature,
            sessionState.maxTokens,
            sessionState.tools,
            sessionState.scenario));
    renderOutput();
    inputMode.clearDirty();
    Notification.show("Execution completed", 1100, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private void refreshRequested() {
    if (sessionState.requestText.isBlank()) {
      renderOutput();
      return;
    }
    runExecution();
  }

  private void clearRequested() {
    sessionState.clearRequestAndOutput();
    syncingState = true;
    try {
      requestInput.clear();
    } finally {
      syncingState = false;
    }
    renderOutput();
    inputMode.clearDirty();
  }

  private void renderOutput() {
    outputSummary.setItems(resultSummary());
    resultPanel.setContext("Run Mode", sessionState.mode.name());
    resultPanel.setMetadata(resultMetadata());
    resultPanel.setPreviewValue(
        sessionState.resultText.isBlank() ? "Run a request to produce output." : sessionState.resultText);
    planPanel.setValue(planText());
    traceSummaryPanel.setValue(traceSummaryText());
    jsonPanel.setValue(executionJson());
    updateTrace(sessionState.traceSteps);
  }

  private void updateTrace(List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep> steps) {
    trace.setItems(steps);
    trace.setResultCount(steps.size());
    trace.setEmpty(steps.isEmpty());
  }

  private void openTracePayload(StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep step) {
    if (step == null) {
      return;
    }
    new StitchJsonDialog("Trace Step JSON - " + step.id(), step.payload()).open();
    trace.grid().asSingleSelect().clear();
  }

  private boolean saveInputState() {
    syncControlsToState();
    sessionState.requestText = requestInput.getValue();
    inputMode.clearDirty();
    return true;
  }

  private void discardInputState() {
    clearRequested();
  }

  private Map<String, String> resultMetadata() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    metadata.put("Model", sessionState.model);
    metadata.put("Temperature", String.valueOf(sessionState.temperature));
    metadata.put("Max Tokens", String.valueOf(sessionState.maxTokens));
    metadata.put("Tools", sessionState.tools.isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(", ", sessionState.tools));
    metadata.put("Scenario", scenarioLabel());
    metadata.put("Trace Steps", String.valueOf(sessionState.traceSteps.size()));
    metadata.put("Run History", String.valueOf(provider.runHistory().size()));
    return metadata;
  }

  private Map<String, String> resultSummary() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Mode", sessionState.mode.name());
    summary.put("Model", sessionState.model);
    summary.put("Scenario", scenarioLabel());
    summary.put("Steps", String.valueOf(sessionState.traceSteps.size()));
    return summary;
  }

  private String planText() {
    List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep> planSteps =
        sessionState.traceSteps.stream()
            .filter(step -> step.type() == StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.PLAN)
            .toList();
    if (planSteps.isEmpty()) {
      return "No PLAN steps captured for this run.";
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
    for (StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep step : planSteps) {
      builder.append(step.id()).append(" - ").append(step.summary()).append("\n");
      builder.append(StitchAgentsUiSupport.prettyJson(step.payload())).append("\n\n");
    }
    return builder.toString().trim();
  }

  private String traceSummaryText() {
    if (sessionState.traceSteps.isEmpty()) {
      return "No trace steps captured.";
    }
    long planCount =
        sessionState.traceSteps.stream()
            .filter(step -> step.type() == StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.PLAN)
            .count();
    long toolCount =
        sessionState.traceSteps.stream()
            .filter(step -> step.type() == StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.TOOL)
            .count();
    long responseCount =
        sessionState.traceSteps.stream()
            .filter(step -> step.type() == StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.RESPONSE)
            .count();
    return "PLAN: "
        + planCount
        + "\nTOOL: "
        + toolCount
        + "\nRESPONSE: "
        + responseCount
        + "\n\nLast step:\n"
        + sessionState.traceSteps.getLast().summary();
  }

  private String executionJson() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("mode", sessionState.mode.name());
    payload.put("model", sessionState.model);
    payload.put("temperature", sessionState.temperature);
    payload.put("maxTokens", sessionState.maxTokens);
    payload.put("tools", sessionState.tools);
    payload.put("scenario", sessionState.scenario);
    payload.put("request", sessionState.requestText);
    payload.put("result", sessionState.resultText);
    payload.put("trace", sessionState.traceSteps);
    return StitchAgentsUiSupport.prettyJson(payload);
  }

  private String scenarioLabel() {
    return provider.scenarioName(sessionState.scenario);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public final class StitchAgentsProvider {
  private static final int MAX_RUN_HISTORY = 50;
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchAgentsSessionState sessionState = new StitchAgentsSessionState();
  private final List<ScenarioDefinition> scenarios = new ArrayList<>(seedScenarios());
  private final List<ToolDefinition> tools = new ArrayList<>(seedTools());

  public StitchAgentsProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = runtimeContext;
  }

  public StitchAgentsSessionState sessionState() {
    return sessionState;
  }

  public List<ScenarioDefinition> scenarios() {
    return List.copyOf(scenarios);
  }

  public List<ToolDefinition> tools() {
    return List.copyOf(tools);
  }

  public boolean updateScenario(ScenarioDefinition updated) {
    if (updated == null || updated.id() == null || updated.id().isBlank()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (int index = 0; index < scenarios.size(); index++) {
      if (scenarios.get(index).id().equals(updated.id())) {
        scenarios.set(index, updated);
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  public boolean updateTool(ToolDefinition updated) {
    if (updated == null || updated.id() == null || updated.id().isBlank()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (int index = 0; index < tools.size(); index++) {
      if (tools.get(index).id().equals(updated.id())) {
        tools.set(index, updated);
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  public boolean applyScenario(String id) {
    ScenarioDefinition scenario = findScenario(id);
    if (scenario == null) {
      return false;
    }
    sessionState.mode = scenario.mode();
    sessionState.model = scenario.model();
    sessionState.temperature = scenario.temperature();
    sessionState.maxTokens = scenario.maxTokens();
    sessionState.tools = scenario.tools();
    sessionState.scenario = scenario.id();
    sessionState.requestText = scenario.requestTemplate();
    return true;
  }

  public String scenarioName(String id) {
    ScenarioDefinition scenario = findScenario(id);
    return scenario == null ? "-" : scenario.name();
  }

  public List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun> runHistory() {
    return sessionState.runHistory;
  }

  public void execute(String requestText, ExecutionConfig config) {
    String runId = "run-" + Instant.now().toEpochMilli();
    List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep> trace = new ArrayList<>();
    trace.add(planStep(runId, requestText, config));
    if (config.tools().isEmpty()) {
      trace.add(
          new StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep(
              runId + "-tool-none",
              StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.TOOL,
              "No tools selected; execution stays planner-only.",
              Map.of("tools", List.of(), "status", "SKIPPED")));
    } else {
      int step = 1;
      for (String tool : config.tools()) {
        trace.add(toolStep(runId, tool, step));
        step++;
      }
    }
    String resultText = resultText(requestText, config);
    trace.add(
        new StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep(
            runId + "-response",
            StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.RESPONSE,
            "Compose final response from plan/tool outputs.",
            Map.of("status", "COMPLETED", "resultChars", resultText.length())));

    StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun run =
        new StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun(
            runId,
            Instant.now(),
            config.mode(),
            config.model(),
            config.temperature(),
            config.maxTokens(),
            config.tools(),
            config.scenario(),
            requestText,
            resultText,
            List.copyOf(trace));
    sessionState.resultText = resultText;
    sessionState.traceSteps = run.traceSteps();
    sessionState.selectedRunId = run.runId();
    sessionState.runHistory = appendRun(run);
  }

  private StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep planStep(
      String runId, String requestText, ExecutionConfig config) {
    return new StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep(
        runId + "-plan",
        StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.PLAN,
        "Assemble execution plan from control settings.",
        Map.of(
            "mode",
            config.mode().name(),
            "model",
            config.model(),
            "temperature",
            config.temperature(),
            "maxTokens",
            config.maxTokens(),
            "scenario",
            config.scenario(),
            "requestLength",
            requestText.length(),
            "runtimeApp",
            runtimeContext.appTitle()));
  }

  private static StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep toolStep(String runId, String tool, int step) {
    return new StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep(
        runId + "-tool-" + step,
        StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStepType.TOOL,
        "Invoke tool " + tool + " (mock).",
        Map.of("tool", tool, "step", step, "status", "OK", "durationMs", 25 + (step * 10)));
  }

  private static String resultText(String requestText, ExecutionConfig config) {
    return "Execution complete (mock).\n"
        + "Mode: "
        + config.mode().name()
        + "\nModel: "
        + config.model()
        + "\nTemperature: "
        + config.temperature()
        + "\nMax Tokens: "
        + config.maxTokens()
        + "\nTools: "
        + (config.tools().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(", ", config.tools()))
        + "\nScenario: "
        + (config.scenario().isBlank() ? "-" : config.scenario())
        + "\n\nRequest:\n"
        + requestText;
  }

  private List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun> appendRun(StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun run) {
    List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun> next = new ArrayList<>();
    next.add(run);
    next.addAll(sessionState.runHistory.stream().limit(MAX_RUN_HISTORY - 1).toList());
    return List.copyOf(next);
  }

  private ScenarioDefinition findScenario(String id) {
    for (ScenarioDefinition scenario : scenarios) {
      if (scenario.id().equals(id)) {
        return scenario;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static List<ScenarioDefinition> seedScenarios() {
    return List.of(
        new ScenarioDefinition("INCIDENT_TRIAGE", "Incident Triage", "Classify and route a production incident based on status and impact clues.", StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode.AUTO, "mock-fast", 0.2d, 800, List.of("CATALOG_SEARCH", "ASSET_LOOKUP"), "Analyze current incident indicators and produce a triage plan with escalation targets.", List.of("Supports high-priority incident workflows.", "Prefers deterministic planning."), Map.of("domain", "ops", "priority", "high")),
        new ScenarioDefinition("SCHEMA_CHANGE_REVIEW", "Schema Change Review", "Review schema-impact risks and produce a compatibility checklist.", StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode.MANUAL, "mock-accurate", 0.1d, 1200, List.of("SQL_PLAN", "CATALOG_SEARCH"), "Evaluate a proposed schema change and list compatibility risks and mitigations.", List.of("Use when validating rollout readiness.", "Includes SQL impact checks."), Map.of("domain", "data", "priority", "medium")),
        new ScenarioDefinition("ACCESS_POLICY_CHECK", "Access Policy Check", "Inspect entitlement posture and identify likely access blockers.", StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode.SCENARIO, "mock-gpt", 0.3d, 900, List.of("ENTITLEMENTS_CHECK", "ASSET_LOOKUP"), "Review access policy readiness for a new service onboarding.", List.of("Focused on entitlements and ownership.", "Returns remediation hints."), Map.of("domain", "security", "priority", "medium")));
  }

  private static List<ToolDefinition> seedTools() {
    return List.of(
        new ToolDefinition("CATALOG_SEARCH", "Catalog Search", "Lookup catalog entities by keyword, group, owner, and tags.", "query, type, group, tags, owner", "matched assets with summary metadata", "Use read-only catalog context for decision support.", Map.of("scope", "catalog", "mode", "read-only")),
        new ToolDefinition("ASSET_LOOKUP", "Asset Lookup", "Resolve canonical asset identity and lightweight technical metadata.", "asset id or group/name", "asset identity envelope", "Prefer canonical IDs when available.", Map.of("scope", "assets", "mode", "read-only")),
        new ToolDefinition("SQL_PLAN", "SQL Plan", "Generate a SQL impact plan for table/schema operations.", "sql intent, target schema", "ordered execution checklist", "Mock planning only in Phase 3.", Map.of("scope", "data", "mode", "planning")),
        new ToolDefinition("ENTITLEMENTS_CHECK", "Entitlements Check", "Evaluate likely entitlement constraints for actors and assets.", "subject, asset, action", "access posture summary", "Use alongside ownership metadata.", Map.of("scope", "security", "mode", "analysis")));
  }

  public record ExecutionConfig(StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode mode, String model, double temperature, int maxTokens, List<String> tools, String scenario) {}

  public record ScenarioDefinition(
      String id,
      String name,
      String summary,
      StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode mode,
      String model,
      double temperature,
      int maxTokens,
      List<String> tools,
      String requestTemplate,
      List<String> notes,
      Map<String, Object> payload) {}

  public record ToolDefinition(
      String id,
      String name,
      String summary,
      String inputs,
      String outputs,
      String safetyNotes,
      Map<String, Object> payload) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsScenarioEditorDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.IntegerField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.NumberField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditorModeController;

final class StitchAgentsScenarioEditorDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchAgentsProvider provider;
  private final Consumer<StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition> onSaved;
  private final Runnable onOpenInPlayground;
  private final StitchEditorModeController modeController = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
  private final VerticalLayout overviewTab = new VerticalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout configurationTab = new VerticalLayout();
  private final TextArea jsonTab = new TextArea("Scenario JSON");
  private final TextField nameField = new TextField("Name");
  private final TextArea summaryField = new TextArea("Summary");
  private final ComboBox<StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode> modeField = new ComboBox<>("Mode");
  private final TextField modelField = new TextField("Model");
  private final NumberField temperatureField = new NumberField("Temperature");
  private final IntegerField maxTokensField = new IntegerField("Max Tokens");
  private final TextField toolsField = new TextField("Tools (comma-separated)");
  private final TextArea templateField = new TextArea("Request Template");
  private final TextArea notesField = new TextArea("Notes (one per line)");
  private final Button editAction = action("EDIT", "Edit selected scenario", this::editRequested);
  private final Button saveAction = action("SAVE", "Save scenario updates", this::saveRequestedFromAction);
  private final Button cancelAction = action("CANCEL", "Cancel scenario editing", this::cancelRequested);

  private StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition selected;
  private StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition persisted;

  StitchAgentsScenarioEditorDialog(
      StitchAgentsProvider provider,
      StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition selected,
      Consumer<StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition> onSaved,
      Runnable onOpenInPlayground) {
    super("Scenario");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.selected = Objects.requireNonNull(selected, "selected");
    this.persisted = this.selected;
    this.onSaved = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onSaved, value -> {});
    this.onOpenInPlayground = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onOpenInPlayground, () -> {});

    addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-dialog");
    setWidth("min(1160px, 96vw)");
    setHeight("88vh");
    setMaxHeight("92vh");
    body().getStyle().set("max-height", "74vh");
    body().getStyle().set("overflow", "auto");
    body().getStyle().set("min-height", "0");

    modeField.setItems(StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode.values());
    modeField.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    modelField.setWidth("14rem");
    toolsField.setWidthFull();
    summaryField.setWidthFull();
    summaryField.setMinHeight("7rem");
    templateField.setWidthFull();
    templateField.setMinHeight("10rem");
    notesField.setWidthFull();
    notesField.setMinHeight("8rem");
    jsonTab.setWidthFull();
    jsonTab.setMinHeight("18rem");
    jsonTab.setReadOnly(true);

    HorizontalLayout identityRow = new HorizontalLayout(modeField, modelField, temperatureField, maxTokensField);
    identityRow.setPadding(false);
    identityRow.setSpacing(true);
    identityRow.setWidthFull();
    identityRow.setFlexGrow(1, modeField, modelField, temperatureField, maxTokensField);
    configurationTab.setPadding(false);
    configurationTab.setSpacing(true);
    configurationTab.setWidthFull();
    configurationTab.add(
        nameField, summaryField, identityRow, toolsField, templateField, notesField, openInPlaygroundButton());

    overviewTab.setPadding(false);
    overviewTab.setSpacing(true);
    overviewTab.setWidthFull();

    tabs.addTab("overview", "Overview", overviewTab)
        .addTab("configuration", "Configuration", configurationTab)
        .addTab("json", "JSON", jsonTab)
        .selectTab("overview");

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(summaryStrip, tabs);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-dialog-content");
    content.getStyle().set("min-height", "0");
    addToBody(content);

    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> selected);
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::closeRequested);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(0, editAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(1, saveAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(2, cancelAction);

    registerDirtyTracking();
    refreshView();
  }

  private Button openInPlaygroundButton() {
    Button open = new Button("OPEN IN PLAYGROUND", event -> onOpenInPlayground.run());
    open.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    open.addClassName("stitch-agents-open-playground");
    open.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Open scenario in playground");
    open.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Open scenario in playground");
    return open;
  }

  private void editRequested() {
    modeController.enterEditMode();
    modeController.clearDirty();
    tabs.selectTab("configuration");
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void saveRequestedFromAction() {
    saveRequested();
  }

  private boolean saveRequested() {
    if (!modeController.isEditMode()) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition updated =
          new StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition(
              selected.id(),
              nameField.getValue(),
              summaryField.getValue(),
              modeField.getValue() == null ? StitchAgentsSessionState.Mode.AUTO : modeField.getValue(),
              modelField.getValue(),
              temperatureField.getValue() == null ? 0.2d : temperatureField.getValue(),
              maxTokensField.getValue() == null ? 800 : maxTokensField.getValue(),
              parseTools(toolsField.getValue()),
              templateField.getValue(),
              parseNotes(notesField.getValue()),
              selected.payload());
      if (!provider.updateScenario(updated)) {
        StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save scenario", "Scenario update could not be applied.");
        return false;
      }
      selected = updated;
      persisted = updated;
      modeController.clear();
      refreshView();
      onSaved.accept(updated);
      Notification.show("Scenario saved", 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save scenario", StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void cancelRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      modeController.clear();
      selected = persisted;
      refreshView();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(this::saveRequested, this::discardChanges, () -> {});
  }

  private void discardChanges() {
    selected = persisted;
    modeController.clear();
    refreshView();
  }

  private void closeRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      close();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        () -> {
          if (saveRequested()) {
            close();
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        },
        () -> {
          discardChanges();
          close();
        },
        () -> {});
  }

  private void refreshView() {
    summaryStrip.setItems(summaryValues(selected));
    overviewTab.removeAll();
    overviewTab.add(overviewContent(selected));
    nameField.setValue(selected.name());
    summaryField.setValue(selected.summary());
    modeField.setValue(selected.mode());
    modelField.setValue(selected.model());
    temperatureField.setValue(selected.temperature());
    maxTokensField.setValue(selected.maxTokens());
    toolsField.setValue(String.join(", ", selected.tools()));
    templateField.setValue(selected.requestTemplate());
    notesField.setValue(String.join("\n", selected.notes()));
    jsonTab.setValue(StitchAgentsUiSupport.prettyJson(selected));
    setDialogTitle("Scenario - " + selected.name());
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void refreshActions() {
    boolean editMode = modeController.isEditMode();
    editAction.setVisible(!editMode);
    editAction.setEnabled(!editMode);
    saveAction.setVisible(editMode);
    saveAction.setEnabled(editMode);
    cancelAction.setVisible(editMode);
    cancelAction.setEnabled(editMode);
    nameField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    summaryField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    modeField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    modelField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    temperatureField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    maxTokensField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    toolsField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    templateField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    notesField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
  }

  private static Component overviewContent(StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition scenario) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Scenario", scenario.id());
    values.put("Name", scenario.name());
    values.put("Mode", scenario.mode().name());
    values.put("Model", scenario.model());
    values.put("Temperature", String.valueOf(scenario.temperature()));
    values.put("Max Tokens", String.valueOf(scenario.maxTokens()));
    values.put("Tools", scenario.tools().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(", ", scenario.tools()));
    values.put("Summary", scenario.summary());
    values.put("Notes", scenario.notes().isEmpty() ? "-" : String.join(" | ", scenario.notes()));
    FormLayout form = StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(List.copyOf(values.keySet()), values, Map.of());
    form.addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-form");
    return form;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> summaryValues(StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition scenario) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Scenario", scenario.id());
    values.put("Mode", scenario.mode().name());
    values.put("Model", scenario.model());
    values.put("Tools", String.valueOf(scenario.tools().size()));
    return values;
  }

  private void registerDirtyTracking() {
    nameField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    summaryField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    modeField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    modelField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    temperatureField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    maxTokensField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    toolsField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    templateField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
    notesField.addValueChangeListener(this::markDirtyIfClient);
  }

  private void markDirtyIfClient(com.vaadin.flow.component.AbstractField.ComponentValueChangeEvent<?, ?> event) {
    if (event.isFromClient() && modeController.isEditMode()) {
      modeController.markDirty();
      refreshActions();
    }
  }

  private static List<String> parseTools(String value) {
    String normalized = value == null ? "" : value;
    return java.util.Arrays.stream(normalized.split(","))
        .map(String::trim)
        .filter(part -> !part.isBlank())
        .distinct()
        .toList();
  }

  private static List<String> parseNotes(String value) {
    String normalized = value == null ? "" : value;
    return java.util.Arrays.stream(normalized.split("\\R"))
        .map(String::trim)
        .filter(part -> !part.isBlank())
        .toList();
  }

  private static Button action(String text, String ariaLabel, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button(text, event -> action.run());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-action-button");
    button.addClassName("stitch-btn");
    StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, text);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    return button;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsScenariosScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.QueryParameters;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;

@Route(value = StitchAgentsFeature.SCENARIOS_ROUTE, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchAgentsScenariosScreen
    extends StitchAgentsListScreen<StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition> {
  public StitchAgentsScenariosScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchAgentsProvider provider) {
    super(
        stitch,
        provider,
        "Agents Scenarios",
        "Browse and manage scenario templates.",
        "stitch-agents-scenarios-screen",
        "Search scenarios",
        "Agents scenarios search",
        "Refresh scenarios",
        "Scenarios",
        "Agents scenarios grid",
        "No scenarios",
        "No scenarios matched the current search.");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(StitchGridColumn.name("Name", StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition::name).key("name"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Scenario", StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition::id)
            .key("id")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.<StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition>status(
                "Mode", scenario -> scenario.mode().name())
            .key("mode"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Model", StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition::model)
            .key("model")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Summary", StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition::summary)
            .key("summary")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition> loadRows(String query) {
    return provider().scenarios().stream()
        .filter(scenario -> StitchAgentsUiSupport.matches(query, scenario.id(), scenario.name(), scenario.summary()))
        .toList();
  }

  @Override
  protected void openRow(StitchAgentsProvider.ScenarioDefinition scenario) {
    if (scenario == null) {
      return;
    }
    new StitchAgentsScenarioEditorDialog(
            provider(),
            scenario,
            saved -> refreshList(),
            () -> openInPlayground(scenario.id()))
        .open();
  }

  private void openInPlayground(String scenarioId) {
    if (scenarioId == null || scenarioId.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    provider().applyScenario(scenarioId);
    UI ui = UI.getCurrent();
    if (ui != null) {
      ui.navigate(
          StitchAgentsFeature.PLAYGROUND_ROUTE,
          QueryParameters.simple(Map.of("scenario", scenarioId)));
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsSessionState.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public final class StitchAgentsSessionState {
  Mode mode = Mode.AUTO;
  String model = "mock-gpt";
  double temperature = 0.2d;
  int maxTokens = 1024;
  List<String> tools = List.of();
  String scenario = "";
  String requestText = "";
  String resultText = "";
  List<TraceStep> traceSteps = List.of();
  List<TraceRun> runHistory = List.of();
  String selectedRunId = "";

  public void clearRequestAndOutput() {
    requestText = "";
    resultText = "";
    traceSteps = List.of();
  }

  public enum Mode {
    AUTO,
    MANUAL,
    SCENARIO
  }

  public enum TraceStepType {
    PLAN,
    TOOL,
    RESPONSE
  }

  public record TraceStep(String id, TraceStepType type, String summary, Map<String, Object> payload) {}

  public record TraceRun(
      String runId,
      Instant startedUtc,
      Mode mode,
      String model,
      double temperature,
      int maxTokens,
      List<String> tools,
      String scenario,
      String requestText,
      String resultText,
      List<TraceStep> traceSteps) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsToolEditorDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditorModeController;

final class StitchAgentsToolEditorDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchAgentsProvider provider;
  private final Consumer<StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition> onSaved;
  private final StitchEditorModeController modeController = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
  private final VerticalLayout overviewTab = new VerticalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout configurationTab = new VerticalLayout();
  private final TextArea jsonTab = new TextArea("Tool JSON");
  private final TextField nameField = new TextField("Name");
  private final TextArea summaryField = new TextArea("Summary");
  private final TextField inputsField = new TextField("Inputs");
  private final TextField outputsField = new TextField("Outputs");
  private final TextArea safetyField = new TextArea("Safety Notes");
  private final Button editAction = action("EDIT", "Edit selected tool", this::editRequested);
  private final Button saveAction = action("SAVE", "Save tool updates", this::saveRequestedFromAction);
  private final Button cancelAction = action("CANCEL", "Cancel tool editing", this::cancelRequested);

  private StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition selected;
  private StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition persisted;

  StitchAgentsToolEditorDialog(
      StitchAgentsProvider provider,
      StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition selected,
      Consumer<StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition> onSaved) {
    super("Tool");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.selected = Objects.requireNonNull(selected, "selected");
    this.persisted = this.selected;
    this.onSaved = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onSaved, definition -> {});

    addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-dialog");
    setWidth("min(1120px, 96vw)");
    setHeight("86vh");
    setMaxHeight("92vh");
    body().getStyle().set("max-height", "72vh");
    body().getStyle().set("overflow", "auto");
    body().getStyle().set("min-height", "0");

    summaryStrip.addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-summary");
    overviewTab.setPadding(false);
    overviewTab.setSpacing(true);
    overviewTab.setWidthFull();
    configurationTab.setPadding(false);
    configurationTab.setSpacing(true);
    configurationTab.setWidthFull();

    summaryField.setWidthFull();
    summaryField.setMinHeight("8rem");
    safetyField.setWidthFull();
    safetyField.setMinHeight("7rem");
    jsonTab.setWidthFull();
    jsonTab.setMinHeight("20rem");
    jsonTab.setReadOnly(true);

    configurationTab.add(nameField, summaryField, inputsField, outputsField, safetyField);

    tabs.addTab("overview", "Overview", overviewTab)
        .addTab("configuration", "Configuration", configurationTab)
        .addTab("json", "JSON", jsonTab)
        .selectTab("overview");

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(summaryStrip, tabs);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-dialog-content");
    content.getStyle().set("min-height", "0");
    addToBody(content);

    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> selected);
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::closeRequested);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(0, editAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(1, saveAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(2, cancelAction);

    registerDirtyTracking(nameField, summaryField, inputsField, outputsField, safetyField);
    refreshView();
  }

  private void editRequested() {
    modeController.enterEditMode();
    modeController.clearDirty();
    tabs.selectTab("configuration");
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void saveRequestedFromAction() {
    saveRequested();
  }

  private boolean saveRequested() {
    if (!modeController.isEditMode()) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition updated =
          new StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition(
              selected.id(),
              nameField.getValue(),
              summaryField.getValue(),
              inputsField.getValue(),
              outputsField.getValue(),
              safetyField.getValue(),
              selected.payload());
      if (!provider.updateTool(updated)) {
        StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save tool", "Tool update could not be applied.");
        return false;
      }
      selected = updated;
      persisted = updated;
      modeController.clear();
      refreshView();
      onSaved.accept(updated);
      Notification.show("Tool saved", 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save tool", StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void cancelRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      modeController.clear();
      selected = persisted;
      refreshView();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(this::saveRequested, this::discardChanges, () -> {});
  }

  private void discardChanges() {
    selected = persisted;
    modeController.clear();
    refreshView();
  }

  private void closeRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      close();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        () -> {
          if (saveRequested()) {
            close();
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        },
        () -> {
          discardChanges();
          close();
        },
        () -> {});
  }

  private void refreshView() {
    summaryStrip.setItems(summaryValues(selected));
    overviewTab.removeAll();
    overviewTab.add(overviewContent(selected));
    nameField.setValue(selected.name());
    summaryField.setValue(selected.summary());
    inputsField.setValue(selected.inputs());
    outputsField.setValue(selected.outputs());
    safetyField.setValue(selected.safetyNotes());
    jsonTab.setValue(StitchAgentsUiSupport.prettyJson(selected));
    setDialogTitle("Tool - " + selected.name());
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void refreshActions() {
    boolean editMode = modeController.isEditMode();
    editAction.setVisible(!editMode);
    editAction.setEnabled(!editMode);
    saveAction.setVisible(editMode);
    saveAction.setEnabled(editMode);
    cancelAction.setVisible(editMode);
    cancelAction.setEnabled(editMode);
    nameField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    summaryField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    inputsField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    outputsField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    safetyField.setReadOnly(!editMode);
  }

  private static Component overviewContent(StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition tool) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Tool", tool.id());
    values.put("Name", tool.name());
    values.put("Inputs", tool.inputs());
    values.put("Outputs", tool.outputs());
    values.put("Safety", tool.safetyNotes());
    values.put("Summary", tool.summary());
    FormLayout form =
        org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(
            List.copyOf(values.keySet()), values, Map.of());
    form.addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-form");
    return form;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> summaryValues(StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition tool) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("Tool", tool.id());
    values.put("Name", tool.name());
    values.put("Inputs", tool.inputs());
    values.put("Outputs", tool.outputs());
    return values;
  }

  private void registerDirtyTracking(Component... fields) {
    for (Component field : fields) {
      if (field instanceof TextField textField) {
        textField.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (event.isFromClient() && modeController.isEditMode()) {
                modeController.markDirty();
                refreshActions();
              }
            });
      } else if (field instanceof TextArea textArea) {
        textArea.addValueChangeListener(
            event -> {
              if (event.isFromClient() && modeController.isEditMode()) {
                modeController.markDirty();
                refreshActions();
              }
            });
      }
    }
  }

  private static Button action(String text, String ariaLabel, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button(text, event -> action.run());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-action-button");
    button.addClassName("stitch-btn");
    StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, text);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    return button;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;

@Route(value = StitchAgentsFeature.TOOLS_ROUTE, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchAgentsToolsScreen extends StitchAgentsListScreen<StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition> {
  public StitchAgentsToolsScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchAgentsProvider provider) {
    super(
        stitch,
        provider,
        "Agents Tools",
        "Browse and manage tool definitions.",
        "stitch-agents-tools-screen",
        "Search tools",
        "Agents tools search",
        "Refresh tools",
        "Tools",
        "Agents tools grid",
        "No tools",

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition> grid) {

    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Name", StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition::name)

    grid.addColumn(

        StitchGridColumn.text("Inputs", StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition::inputs)
            .key("inputs")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));

        StitchGridColumn.text("Outputs", StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition::outputs)
            .key("outputs")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
  }

  protected List<StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition> loadRows(String query) {

        .filter(tool -> StitchAgentsUiSupport.matches(query, tool.id(), tool.name(), tool.summary()))
        .toList();
  }

  @Override
  protected void openRow(StitchAgentsProvider.ToolDefinition tool) {
    if (tool == null) {
      return;
    }
    new StitchAgentsToolEditorDialog(provider(), tool, saved -> refreshList()).open();
  }
