===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsTraceRunDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

final class StitchAgentsTraceRunDialog extends StitchDialog {
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
  private final TextArea summaryTab = new TextArea("Run Summary");
  private final StitchResultsView<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep> stepsTab = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final TextArea payloadTab = new TextArea("Step Payload");
  private final TextArea jsonTab = new TextArea("Trace JSON");
  private final StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun run;
  private StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep selectedStep;

  StitchAgentsTraceRunDialog(StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun run) {
    super("Trace Run");
    this.run = Objects.requireNonNull(run, "run");
    this.selectedStep = run.traceSteps().stream().findFirst().orElse(null);

    addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-dialog");
    setWidth("min(1160px, 96vw)");
    setHeight("88vh");
    setMaxHeight("92vh");
    body().getStyle().set("max-height", "74vh");
    body().getStyle().set("overflow", "auto");
    body().getStyle().set("min-height", "0");

    summaryTab.setWidthFull();
    summaryTab.setMinHeight("12rem");
    summaryTab.setReadOnly(true);
    payloadTab.setWidthFull();
    payloadTab.setMinHeight("12rem");
    payloadTab.setReadOnly(true);
    jsonTab.setWidthFull();
    jsonTab.setMinHeight("18rem");
    jsonTab.setReadOnly(true);

    configureStepsGrid();
    refreshSummary();
    refreshPayload();
    refreshJson();

    tabs.addTab("summary", "Summary", summaryTab)
        .addTab("steps", "Steps", stepsTab)
        .addTab("payload", "Payload", payloadTab)
        .addTab("json", "JSON", jsonTab)
        .selectTab("summary");

    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout(summaryStrip, tabs);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.addClassName("stitch-agents-editor-dialog-content");
    addToBody(content);

    setDialogTitle("Trace Run - " + run.runId());
    withJsonPayloadSupplier(this::jsonPayload);
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::close);
  }

  private void configureStepsGrid() {
    StitchAgentsUiSupport.configureResults(
        stepsTab, "Agents trace steps grid", "No steps", "Selected run does not include trace steps.");
    stepsTab.toolbar().setVisible(false);
    stepsTab
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Step", StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep::id)
                .key("step")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.NAME));
    stepsTab
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep>text("Type", step -> step.type().name())
                .key("type")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    stepsTab
        .grid()
        .addColumn(
            StitchGridColumn.text("Summary", StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep::summary)
                .key("summary")
                .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    stepsTab.grid().asSingleSelect().addValueChangeListener(event -> stepSelected(event.getValue()));
    stepsTab.setItems(run.traceSteps());
    stepsTab.setResultCount(run.traceSteps().size());
    stepsTab.setEmpty(run.traceSteps().isEmpty());
  }

  private void stepSelected(StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceStep step) {
    selectedStep = step;
    refreshPayload();
    refreshJson();
  }

  private void refreshSummary() {
    summaryStrip.setItems(summaryItems(run));
    summaryTab.setValue(
        "Request\n"
            + run.requestText()
            + "\n\nResult\n"
            + run.resultText());
  }

  private void refreshPayload() {
    if (selectedStep == null) {
      payloadTab.setValue("Select a step to inspect payload details.");
      return;
    }
    payloadTab.setValue(StitchAgentsUiSupport.prettyJson(selectedStep.payload()));
  }

  private void refreshJson() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("run", run);
    payload.put("selectedStep", selectedStep);
    jsonTab.setValue(StitchAgentsUiSupport.prettyJson(payload));
  }

  private Object jsonPayload() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("run", run);
    payload.put("selectedStep", selectedStep);
    return payload;
  }

  private static Map<String, String> summaryItems(StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun run) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Run", run.runId());
    summary.put("Mode", run.mode().name());
    summary.put("Model", run.model());
    summary.put("Scenario", run.scenario().isBlank() ? "-" : run.scenario());
    summary.put("Steps", String.valueOf(run.traceSteps().size()));
    return summary;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsTraceViewerScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;

@Route(value = StitchAgentsFeature.TRACE_VIEWER_ROUTE, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchAgentsTraceViewerScreen
    extends StitchAgentsListScreen<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun> {
  public StitchAgentsTraceViewerScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchAgentsProvider provider) {
    super(
        stitch,
        provider,
        "Agents Trace Viewer",
        "Inspect execution history from run results.",
        "stitch-agents-trace-screen",
        "Search runs",
        "Agents run search",
        "Refresh trace history",
        "Runs",
        "Agents runs grid",
        "No trace history",
        "Run requests from Playground to capture trace history.");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.timestamp("Started", StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun::startedUtc)
            .key("started")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP));
    grid.addColumn(StitchGridColumn.name("Run", StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun::runId).key("run"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun>status("Mode", run -> run.mode().name())
            .key("mode"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun>text(
                "Scenario", run -> run.scenario().isBlank() ? "-" : run.scenario())
            .key("scenario")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun>text(
                "Summary", run -> summarize(run.requestText()))
            .key("summary")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun> loadRows(String query) {
    return provider().runHistory().stream()
        .filter(
            run ->
                StitchAgentsUiSupport.matches(
                    query, run.runId(), run.requestText(), run.scenario(), run.mode().name()))
        .toList();
  }

  @Override
  protected void openRow(StitchAgentsSessionState.TraceRun run) {
    if (run == null) {
      return;
    }
    provider().sessionState().selectedRunId = run.runId();
    new StitchAgentsTraceRunDialog(run).open();
  }

  private static String summarize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.length() <= 72) {
      return value == null ? "" : value;
    }
    return value.substring(0, 69) + "...";
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/agents/StitchAgentsUiSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.agents;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeEnterEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsSearch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;

final class StitchAgentsUiSupport {
  private StitchAgentsUiSupport() {}

  static void requireEnabled(Stitch stitch) {
    stitch
        .features()
        .agents()
        .filter(StitchAgentsFeature::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  static <T extends Component> T aria(T component, String label) {
    component.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label);
    return component;
  }

  static String firstQueryParam(BeforeEnterEvent event, String key) {
    List<String> values = event.getLocation().getQueryParameters().getParameters().get(key);
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return values.getFirst();
  }

  static <T> void configureResults(
      StitchResultsView<T> results, String aria, String emptyTitle, String emptyMessage) {
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(25, 50, 100);
    results.setPageSize(25);
    results.setResultCountVisible(true);
    aria(results.grid(), aria);
    results.setEmptyState(emptyTitle, emptyMessage);
  }

  static StitchSection fullSection(String title, Component content) {
    StitchSection section = new StitchSection(title);
    section.setWidthFull();
    section.setHeight(null);
    section.body().setWidthFull();
    section.body().setHeight(null);
    section.addToBody(content);
    return section;
  }

  static HorizontalLayout splitLayout(StitchSection left, StitchSection right, String rightWidth) {
    right.setWidth(rightWidth);
    right.getStyle().set("flex", "0 0 " + rightWidth);
    HorizontalLayout content = new HorizontalLayout(left, right);
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(true);
    content.setSizeFull();
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.setFlexGrow(1, left);
    content.setFlexGrow(0, right);
    return content;
  }

  static Button refreshAction(String aria, Runnable action) {
    Button refresh = aria(new Button("REFRESH", event -> action.run()), aria);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refresh);
    return refresh;
  }

  static <T> void attachOpenAction(StitchResultsView<T> results, Consumer<T> openHandler) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(results, "results");
    Objects.requireNonNull(openHandler, "openHandler");
    StitchRowActions<T> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    rowActions.addAction(StitchRowActions.Action.icon(VaadinIcon.EXTERNAL_LINK, "OPEN", openHandler::accept));
    rowActions.addColumn(results.grid());
    results.grid().addItemDoubleClickListener(event -> openHandler.accept(event.getItem()));
  }

  static boolean matches(String query, String... values) {
    if (query == null || query.isBlank()) {
      return true;
    }
    if (values == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      if (StitchResultsSearch.normalize(value).contains(query)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  static void openJson(String titlePrefix, String id, Object payload) {
    new StitchJsonDialog(titlePrefix + " - " + id, payload).open();
  }

  static String prettyJson(Object payload) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(payload);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return String.valueOf(payload);
    }
  }
}
