===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetEditorDescriptor.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;

public record StitchAssetEditorDescriptor(
    String sourceId,
    StitchAssetsScreenConfig config,
    StitchAssetsDataProvider dataProvider,
    Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass,
    DefinitionType definitionType,
    String defaultDraftName,
    StitchAssetDraftCustomizer draftCustomizer,
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor uiDescriptor) {

  public StitchAssetEditorDescriptor {
    sourceId = require(sourceId, "sourceId");
    config = Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config");
    dataProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(dataProvider, "dataProvider");
    definitionClass = Objects.requireNonNull(definitionClass, "definitionClass");
    definitionType = Objects.requireNonNull(definitionType, "definitionType");
    defaultDraftName = require(defaultDraftName, "defaultDraftName");
    draftCustomizer = draftCustomizer == null ? StitchAssetDraftCustomizer.NOOP : draftCustomizer;
    uiDescriptor = Objects.requireNonNull(uiDescriptor, "uiDescriptor");
  }

  public void customizeDraft(ObjectNode draft, String group, String name) {
    draftCustomizer.customize(draft, group, name);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetEditorDescriptors.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;

final class StitchAssetEditorDescriptors {
  private final Map<String, StitchAssetEditorDescriptor> bySourceId;

  StitchAssetEditorDescriptors(Stitch stitch, StitchAssetsDataProviders providers) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(stitch, "stitch");
    Objects.requireNonNull(providers, "providers");

    StitchAssetUiBuilder uiBuilder = new StitchAssetUiBuilder();
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetEditorDescriptor> descriptors = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchAssetSourceSpec source : StitchAssetSourceSpec.defaults()) {
      StitchAssetsScreenConfig config = StitchAssetsViewSupport.requireConfig(stitch, source.sourceId());
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor uiDescriptor =
          uiBuilder.buildDescriptor(
              source,
              config.resultsConfig().summaryFields(),
              config.editorOverrides());
      StitchAssetEditorDescriptor descriptor =
          new StitchAssetEditorDescriptor(
              source.sourceId(),
              config,
              providers.provider(source.sourceId()),
              source.definitionClass(),
              source.definitionType(),
              source.defaultDraftName(),
              source.draftCustomizer(),
              uiDescriptor);
      descriptors.put(source.sourceId().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), descriptor);
    }
    this.bySourceId = Map.copyOf(descriptors);
  }

  Optional<StitchAssetEditorDescriptor> find(String sourceId) {
    if (sourceId == null || sourceId.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.ofNullable(bySourceId.get(sourceId.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetEditorDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditorModeController;

final class StitchAssetEditorDialog extends StitchDialog {
  enum OpenMode {
    VIEW,
    EDIT,
    CREATE
  }

  private final StitchAssetEditorDescriptor descriptor;
  private final StitchAssetsEditorProvider editorProvider;
  private final StitchEditorModeController modeController = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final Consumer<Definition> onSaved;
  private final StitchAssetEditorPanel editorPanel;

  private final Button editAction = action("EDIT", "Edit definition", this::editRequested);
  private final Button saveAction = action("SAVE", "Save definition changes", this::saveRequestedFromAction);
  private final Button cancelAction = action("CANCEL", "Cancel definition editing", this::cancelRequested);

  private ObjectNode persistedDocument = null;
  private boolean createMode;
  private String entityType = "Asset";
  private String currentGroup;
  private String currentName;
  private final String preferredCreateGroup;

  StitchAssetEditorDialog(
      StitchAssetEditorDescriptor descriptor,
      StitchAssetsEditorProvider editorProvider,
      StitchAssetsRow row,
      OpenMode openMode,
      String preferredCreateGroup,
      Consumer<Definition> onSaved) {
    super("Asset");
    this.descriptor = Objects.requireNonNull(descriptor, "descriptor");
    this.editorProvider = Objects.requireNonNull(editorProvider, "editorProvider");
    this.onSaved = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onSaved, definition -> {});
    this.preferredCreateGroup = Strings.trimToNull(preferredCreateGroup);
    this.editorPanel = new StitchAssetEditorPanel(descriptor.uiDescriptor());

    addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-dialog");
    setWidth("min(1240px, 96vw)");
    setHeight("88vh");
    setMaxHeight("92vh");
    body().getStyle().set("max-height", "74vh");
    body().getStyle().set("overflow", "auto");
    body().getStyle().set("min-height", "0");
    editorPanel.setWidthFull();

    addToBody(editorPanel);
    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> editorPanel.documentCopy());
    addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", this::closeRequested);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(0, editAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(1, saveAction);
    footer().addComponentAtIndex(2, cancelAction);

    editorPanel.onDirtyChanged(
        dirty -> {
          if (dirty && modeController.isEditMode()) {
            modeController.markDirty();
          }
          refreshActions();
        });

    initializeSelection(row, openMode == null ? OpenMode.VIEW : openMode);
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void initializeSelection(StitchAssetsRow row, OpenMode mode) {
    entityType = singularize(descriptor.config().label());
    createMode = mode == OpenMode.CREATE || row == null;
    if (createMode) {
      initializeCreateDraft(row);
      modeController.enterEditMode();
      modeController.clearDirty();
      refreshActions();
      return;
    }

    String rowGroup = row == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(row.group());
    String rowName = row == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(row.name());
    if (rowGroup == null || rowName == null) {
      initializeCreateDraft(row);
      modeController.enterEditMode();
      modeController.clearDirty();
      refreshActions();
      return;
    }

    Definition loaded = editorProvider.load(descriptor.definitionClass(), rowGroup, rowName).orElse(null);
    if (loaded == null) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          entityType + " unavailable",
          "Unable to resolve the selected definition from discovery cache.");
      initializeCreateDraft(row);
      modeController.enterEditMode();
      modeController.clearDirty();
      refreshActions();
      return;
    }

    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = loaded.envelope();
    currentGroup = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group());
    currentName = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name());
    persistedDocument = editorProvider.toObjectNode(loaded);
    editorPanel.setDocument(persistedDocument);
    refreshSchemaReferenceOptions();
    if (mode == OpenMode.EDIT) {
      modeController.enterEditMode();
      modeController.clearDirty();
    } else {
      modeController.clear();
    }
  }

  private void initializeCreateDraft(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    String draftGroup = row == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(row.group());
    if (draftGroup == null) {
      draftGroup = preferredCreateGroup;
    }
    if (draftGroup == null) {
      draftGroup = "default";
    }
    String draftName = Strings.firstNonBlank(descriptor.defaultDraftName(), "new-asset");
    ObjectNode draft = editorProvider.baseDraftEnvelope(descriptor.definitionType(), draftGroup, draftName);
    descriptor.customizeDraft(draft, draftGroup, draftName);
    currentGroup = draftGroup;
    currentName = draftName;
    persistedDocument = draft.deepCopy();
    editorPanel.setDocument(persistedDocument);
    refreshSchemaReferenceOptions();
  }

  private void editRequested() {
    if (createMode) {
      return;
    }
    modeController.enterEditMode();
    modeController.clearDirty();
    editorPanel.clearDirty();
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void saveRequestedFromAction() {
    saveRequested();
  }

  private boolean saveRequested() {
    if (!modeController.isEditMode()) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      ObjectNode normalized =
          editorProvider.normalizeForSave(editorPanel.documentCopy(), descriptor.definitionType(), createMode);
      Definition parsed = editorProvider.parse(normalized, descriptor.definitionClass());
      editorProvider.save(parsed);

      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = parsed.envelope();
      currentGroup = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.group());
      currentName = Strings.trimToNull(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name());
      persistedDocument = editorProvider.toObjectNode(parsed);
      createMode = false;
      modeController.clear();
      editorPanel.setDocument(persistedDocument);
      refreshSchemaReferenceOptions();
      onSaved.accept(parsed);
      Notification.show(entityType + " saved", 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      refreshActions();
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to save " + entityType.toLowerCase(), StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error));
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void cancelRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      discardChanges();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(this::saveRequested, this::discardChanges, () -> {});
  }

  private void discardChanges() {
    if (persistedDocument != null) {
      editorPanel.setDocument(persistedDocument);
    }
    if (createMode) {
      modeController.enterEditMode();
      modeController.clearDirty();
    } else {
      modeController.clear();
    }
    refreshActions();
  }

  private void closeRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      close();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        () -> {
          if (saveRequested()) {
            close();
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        },
        () -> {
          discardChanges();
          close();
        },
        () -> {});
  }

  private void refreshActions() {
    boolean editMode = modeController.isEditMode();
    editAction.setVisible(!editMode && !createMode);
    editAction.setEnabled(!editMode && !createMode);
    saveAction.setVisible(editMode);
    saveAction.setEnabled(editMode);
    cancelAction.setVisible(editMode);
    cancelAction.setEnabled(editMode);
    editorPanel.setModes(editMode, createMode);
    String resolvedName = Strings.firstNonBlank(currentName, "draft");
    setDialogTitle(entityType + " - " + resolvedName);
  }

  private void refreshSchemaReferenceOptions() {
    editorPanel.setSchemaReferenceOptions(
        editorProvider.schemaReferenceOptions(descriptor.sourceId(), currentGroup));
  }

  private static Button action(String text, String ariaLabel, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button(text, event -> action.run());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-dialog-action-button");
    button.addClassName("stitch-btn");
    StitchActionStyles.applyByLabel(button, text);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    return button;
  }

  private static String singularize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "Asset";
    }
    String lower = normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (lower.endsWith("s") && lower.length() > 1) {
      lower = lower.substring(0, lower.length() - 1);
    }
    return Character.toUpperCase(lower.charAt(0)) + lower.substring(1);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetEditorPanel.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.JsonNodeFactory;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.details.Details;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.select.Select;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.IntegerField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.NumberField;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchBooleanToggle;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSummaryStrip;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;

final class StitchAssetEditorPanel extends VerticalLayout {
  private static final JsonNodeFactory JSON = JsonNodeFactory.instance;
  private static final List<String> OPTIONAL_PANEL_TOKENS =
      List.of(
          "tls",
          "kerberos",
          "otel",
          "semantic",
          "routing",
          "control",
          "runtime",
          "deployment",
          "entitlement",
          "delegated");

  private final StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor;
  private final StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
  private final VerticalLayout panelHost = new VerticalLayout();
  private final Set<String> visibilityControllers = new LinkedHashSet<>();

  private ObjectNode document = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
  private Consumer<Boolean> dirtyCallback = ignored -> {};
  private boolean dirty;
  private boolean editMode;
  private boolean createMode;
  private boolean refreshing;
  private String selectedBodyTabId = "overview";
  private int activeFieldGridColumns = 4;
  private final Map<String, Boolean> expandedState = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private List<StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption> schemaReferenceOptions = List.of();

  StitchAssetEditorPanel(StitchAssetUiDescriptor descriptor) {
    this.descriptor = Objects.requireNonNull(descriptor, "descriptor");

    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.8rem");
    addClassNames("stitch-asset-editor-dialog-content", "stitch-asset-editor-layout");

    summaryStrip.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-summary");
    summaryStrip.setWidthFull();

    panelHost.setPadding(false);
    panelHost.setSpacing(false);
    panelHost.setWidthFull();
    panelHost.getStyle().set("gap", "0.8rem");
    panelHost.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-panels");

    add(summaryStrip, panelHost);
    collectVisibilityControllers();
    rerender();
  }

  void onDirtyChanged(Consumer<Boolean> callback) {
    dirtyCallback = callback == null ? ignored -> {} : callback;
    dirtyCallback.accept(dirty);
  }

  void setDocument(ObjectNode value) {
    document =
        value == null
            ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode()
            : value.deepCopy();
    clearDirty();
    rerender();
  }

  ObjectNode documentCopy() {
    return document == null
        ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode()
        : document.deepCopy();
  }

  void clearDirty() {
    if (!dirty) {
      return;
    }
    dirty = false;
    dirtyCallback.accept(false);
  }

  void setModes(boolean editMode, boolean createMode) {
    this.editMode = editMode;
    this.createMode = createMode;
    rerender();
  }

  void setSchemaReferenceOptions(List<StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption> options) {
    schemaReferenceOptions =
        options == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(options.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList());
    rerender();
  }

  void selectTab(String tabId) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(tabId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return;
    }
    selectedBodyTabId = normalized;
  }

  private void rerender() {
    refreshing = true;
    try {
      renderSummary();
      renderPanels();
    } finally {
      refreshing = false;
    }
  }

  private void renderSummary() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<String> summaryFields = descriptor.summaryFields();
    if (summaryFields.isEmpty()) {
      summaryFields = List.of("group", "name", "type");
    }
    for (String path : summaryFields) {
      String value = readValue(path, true);
      if (value.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      values.put(summaryLabel(path), value);
      if (values.size() >= 5) {
        break;
      }
    }
    if (values.isEmpty()) {
      values.put("Group", readValue("group", true));
      values.put("Name", readValue("name", true));
    }
    summaryStrip.setItems(values);
    summaryStrip.setVisible(!values.isEmpty());
  }

  private void renderPanels() {
    panelHost.removeAll();
    List<PanelSpec> panels = buildPanels();
    PanelSpec envelopePanel = null;
    List<PanelSpec> bodyPanels = new ArrayList<>();
    for (PanelSpec panel : panels) {
      if (!isVisible(panel.tabRule()) || !isVisible(panel.groupRule())) {
        continue;
      }
      if (panel.envelope()) {
        envelopePanel = panel;
      } else {
        bodyPanels.add(panel);
      }
    }

    if (envelopePanel != null) {
      panelHost.add(buildPanelSection(envelopePanel, false, true, false));
    }

    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation mode = descriptor.nestedRecordPresentation();
    if (mode == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.STACKED_PANELS) {
      boolean firstVisible = true;
      for (PanelSpec panel : bodyPanels) {
        panelHost.add(buildPanelSection(panel, false, firstVisible, false));
        firstVisible = false;
      }
      panelHost.add(buildJsonSection());
      return;
    }

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    tabs.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-tabs");
    tabs.setWidthFull();
    List<PanelSpec> forcedStacked = new ArrayList<>();
    boolean selectedApplied = false;
    boolean hasAnyTab = false;
    String firstTabId = null;
    boolean firstVisible = true;
    for (PanelSpec panel : bodyPanels) {
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation panelMode =
          resolvePanelPresentation(panel);
      if (panelMode == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.STACKED_PANELS) {
        forcedStacked.add(panel);
        continue;
      }
      tabs.addTab(panel.id(), panel.label(), buildPanelSection(panel, true, firstVisible, true));
      hasAnyTab = true;
      if (firstTabId == null) {
        firstTabId = panel.id();
      }
      firstVisible = false;
      if (panel.id().equalsIgnoreCase(selectedBodyTabId)) {
        tabs.selectTab(panel.id());
        selectedApplied = true;
      }
    }

    tabs.addTab("json", "JSON", buildJsonPanel());
    if (!selectedApplied && "json".equalsIgnoreCase(selectedBodyTabId)) {
      tabs.selectTab("json");
      selectedApplied = true;
    }
    if (!selectedApplied) {
      if (hasAnyTab) {
        tabs.selectTab(firstTabId == null ? "json" : firstTabId);
      } else {
        tabs.selectTab("json");
      }
    }
    tabs.onTabChanged(
        key -> {
          if (key != null && !key.isBlank()) {
            selectedBodyTabId = key;
          }
        });
    panelHost.add(tabs);

    for (PanelSpec panel : forcedStacked) {
      panelHost.add(buildPanelSection(panel, false, firstVisible, false));
      firstVisible = false;
    }
  }

  private List<PanelSpec> buildPanels() {
    List<PanelSpec> panels = new ArrayList<>();
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab overview = findTab("overview");
    if (overview != null) {
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> envelope = new ArrayList<>();
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> overviewFields = new ArrayList<>();
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group : overview.groups()) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field : group.fields()) {
          if (field == null) {
            continue;
          }
          if ("envelope".equalsIgnoreCase(field.path()) && !field.children().isEmpty()) {
            envelope.addAll(field.children());
          } else {
            overviewFields.add(field);
          }
        }
      }
      if (!envelope.isEmpty()) {
        panels.add(
            new PanelSpec(
                "envelope",
                "",
                envelope,
                null,
                null,
                null,
                StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT,
                true,
                false));
      }
      if (!overviewFields.isEmpty()) {
        panels.add(
            new PanelSpec(
                "overview",
                "Overview",
                List.copyOf(overviewFields),
                null,
                null,
                null,
                StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT,
                false,
                false));
      }
    }

    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab semantic = null;
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : descriptor.tabs()) {
      if (tab == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if ("overview".equalsIgnoreCase(tab.id())) {
        continue;
      }
      if ("semantic".equalsIgnoreCase(tab.id())) {
        semantic = tab;
        continue;
      }
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group : tab.groups()) {
        if (group == null || group.fields().isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        panels.add(
            new PanelSpec(
                tab.id() + "-" + group.id(),
                Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(group.label()), tab.label()),
                group.fields(),
                tab.visibilityRule(),
                group.visibilityRule(),
                group.fieldGridColumns(),
                resolvePresentationOverride(group.nestedRecordPresentation(), tab.presentation()),
                false,
                false));
      }
    }

    if (semantic != null) {
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group : semantic.groups()) {
        if (group == null || group.fields().isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        panels.add(
            new PanelSpec(
                "semantic-" + group.id(),
                "Semantic",
                group.fields(),
                semantic.visibilityRule(),
                group.visibilityRule(),
                group.fieldGridColumns(),
                resolvePresentationOverride(group.nestedRecordPresentation(), semantic.presentation()),
                false,
                true));
      }
    }
    return panels;
  }

  private Component buildPanelSection(
      PanelSpec panel, boolean insideTab, boolean firstVisible, boolean tabContainer) {
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field rootStruct = rootStruct(panel.fields());
    PanelToggle toggle = resolvePanelToggle(rootStruct, panel);
    boolean enabled = toggle == null || panelEnabled(toggle);

    StitchSection section = new StitchSection(panel.envelope() ? "" : "");
    section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-panel");
    if (insideTab) {
      section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-tab-panel");
    }
    if (panel.envelope()) {
      section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-envelope-panel");
    } else {
      section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-group-section");
    }
    if (panel.semantic()) {
      section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-semantic-panel");
    }

    if (!enabled) {
      Span disabled = new Span("Disabled");
      disabled.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-disabled-note");
      section.addToBody(disabled);
    } else {
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> bodyFields =
          rootStruct != null && !rootStruct.children().isEmpty()
              ? rootStruct.children()
              : panel.fields();
      int columns = resolvePanelColumns(panel);
      activeFieldGridColumns = columns;
      FormLayout grid = panelGrid(columns);
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field : bodyFields) {
        addField(grid, field, panel.envelope(), columns);
      }
      section.addToBody(grid);
    }

    if (panel.envelope()) {
      return section;
    }

    Details details = new Details();
    details.setWidthFull();
    details.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-group");
    if (tabContainer) {
      details.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-group-in-tab");
    }
    details.setSummary(buildGroupSummary(panel, toggle, enabled));
    details.addContent(section);

    boolean expanded = resolveExpanded(panel, firstVisible, enabled);
    details.setOpened(expanded);
    details.addOpenedChangeListener(event -> expandedState.put(panel.id(), event.isOpened()));
    return details;
  }

  private Component buildJsonPanel() {
    TextArea json = new TextArea("Definition JSON");
    json.setReadOnly(true);
    json.setWidthFull();
    json.setMinHeight("24rem");
    json.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-json");
    json.setValue(pretty(document));
    return json;
  }

  private Component buildGroupSummary(PanelSpec panel, PanelToggle toggle, boolean enabled) {
    HorizontalLayout summary = new HorizontalLayout();
    summary.setPadding(false);
    summary.setSpacing(false);
    summary.setWidthFull();
    summary.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-group-summary");
    summary.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    summary.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);

    Span title = new Span(panel.label());
    title.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-group-title");
    summary.add(title);
    summary.expand(title);

    if (toggle != null) {
      StitchBooleanToggle switcher = new StitchBooleanToggle("Enabled", enabled);
      switcher.setReadOnly(!editMode);
      switcher.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-panel-switch");
      preventDetailsToggle(switcher);
      switcher.addValueChangeListener(
          event -> {
            if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || !editMode) {
              return;
            }
            applyPanelToggle(panel.id(), toggle, event.getValue());
          });
      summary.add(switcher);
    }
    return summary;
  }

  private boolean resolveExpanded(PanelSpec panel, boolean firstVisible, boolean enabled) {
    Boolean remembered = expandedState.get(panel.id());
    if (remembered != null) {
      if (!enabled) {
        return false;
      }
      return remembered;
    }
    if (!enabled) {
      return false;
    }
    if (firstVisible) {
      return true;
    }
    return isEnumDriven(panel);
  }

  private boolean isEnumDriven(PanelSpec panel) {
    if (panel == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return hasAllowedValues(panel.tabRule()) || hasAllowedValues(panel.groupRule());
  }

  private boolean hasAllowedValues(StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule rule) {
    return rule != null && rule.allowedValues() != null && !rule.allowedValues().isEmpty();
  }

  private static void preventDetailsToggle(Component component) {
    if (component == null) {
      return;
    }
    component
        .getElement()
        .executeJs(
            "this.addEventListener('click', function(e){e.stopPropagation();});"
                + "this.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){e.stopPropagation();});");
  }

  private Component buildJsonSection() {
    StitchSection section = new StitchSection("JSON");
    section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-panel");
    section.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-json-section");
    section.addToBody(buildJsonPanel());
    return section;
  }

  private int resolvePanelColumns(PanelSpec panel) {
    if (panel == null || panel.fieldGridColumns() == null) {
      return Math.max(1, descriptor.fieldGridColumns());
    }
    return Math.max(1, Math.min(6, panel.fieldGridColumns()));
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation resolvePanelPresentation(PanelSpec panel) {
    if (panel == null
        || panel.nestedRecordPresentation() == null
        || panel.nestedRecordPresentation()
            == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT) {
      return descriptor.nestedRecordPresentation();
    }
    return panel.nestedRecordPresentation();
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation resolvePresentationOverride(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation group,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation tab) {
    if (group != null && group != StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT) {
      return group;
    }
    if (tab != null && tab != StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT) {
      return tab;
    }
    return StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT;
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab findTab(String id) {
    if (id == null || id.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : descriptor.tabs()) {
      if (tab != null && id.equalsIgnoreCase(tab.id())) {
        return tab;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field rootStruct(List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> fields) {
    if (fields == null || fields.size() != 1) {
      return null;
    }
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field only = fields.get(0);
    if (only == null || only.kind() != StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.STRUCT) {
      return null;
    }
    return only;
  }

  private FormLayout panelGrid(int columns) {
    FormLayout grid = new FormLayout();
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-panel-grid");
    grid.setResponsiveSteps(
        responsiveSteps(columns).toArray(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep[0]));
    return grid;
  }

  private List<FormLayout.ResponsiveStep> responsiveSteps(int columns) {
    int normalized = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, columns));
    List<FormLayout.ResponsiveStep> steps = new ArrayList<>();
    steps.add(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1));
    if (normalized >= 2) {
      steps.add(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("42em", 2));
    }
    if (normalized >= 3) {
      steps.add(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("62em", 3));
    }
    if (normalized >= 4) {
      steps.add(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("84em", 4));
    }
    if (normalized >= 5) {
      steps.add(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("106em", 5));
    }
    if (normalized >= 6) {
      steps.add(new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("126em", 6));
    }
    return List.copyOf(steps);
  }

  private void addField(
      FormLayout grid,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field,
      boolean envelopePanel,
      int columns) {
    if (field == null || !isVisible(field.visibilityRule())) {
      return;
    }
    RenderedField rendered = renderField(field, envelopePanel);
    if (rendered == null || rendered.component() == null) {
      return;
    }
    grid.add(rendered.component());
    if (rendered.fullWidth()) {
      grid.setColspan(rendered.component(), Math.max(1, columns));
    }
  }

  private RenderedField renderField(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    return switch (field.kind()) {
      case STRUCT -> renderNestedStruct(field, envelopePanel);
      case LIST -> renderList(field, envelopePanel);
      case JSON -> renderJson(field, envelopePanel);
      case BOOLEAN -> renderBoolean(field, envelopePanel);
      case ENUM -> renderEnum(field, envelopePanel);
      case INTEGER -> renderInteger(field, envelopePanel);
      case LONG, DOUBLE -> renderDecimal(field, envelopePanel);
      case STRING -> renderString(field, envelopePanel);
    };
  }

  private RenderedField renderNestedStruct(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    if (field.children().isEmpty()) {
      return renderString(field, envelopePanel);
    }
    VerticalLayout nested = new VerticalLayout();
    nested.setPadding(false);
    nested.setSpacing(false);
    nested.setWidthFull();
    nested.getStyle().set("gap", "0.5rem");
    nested.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-nested");

    Span title = new Span(field.label());
    title.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-nested-title");
    nested.add(title);

    int columns = Math.max(1, activeFieldGridColumns);
    FormLayout childGrid = panelGrid(columns);
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field child : field.children()) {
      addField(childGrid, child, envelopePanel, columns);
    }
    nested.add(childGrid);
    return new RenderedField(nested, true);
  }

  private RenderedField renderList(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    if (field.children().isEmpty()) {
      TextArea area = new TextArea(field.label());
      area.setWidthFull();
      area.setMinHeight("7.25rem");
      area.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-field");
      area.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
      area.setValue(listAsLines(field.path()));
      area.addValueChangeListener(
          event -> {
            if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || area.isReadOnly()) {
              return;
            }
            writeListLines(field.path(), event.getValue());
            markDirty();
          });
      return new RenderedField(area, true);
    }

    VerticalLayout list = new VerticalLayout();
    list.setPadding(false);
    list.setSpacing(false);
    list.setWidthFull();
    list.getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
    list.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list");

    HorizontalLayout titleRow = new HorizontalLayout();
    titleRow.setPadding(false);
    titleRow.setSpacing(false);
    titleRow.setWidthFull();
    titleRow.getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
    titleRow.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-title-row");

    Span title = new Span(field.label());
    title.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-title");
    titleRow.add(title);

    if (!isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel)) {
      Button add = new Button("Add item");
      add.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE, ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
      add.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-add");
      add.addClickListener(
          event -> {
            ArrayNode values = arrayNode(field.path(), true);
            values.addObject();
            markDirty();
            rerender();
          });
      titleRow.add(add);
    }
    list.add(titleRow);

    ArrayNode values = arrayNode(field.path(), false);
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      Span empty = new Span("No entries");
      empty.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-empty");
      list.add(empty);
      return new RenderedField(list, true);
    }

    for (int index = 0; index < values.size(); index++) {
      VerticalLayout item = new VerticalLayout();
      item.setPadding(false);
      item.setSpacing(false);
      item.setWidthFull();
      item.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
      item.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-item");

      HorizontalLayout itemHeader = new HorizontalLayout();
      itemHeader.setPadding(false);
      itemHeader.setSpacing(false);
      itemHeader.setWidthFull();
      itemHeader.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
      itemHeader.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-item-header");
      Span itemTitle = new Span("Item " + (index + 1));
      itemTitle.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-item-title");
      itemHeader.add(itemTitle);

      if (!isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel)) {
        int removeIndex = index;
        Button remove = new Button("Remove");
        remove.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE, ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
        remove.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-list-remove");
        remove.addClickListener(
            event -> {
              ArrayNode node = arrayNode(field.path(), false);
              if (node != null && removeIndex >= 0 && removeIndex < node.size()) {
                node.remove(removeIndex);
                if (node.isEmpty()) {
                  removePath(field.path());
                }
                markDirty();
                rerender();
              }
            });
        itemHeader.add(remove);
      }
      item.add(itemHeader);

      int columns = Math.max(1, activeFieldGridColumns);
      FormLayout itemGrid = panelGrid(columns);
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field child : field.children()) {
        addField(
            itemGrid,
            toListItemField(field.path(), index, child),
            envelopePanel,
            columns);
      }
      item.add(itemGrid);
      list.add(item);
    }
    return new RenderedField(list, true);
  }

  private RenderedField renderJson(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    TextArea area = new TextArea(field.label());
    area.setWidthFull();
    area.setMinHeight("7.25rem");
    area.addClassName("stitch-asset-editor-json-field");
    area.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
    JsonNode node = readNode(field.path());
    area.setValue(node == null || node.isNull() ? "" : pretty(node));
    area.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || area.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          String raw = Strings.trimToNull(event.getValue());
          if (raw == null) {
            removePath(field.path());
            markDirty();
            return;
          }
          try {
            JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(raw);
            setValue(field.path(), parsed);
            markDirty();
          } catch (Exception ignored) {
            // Keep current value if parse fails.
          }
        });
    return new RenderedField(area, true);
  }

  private RenderedField renderBoolean(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    StitchBooleanToggle toggle = new StitchBooleanToggle(field.label(), readBoolean(field.path()));
    toggle.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
    toggle.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || toggle.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          setValue(field.path(), JSON.booleanNode(Boolean.TRUE.equals(event.getValue())));
          markDirty();
          handleVisibilityChange(field.path());
        });
    return new RenderedField(toggle, false);
  }

  private RenderedField renderEnum(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    Select<String> select = new Select<>();
    select.setWidthFull();
    select.setLabel(field.label());
    select.setItems(field.enumValues());
    select.setEmptySelectionAllowed(true);
    select.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));

    String current = readValue(field.path(), false);
    if (!current.isBlank() && field.enumValues().stream().noneMatch(value -> value.equalsIgnoreCase(current))) {
      ArrayList<String> items = new ArrayList<>(field.enumValues());
      items.add(current);
      select.setItems(items);
    }
    if (!current.isBlank()) {
      select.setValue(current);
    }
    select.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || select.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          String value = Strings.trimToNull(event.getValue());
          if (value == null) {
            removePath(field.path());
          } else {
            setValue(field.path(), JSON.textNode(value));
          }
          markDirty();
          handleVisibilityChange(field.path());
        });
    return new RenderedField(select, false);
  }

  private RenderedField renderInteger(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    IntegerField input = new IntegerField(field.label());
    input.setWidthFull();
    input.setStepButtonsVisible(true);
    input.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
    JsonNode current = readNode(field.path());
    input.setValue(current != null && current.isNumber() ? current.intValue() : null);
    input.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || input.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          Integer value = event.getValue();
          if (value == null) {
            removePath(field.path());
          } else {
            setValue(field.path(), JSON.numberNode(value));
          }
          markDirty();
        });
    return new RenderedField(input, false);
  }

  private RenderedField renderDecimal(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    NumberField input = new NumberField(field.label());
    input.setWidthFull();
    input.setStepButtonsVisible(true);
    input.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
    JsonNode current = readNode(field.path());
    input.setValue(current != null && current.isNumber() ? current.doubleValue() : null);
    input.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || input.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          Double value = event.getValue();
          if (value == null) {
            removePath(field.path());
            markDirty();
            return;
          }
          if (field.kind() == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.LONG) {
            setValue(field.path(), JSON.numberNode(Math.round(value)));
          } else {
            setValue(field.path(), JSON.numberNode(value));
          }
          markDirty();
        });
    return new RenderedField(input, false);
  }

  private RenderedField renderString(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    if (isSchemaReferenceField(field.path())) {
      return renderSchemaReference(field, envelopePanel);
    }
    String value = readValue(field.path(), false);
    boolean multiLine = isLongTextField(field.path(), value);
    if (multiLine) {
      TextArea area = new TextArea(field.label());
      area.setWidthFull();
      area.setMinHeight("7.25rem");
      area.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
      area.setValue(value);
      area.addValueChangeListener(
          event -> {
            if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || area.isReadOnly()) {
              return;
            }
            writeText(field.path(), event.getValue());
            markDirty();
          });
      return new RenderedField(area, true);
    }

    TextField input = new TextField(field.label());
    input.setWidthFull();
    input.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
    input.setValue(value);
    input.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || input.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          writeText(field.path(), event.getValue());
          markDirty();
        });
    return new RenderedField(input, false);
  }

  private RenderedField renderSchemaReference(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    Select<StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption> select = new Select<>();
    select.setWidthFull();
    select.setLabel(field.label());
    select.setItemLabelGenerator(
        option -> option == null ? "" : Strings.firstNonBlank(option.label(), option.value(), ""));
    select.setReadOnly(isReadOnly(field, envelopePanel));
    select.setEmptySelectionAllowed(true);

    List<StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption> items = new ArrayList<>(schemaReferenceOptions);
    String current = readValue(field.path(), false);
    StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption currentOption = schemaReferenceOption(current);
    if (currentOption == null && !current.isBlank()) {
      currentOption = new StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption(current, current);
      items.add(currentOption);
    }
    select.setItems(items);
    if (currentOption != null) {
      select.setValue(currentOption);
    }

    select.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient() || refreshing || select.isReadOnly()) {
            return;
          }
          StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption option = event.getValue();
          String value = Strings.trimToNull(option == null ? null : option.value());
          if (value == null) {
            removePath(field.path());
          } else {
            setValue(field.path(), JSON.textNode(value));
          }
          markDirty();
        });
    return new RenderedField(select, false);
  }

  private void collectVisibilityControllers() {
    visibilityControllers.clear();
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Tab tab : descriptor.tabs()) {
      if (tab == null) {
        continue;
      }
      collectController(tab.visibilityRule());
      for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Group group : tab.groups()) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        collectController(group.visibilityRule());
        for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field : group.fields()) {
          collectControllers(field);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private void collectControllers(StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field) {
    if (field == null) {
      return;
    }
    collectController(field.visibilityRule());
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field child : field.children()) {
      collectControllers(child);
    }
  }

  private void collectController(StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule rule) {
    if (rule == null) {
      return;
    }
    String path = normalizePath(rule.controllerPath());
    if (!path.isBlank()) {
      visibilityControllers.add(path);
    }
  }

  private boolean isVisible(StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule rule) {
    if (rule == null) {
      return true;
    }
    String current = readValue(rule.controllerPath(), true);
    return rule.matches(current);
  }

  private String summaryLabel(String key) {
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field direct = descriptor.field(key);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct.label();
    }
    StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field envelopeAlias = descriptor.field("envelope." + key);
    if (envelopeAlias != null) {
      return envelopeAlias.label();
    }
    return display(key);
  }

  private boolean isReadOnly(StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field, boolean envelopePanel) {
    if (!editMode || field == null) {
      return true;
    }
    if (field.readOnly()) {
      return true;
    }
    if (envelopePanel || field.path().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("envelope.")) {
      if (createMode) {
        return false;
      }
      return !isEnvelopeEnabledField(field.path());
    }
    return false;
  }

  private boolean isEnvelopeEnabledField(String path) {
    return "envelope.enabled".equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(path), ""));
  }

  private boolean isSchemaReferenceField(String path) {
    String normalized = normalizePath(path);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return false;
    }
    return normalized.endsWith("schemaref")
        || normalized.contains(".schemaref")
        || normalized.endsWith("schemaid")
        || normalized.contains(".schemaid");
  }

  private StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption schemaReferenceOption(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (StitchAssetsEditorProvider.SchemaReferenceOption option : schemaReferenceOptions) {
      if (option != null && normalized.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(option.value(), ""))) {
        return option;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private boolean isLongTextField(String path, String value) {
    String normalized = normalizePath(path);
    if (normalized.contains("schema")
        || normalized.contains("json")
        || normalized.contains("sql")
        || normalized.contains("description")
        || normalized.contains("doc")
        || normalized.contains("notes")) {
      return true;
    }
    return value != null && value.length() > 120;
  }

  private String readValue(String path, boolean withEnvelopeFallback) {
    JsonNode node = readNode(path);
    if ((node == null || node.isNull()) && withEnvelopeFallback && path != null && !path.contains(".")) {
      node = readNode("envelope." + path);
    }
    if (node == null || node.isNull()) {
      return "";
    }
    if (node.isTextual()) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(node.asText()), "");
    }
    if (node.isValueNode()) {
      return node.asText();
    }
    return node.toString();
  }

  private boolean readBoolean(String path) {
    JsonNode node = readNode(path);
    if (node == null || node.isNull()) {
      return false;
    }
    if (node.isBoolean()) {
      return node.booleanValue();
    }
    return "true".equalsIgnoreCase(node.asText(""));
  }

  private JsonNode readNode(String path) {
    List<PathToken> tokens = tokenize(path);
    if (tokens.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode current = document;
    for (PathToken token : tokens) {
      if (!(current instanceof ObjectNode objectNode)) {
        return null;
      }
      JsonNode next = objectNode.get(token.name());
      if (next == null) {
        return null;
      }
      if (token.index() != null) {
        if (!(next instanceof ArrayNode array) || token.index() < 0 || token.index() >= array.size()) {
          return null;
        }
        next = array.get(token.index());
      }
      current = next;
    }
    return current;
  }

  private void writeText(String path, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      removePath(path);
      return;
    }
    setValue(path, JSON.textNode(normalized));
  }

  private void writeListLines(String path, String value) {
    String raw = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (raw == null) {
      removePath(path);
      return;
    }
    ArrayNode array = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createArrayNode();
    for (String line : raw.split("\\R")) {
      String item = Strings.trimToNull(line);
      if (item != null) {
        array.add(item);
      }
    }
    if (array.isEmpty()) {
      removePath(path);
    } else {
      setValue(path, array);
    }
  }

  private String listAsLines(String path) {
    JsonNode node = readNode(path);
    if (!(node instanceof ArrayNode array) || array.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (JsonNode item : array) {
      if (item == null || item.isNull()) {
        continue;
      }
      values.add(item.isValueNode() ? item.asText() : item.toString());
    }
    return String.join("\n", values);
  }

  private ArrayNode arrayNode(String path, boolean create) {
    JsonNode current = readNode(path);
    if (current instanceof ArrayNode array) {
      return array;
    }
    if (!create) {
      return null;
    }
    ArrayNode created = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createArrayNode();
    setValue(path, created);
    JsonNode refreshed = readNode(path);
    return refreshed instanceof ArrayNode array ? array : created;
  }

  private void removePath(String path) {
    setValue(path, null);
  }

  private void setValue(String path, JsonNode value) {
    List<PathToken> tokens = tokenize(path);
    if (tokens.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    ObjectNode parent = resolveParent(tokens, value != null);
    if (parent == null) {
      return;
    }
    PathToken leaf = tokens.get(tokens.size() - 1);
    if (leaf.index() == null) {
      if (value == null) {
        parent.remove(leaf.name());
      } else {
        parent.set(leaf.name(), value);
      }
      return;
    }

    ArrayNode array = ensureArray(parent, leaf.name(), value != null);
    if (array == null) {
      return;
    }
    int index = leaf.index();
    if (index < 0) {
      return;
    }
    if (value == null) {
      if (index < array.size()) {
        array.remove(index);
      }
      if (array.isEmpty()) {
        parent.remove(leaf.name());
      }
      return;
    }
    while (array.size() <= index) {
      array.addNull();
    }
    array.set(index, value);
  }

  private ObjectNode resolveParent(List<PathToken> tokens, boolean create) {
    ObjectNode current = document;
    for (int i = 0; i < tokens.size() - 1; i++) {
      PathToken token = tokens.get(i);
      if (token.index() == null) {
        JsonNode next = current.get(token.name());
        if (next == null || next.isNull()) {
          if (!create) {
            return null;
          }
          ObjectNode created = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
          current.set(token.name(), created);
          current = created;
          continue;
        }
        if (!(next instanceof ObjectNode objectNode)) {
          if (!create) {
            return null;
          }
          ObjectNode replacement = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
          current.set(token.name(), replacement);
          current = replacement;
          continue;
        }
        current = objectNode;
        continue;
      }

      ArrayNode array = ensureArray(current, token.name(), create);
      if (array == null) {
        return null;
      }
      int index = token.index();
      if (index < 0) {
        return null;
      }
      while (array.size() <= index) {
        array.addObject();
      }
      JsonNode item = array.get(index);
      if (item instanceof ObjectNode objectNode) {
        current = objectNode;
      } else if (create) {
        ObjectNode replacement = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
        array.set(index, replacement);
        current = replacement;
      } else {
        return null;
      }
    }
    return current;
  }

  private ArrayNode ensureArray(ObjectNode parent, String field, boolean create) {
    if (parent == null || field == null || field.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode current = parent.get(field);
    if (current instanceof ArrayNode array) {
      return array;
    }
    if (!create) {
      return null;
    }
    ArrayNode created = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createArrayNode();
    parent.set(field, created);
    return created;
  }

  private List<PathToken> tokenize(String path) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<PathToken> tokens = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String segment : normalized.split("\\.")) {
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(segment);
      if (name == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Integer index = null;
      int open = name.indexOf('[');
      int close = name.endsWith("]") ? name.lastIndexOf(']') : -1;
      if (open > 0 && close > open) {
        String rawIndex = name.substring(open + 1, close).trim();
        name = name.substring(0, open).trim();
        if (!rawIndex.isBlank()) {
          try {
            index = Integer.parseInt(rawIndex);
          } catch (NumberFormatException ignored) {
            index = null;
          }
        }
      }
      if (!name.isBlank()) {
        tokens.add(new PathToken(name, index));
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(tokens);
  }

  private void markDirty() {
    if (dirty) {
      return;
    }
    dirty = true;
    dirtyCallback.accept(true);
  }

  private void handleVisibilityChange(String path) {
    String normalized = normalizePath(path);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    if (visibilityControllers.contains(normalized)) {
      rerender();
    }
  }

  private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field toListItemField(
      String listPath, int index, StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field field) {
    String indexedPath = indexedPath(listPath, index, field.path());
    List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> children = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field child : field.children()) {
      children.add(toListItemField(listPath, index, child));
    }
    return new StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field(
        indexedPath,
        field.label(),
        field.kind(),
        field.javaType(),
        field.genericType(),
        field.enumValues(),
        field.readOnly(),
        children,
        field.visibilityRule());
  }

  private static String indexedPath(String listPath, int index, String childPath) {
    String prefix = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(listPath), "");
    String child = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(childPath), "");
    String marker = prefix + ".";
    if (!child.startsWith(marker)) {
      return child;
    }
    String suffix = child.substring(marker.length());
    return prefix + "[" + Math.max(0, index) + "]." + suffix;
  }

  private PanelToggle resolvePanelToggle(
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field rootStruct, PanelSpec panel) {
    if (rootStruct == null || panel.envelope()) {
      return null;
    }
    String structPath = normalizePath(rootStruct.path());
    if (structPath.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field child : rootStruct.children()) {
      if (child == null || child.kind() != StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Kind.BOOLEAN) {
        continue;
      }
      String childPath = normalizePath(child.path());
      if (childPath.equals(structPath + ".enabled")) {
        return new PanelToggle(PanelToggle.Mode.BOOLEAN_FIELD, child.path());
      }
    }
    for (String token : OPTIONAL_PANEL_TOKENS) {
      if (structPath.contains(token)) {
        return new PanelToggle(PanelToggle.Mode.STRUCT_PRESENCE, rootStruct.path());
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private boolean panelEnabled(PanelToggle toggle) {
    if (toggle == null) {
      return true;
    }
    return switch (toggle.mode()) {
      case BOOLEAN_FIELD -> readBoolean(toggle.path());
      case STRUCT_PRESENCE -> {
        JsonNode node = readNode(toggle.path());
        yield node != null && !node.isNull();
      }
    };
  }

  private void applyPanelToggle(String panelId, PanelToggle toggle, boolean enabled) {
    if (toggle == null) {
      return;
    }
    switch (toggle.mode()) {
      case BOOLEAN_FIELD -> {
        String parentPath = parentPath(toggle.path());
        if (enabled) {
          ensureObject(parentPath);
        }
        setValue(toggle.path(), JSON.booleanNode(enabled));
      }
      case STRUCT_PRESENCE -> {
        if (enabled) {
          ensureObject(toggle.path());
        } else {
          removePath(toggle.path());
        }
      }
    }
    if (panelId != null && !panelId.isBlank()) {
      expandedState.put(panelId, enabled);
    }
    markDirty();
    rerender();
  }

  private void ensureObject(String path) {
    if (Strings.trimToNull(path) == null) {
      return;
    }
    JsonNode current = readNode(path);
    if (current instanceof ObjectNode) {
      return;
    }
    setValue(path, DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode());
  }

  private static String parentPath(String path) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "";
    }
    int lastDot = normalized.lastIndexOf('.');
    if (lastDot <= 0) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, lastDot);
  }

  private static String normalizePath(String path) {
    if (path == null || path.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return path.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String display(String key) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "Field";
    }
    String spaced = normalized.replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ').replace('.', ' ');
    spaced = spaced.replaceAll("([a-z])([A-Z])", "$1 $2");
    if (spaced.isBlank()) {
      return "Field";
    }
    return spaced.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + spaced.substring(1);
  }

  private static String pretty(JsonNode node) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(node);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return node == null ? "" : node.toString();
    }
  }

  private record PanelSpec(
      String id,
      String label,
      List<StitchAssetUiDescriptor.Field> fields,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule tabRule,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.VisibilityRule groupRule,
      Integer fieldGridColumns,
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation,
      boolean envelope,
      boolean semantic) {}

  private record RenderedField(Component component, boolean fullWidth) {}

  private record PathToken(String name, Integer index) {}

  private record PanelToggle(Mode mode, String path) {
    private enum Mode {
      BOOLEAN_FIELD,
      STRUCT_PRESENCE
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetResultsConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;

public final class StitchAssetResultsConfig {
  private final List<StitchAssetsColumn> visibleFields;
  private final String summaryLabel;
  private final List<String> summaryFields;

  private StitchAssetResultsConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.visibleFields = List.copyOf(builder.visibleFields);
    this.summaryLabel = optional(builder.summaryLabel);
    this.summaryFields = List.copyOf(builder.summaryFields);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public List<StitchAssetsColumn> visibleFields() {
    return visibleFields;
  }

  public String summaryLabel() {
    return summaryLabel;
  }

  public List<String> summaryFields() {
    return summaryFields;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final List<StitchAssetsColumn> visibleFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private String summaryLabel = "Summary";
    private final List<String> summaryFields = new ArrayList<>();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withVisibleFields(List<StitchAssetsColumn> columns) {
      visibleFields.clear();
      if (columns != null) {
        for (StitchAssetsColumn column : columns) {
          if (column == null) {
            continue;
          }
          visibleFields.add(new StitchAssetsColumn(normalize(column.key()), column.label()));
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addVisibleField(String key, String label) {
      String normalized = normalize(key);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        visibleFields.add(new StitchAssetsColumn(normalized, label));
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryLabel(String value) {
      summaryLabel = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryFields(List<String> fields) {
      summaryFields.clear();
      if (fields != null) {
        LinkedHashSet<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>();
        for (String field : fields) {
          String normalized = normalize(field);
          if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
            deduped.add(normalized);
          }
        }
        summaryFields.addAll(deduped);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryFields(String... fields) {
      summaryFields.clear();
      if (fields != null) {
        LinkedHashSet<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>();
        for (String field : fields) {
          String normalized = normalize(field);
          if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
            deduped.add(normalized);
          }
        }
        summaryFields.addAll(deduped);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public StitchAssetResultsConfig build() {
      return new StitchAssetResultsConfig(this);
    }
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static List<StitchAssetsColumn> mergeVisibleFields(
      List<StitchAssetsColumn> defaults, List<String> extraFields, List<String> explicitOrder) {
    java.util.LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetsColumn> merged = new java.util.LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (defaults != null) {
      for (StitchAssetsColumn column : defaults) {
        if (column == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = normalize(column.key());
        if (key.isBlank() || isReservedLeadingField(key)) {
          continue;
        }
        merged.putIfAbsent(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), new StitchAssetsColumn(key, column.label()));
      }
    }
    if (extraFields != null) {
      for (String field : extraFields) {
        String key = normalize(field);
        if (key.isBlank() || isReservedLeadingField(key)) {
          continue;
        }
        merged.putIfAbsent(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), new StitchAssetsColumn(key, null));
      }
    }
    if (explicitOrder == null || explicitOrder.isEmpty()) {
      return List.copyOf(merged.values());
    }
    for (String field : explicitOrder) {
      String key = normalize(field);
      if (key.isBlank() || isReservedLeadingField(key)) {
        continue;
      }
      merged.putIfAbsent(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), new StitchAssetsColumn(key, null));
    }
    List<StitchAssetsColumn> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> used = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String field : explicitOrder) {
      String key = normalize(field).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      StitchAssetsColumn column = merged.get(key);
      if (column == null || !used.add(key)) {
        continue;
      }
      ordered.add(column);
    }
    for (java.util.Map.Entry<String, StitchAssetsColumn> entry : merged.entrySet()) {
      if (used.add(entry.getKey())) {
        ordered.add(entry.getValue());
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  public static List<String> normalizeFieldKeys(List<String> keys) {
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = normalize(key);
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  public static boolean isReservedLeadingField(String key) {
    String normalized = normalize(key).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "enabled", "group", "name", "summary", "actions" -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsColumn.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.Locale;

public record StitchAssetsColumn(String key, String label) {
  public StitchAssetsColumn {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("key is required");
    }
    key = key.trim();
    label = (label == null || label.isBlank()) ? toDisplayLabel(key) : label.trim();
  }

  private static String toDisplayLabel(String key) {
    String normalized = key.replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ').replace('.', ' ').trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + normalized.substring(1);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

@Route(value = "assets/configs", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchAssetsConfigsView extends StitchAssetsView {
  public StitchAssetsConfigsView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, Stitch stitch, StitchAssetsDataProviders providers) {
    super(runtimeContext, stitch, providers, StitchAssetsFeature.CONFIGS);
    addClassName("stitch-assets-configs-page");
    body().addClassName("stitch-assets-configs-body");
    filtersBar().addClassName("stitch-assets-configs-filters");
    resultsView().addClassName("stitch-assets-configs-results");
    resultsView().grid().addClassName("stitch-assets-configs-grid");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAssetsRow> grid) {
    super.configureGrid(grid);
    tuneColumn(grid, "enabled", "7.3rem", 0, false);
    tuneColumn(grid, "group", "11.5rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "name", "14rem", 2, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "configId", "15rem", 2, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "schemaRef", "13.5rem", 2, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "domain", "10.5rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "resourceId", "16rem", 2, true);
  }

  private static void tuneColumn(
      Grid<StitchAssetsRow> grid, String key, String width, int flexGrow, boolean resizable) {
    if (grid == null || key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    grid.getColumns().stream()
        .filter(column -> key.equalsIgnoreCase(column.getKey()))
        .findFirst()
        .ifPresent(
            column -> {
              if (Strings.isNotBlank(width)) {
                column.setAutoWidth(false);
                column.setWidth(width);
              }
              column.setFlexGrow(Math.max(0, flexGrow));
              column.setResizable(resizable);
            });
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public interface StitchAssetsDataProvider {

  List<StitchAssetsRow> loadRows();

    return Map.of();
