===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsDataProviders.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public class StitchAssetsDataProviders {
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final Map<String, StitchAssetsDataProvider> providers;

  public StitchAssetsDataProviders(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetsDataProvider> byId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchAssetSourceSpec source : StitchAssetSourceSpec.defaults()) {
      byId.put(
          source.sourceId().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT),
          new SimpleProvider(source.sourceId(), () -> loadRows(source), Map.of()));
    }
    this.providers = Map.copyOf(byId);
  }

  public StitchAssetsDataProvider provider(String sourceId) {
    String normalized = sourceId == null ? "" : sourceId.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    StitchAssetsDataProvider provider = providers.get(normalized);
    if (provider == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unknown assets source: " + sourceId);
    }
    return provider;
  }

  private List<StitchAssetsRow> loadRows(StitchAssetSourceSpec source) {
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = session().internal().discoveryCache();
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Definition> definitions = discoveryCache.allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    Map<String, StitchAssetsRow> rows = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Definition definition : definitions) {
      if (definition == null || !source.definitionClass().isInstance(definition)) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
      if (envelope == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String group = normalize(envelope.group());
      String name = normalize(envelope.name());
      if (group.isBlank() || name.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }

      Map<String, Object> fields = flattenFields(definition, envelope);
      StitchAssetsRow candidate =
          new StitchAssetsRow(
              String.join("::", normalize(source.sourceId()), group, name),
              Boolean.TRUE.equals(envelope.enabled()),
              group,
              name,
              fields,
              definition);

      StitchAssetsRow current = rows.get(candidate.id());
      if (current == null || isNewer(definition, current.sourceObject())) {
        rows.put(candidate.id(), candidate);
      }
    }
    return rows.values().stream().sorted(StitchAssetsSort.defaultComparator()).toList();
  }

  private Map<String, Object> flattenFields(Definition definition, DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("type", envelope == null || envelope.type() == null ? "" : envelope.type().name());
    fields.put("lifecycleStatus", normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.lifecycleStatus()));
    fields.put("updated", normalize(envelope == null ? null : envelope.updatedTimeUtc()));

    JsonNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().valueToTree(definition);
    if (root instanceof ObjectNode objectNode) {
      objectNode.fields().forEachRemaining(entry -> flattenNode(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue(), fields));
    }
    return Map.copyOf(fields);
  }

  private void flattenNode(String path, JsonNode node, Map<String, Object> target) {
    if (path == null || path.isBlank() || node == null || node.isNull()) {
      return;
    }
    if (path.equalsIgnoreCase("envelope")) {
      return;
    }
    if (node.isValueNode()) {
      target.put(path, node.isTextual() ? normalize(node.asText()) : node.asText());
      return;
    }
    if (node.isArray()) {
      if (node.isEmpty()) {
        target.put(path, "");
        return;
      }
      boolean scalarArray = true;
      for (JsonNode item : node) {
        if (item == null || !item.isValueNode()) {
          scalarArray = false;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (scalarArray) {
        String joined =
            java.util.stream.StreamSupport.stream(node.spliterator(), false)
                .map(item -> normalize(item.asText()))
                .filter(value -> !value.isBlank())
                .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.joining(", "));
        target.put(path, joined);
      } else {
        target.put(path, node.toString());
      }
      return;
    }
    if (node.isObject()) {
      node.fields()
          .forEachRemaining(entry -> flattenNode(path + "." + entry.getKey(), entry.getValue(), target));
    }
  }

  private SessionImpl session() {
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (current instanceof SessionImpl resolved) {
      return resolved;
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
  }

  private static boolean isNewer(Definition current, Object existing) {
    if (!(existing instanceof Definition existingDefinition)) {
      return true;
    }
    long currentEpoch = recencyEpoch(current == null ? null : current.envelope());
    long existingEpoch = recencyEpoch(existingDefinition.envelope());
    return currentEpoch > existingEpoch;
  }

  private static long recencyEpoch(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    long updated = parseEpoch(envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    if (updated > Long.MIN_VALUE) {
      return updated;
    }
    return parseEpoch(envelope.createdTimeUtc());
  }

  private static long parseEpoch(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(value.trim()).toEpochMilli();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  private record SimpleProvider(
      String id, Supplier<List<StitchAssetsRow>> loader, Map<String, String> labels)
      implements StitchAssetsDataProvider {
    private SimpleProvider {
      Objects.requireNonNull(id, "id");
      Objects.requireNonNull(loader, "loader");
      labels = labels == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(labels);
    }

    @Override
    public List<StitchAssetsRow> loadRows() {
      List<StitchAssetsRow> rows = loader.get();
      return rows == null ? List.of() : rows;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> fieldLabels() {
      return labels;
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsEditorProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchGroupAccess;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

/** Shared discovery-cache load/save helper for asset editor screens. */
public final class StitchAssetsEditorProvider {
  private static final String DEFAULT_ACTOR = "stitch";

  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchGroupAccess groupAccess;

  public StitchAssetsEditorProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    if (runtimeContext == null || runtimeContext.session() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Runtime session is required");
    }
    this.runtimeContext = runtimeContext;
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.groupAccess = new StitchGroupAccess(current);
  }

  public <T extends Definition> Optional<T> load(
      Class<T> definitionClass, String group, String name) {
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    return cache.get(definitionClass, require(group, "group"), require(name, "name"));
  }

  public <T extends Definition> T parse(String json, Class<T> definitionClass) throws Exception {
    JsonNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(require(json, "json"));
    return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().treeToValue(root, definitionClass);
  }

  public <T extends Definition> T parse(JsonNode root, Class<T> definitionClass) throws Exception {
    if (root == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("json is required");
    }
    return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().treeToValue(root, definitionClass);
  }

  public <T extends Definition> void save(T definition) {
    requireCache().upsert(definition);
  }

  public ObjectNode toObjectNode(Object payload) {
    if (payload == null) {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    }
    JsonNode tree = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().valueToTree(payload);
    if (tree instanceof ObjectNode objectNode) {
      return objectNode.deepCopy();
    }
    return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
  }

  public ObjectNode baseDraftEnvelope(DefinitionType type, String group, String name) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(group), "default");
    String resolvedName = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(name), "new-asset");
    String now = Instant.now().toString();

    ObjectNode root = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
    ObjectNode envelope = root.putObject("envelope");
    envelope.put("group", resolvedGroup);
    envelope.put("type", (type == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : type).name());
    envelope.put("name", resolvedName);
    envelope.put("uuid", UUID.randomUUID().toString());
    envelope.put("enabled", true);
    envelope.put("lifecycleStatus", "ACTIVE");
    envelope.put("createdTimeUtc", now);
    envelope.put("createdBy", DEFAULT_ACTOR);
    envelope.put("updatedTimeUtc", now);
    envelope.put("updatedBy", DEFAULT_ACTOR);
    return root;
  }

  public ObjectNode normalizeForSave(
      ObjectNode document, DefinitionType definitionType, boolean createMode) {
    ObjectNode root =
        document == null ? DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode() : document.deepCopy();
    JsonNode envelopeNode = root.get("envelope");
    ObjectNode envelope =
        envelopeNode instanceof ObjectNode existingEnvelope ? existingEnvelope : root.putObject("envelope");
    String now = Instant.now().toString();

    String group = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(envelope.path("group").asText(null)), "default");
    String name = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(envelope.path("name").asText(null)), "new-asset");
    envelope.put("group", group);
    envelope.put("name", name);
    envelope.put("type", (definitionType == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : definitionType).name());
    if (Strings.trimToNull(envelope.path("uuid").asText(null)) == null) {
      envelope.put("uuid", UUID.randomUUID().toString());
    }
    if (!envelope.has("enabled") || envelope.path("enabled").isNull()) {
      envelope.put("enabled", true);
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(envelope.path("lifecycleStatus").asText(null)) == null) {
      envelope.put("lifecycleStatus", "ACTIVE");
    }

    if (createMode || Strings.trimToNull(envelope.path("createdTimeUtc").asText(null)) == null) {
      envelope.put("createdTimeUtc", now);
    }
    if (createMode || Strings.trimToNull(envelope.path("createdBy").asText(null)) == null) {
      envelope.put("createdBy", DEFAULT_ACTOR);
    }
    envelope.put("updatedTimeUtc", now);
    envelope.put("updatedBy", DEFAULT_ACTOR);
    return root;
  }

  public String pretty(Object value) {
    try {
      return DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(value);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return value == null ? "{}" : String.valueOf(value);
    }
  }

  public List<SchemaReferenceOption> schemaReferenceOptions(String sourceId, String preferredGroup) {
    List<SchemaCandidate> visible = visibleSchemaCandidates();
    if (visible.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }

    String normalizedSource = normalize(sourceId);
    List<SchemaCandidate> relevant = new ArrayList<>();
    for (SchemaCandidate candidate : visible) {
      if (isRelevantSchema(candidate, normalizedSource)) {
        relevant.add(candidate);
      }
    }
    if (relevant.isEmpty()) {
      relevant = visible;
    }

    String preferred = normalize(preferredGroup);
    relevant.sort(
        Comparator.<SchemaCandidate, Integer>comparing(
                option -> preferred.isBlank() || !preferred.equalsIgnoreCase(normalize(option.group())) ? 1 : 0)
            .thenComparing(option -> normalize(option.label())));

    LinkedHashMap<String, SchemaReferenceOption> deduped = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (SchemaCandidate candidate : relevant) {
      deduped.putIfAbsent(
          normalize(candidate.value()), new SchemaReferenceOption(candidate.value(), candidate.label()));
    }
    return List.copyOf(deduped.values());
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireCache() {
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not available");
    }
    return cache;
  }

  private List<SchemaCandidate> visibleSchemaCandidates() {
    List<String> visibleGroups = visibleGroups();
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireCache();
    List<Definition> definitions = cache.allDefinitions();
    if (definitions == null || definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<SchemaCandidate> candidates = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Definition definition : definitions) {
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionSchema schema)) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = schema.envelope();
      if (envelope == null) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("schema.envelope is required");
      }
      String group = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope.group(), "schema.envelope.group");
      String name = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope.name(), "schema.envelope.name");
      if (!visibleGroups.isEmpty() && !containsIgnoreCase(visibleGroups, group)) {
        continue;
      }
      String value = "schema:" + group + "/" + name;
      String label = group + " / " + name;
      candidates.add(new SchemaCandidate(value, label, group, schema.schemaType(), schema.schemaUsage()));
    }
    return List.copyOf(candidates);
  }

  private List<String> visibleGroups() {
    String subject =
        StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
    try {
      StitchGroupAccess.GroupScope scope = groupAccess.scopeForSubject(subject);
      if (scope == null || scope.visibleGroups() == null || scope.visibleGroups().isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      return List.copyOf(scope.visibleGroups());
    } catch (RuntimeException ignored) {
      return List.of();
    }
  }

  private boolean isRelevantSchema(SchemaCandidate candidate, String sourceId) {
    if (candidate == null || sourceId == null || sourceId.isBlank()) {
      return true;
    }
    DefinitionSchema.SchemaType type = candidate.type();
    DefinitionSchema.SchemaUsage usage = candidate.usage();
    return switch (sourceId) {
      case StitchAssetsFeature.CONFIGS -> type == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.CONFIG;
      case StitchAssetsFeature.SERVICES ->
          usage == DefinitionSchema.SchemaUsage.SERVICE
              || type == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.TRANSPORT;
      case StitchAssetsFeature.DATASETS, StitchAssetsFeature.INGESTION ->
          type == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.TABULAR
              || type == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.MAPPING;
      case StitchAssetsFeature.STREAMS ->
          type == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.TRANSPORT
              || type == DefinitionSchema.SchemaType.MAPPING;
      default -> true;
    };
  }

  private static boolean containsIgnoreCase(List<String> values, String value) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String candidate : values) {
      if (candidate != null && value.equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.trim())) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  public record SchemaReferenceOption(String value, String label) {}

  private record SchemaCandidate(
      String value,
      String label,
      String group,
      DefinitionSchema.SchemaType type,
      DefinitionSchema.SchemaUsage usage) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchAssetsFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "assets";
  public static final String APPS = "apps";
  public static final String SERVICES = "services";
  public static final String CONNECTIONS = "connections";
  public static final String INGESTION = "ingestion";
  public static final String DATASETS = "datasets";
  public static final String STREAMS = "streams";
  public static final String CONFIGS = "configs";
  public static final String SCHEMAS = "schemas";
  public static final String ENTRY_APPS = "assets.apps";
  public static final String ENTRY_SERVICES = "assets.services";
  public static final String ENTRY_CONNECTIONS = "assets.connections";
  public static final String ENTRY_INGESTION = "assets.ingestion";
  public static final String ENTRY_DATASETS = "assets.datasets";
  public static final String ENTRY_STREAMS = "assets.streams";
  public static final String ENTRY_CONFIGS = "assets.configs";
  public static final String ENTRY_SCHEMAS = "assets.schemas";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final Map<String, StitchAssetsScreenConfig> screens;

  private StitchAssetsFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;

    StitchAssetUiBuilder uiBuilder = new StitchAssetUiBuilder();
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetsScreenConfig> configured = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchAssetSourceSpec source : StitchAssetSourceSpec.defaults()) {
      AssetScreenBuilder overrides = builder.screenBuilders.get(normalizeId(source.sourceId()));
      if (overrides == null) {
        overrides = new AssetScreenBuilder();
      }
      int resolvedOrder = overrides.orderOverride == null ? source.order() : overrides.orderOverride;
      StitchAssetResultsConfig resultsConfig =
          uiBuilder.buildResultsConfig(source, overrides.resultsOverrides(), overrides.summaryHints());

      StitchAssetsScreenConfig config =
          StitchAssetsScreenConfig.builder(source.sourceId())
              .withLabel(source.label())
              .withRoutePath(source.routePath())
              .withPageTitle(source.pageTitle())
              .withPageSubtitle(source.pageSubtitle())
              .withOrder(resolvedOrder)
              .withEnabled(true)
              .withResultsConfig(resultsConfig)
              .withEditorOverrides(
                  overrides.editorOverrides(
                      builder.defaultFieldGridColumns, builder.defaultNestedRecordPresentation))
              .build();
      configured.put(source.sourceId(), config);
    }
    this.screens = Map.copyOf(configured);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public Optional<StitchAssetsScreenConfig> screen(String id) {
    if (id == null || id.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.ofNullable(screens.get(normalizeId(id)));
  }

  public List<StitchAssetsScreenConfig> screens() {
    List<StitchAssetsScreenConfig> values = new ArrayList<>(screens.values());
    values.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(StitchAssetsScreenConfig::order)
            .thenComparing(config -> config.label().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    List<StitchMenuEntry> entries = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchAssetsScreenConfig screen : screens()) {
      if (!screen.enabled()) {
        continue;
      }
      entries.add(
          StitchMenuEntry.builder(entryIdForScreen(screen.id()))
              .withLabel(screen.label())
              .withRoutePath(screen.routePath())
              .withOrder(screen.order())
              .build());
    }
    return List.copyOf(entries);
  }

  private static String entryIdForScreen(String screenId) {
    String normalized = normalizeId(screenId);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case APPS -> ENTRY_APPS;
      case SERVICES -> ENTRY_SERVICES;
      case CONNECTIONS -> ENTRY_CONNECTIONS;
      case INGESTION -> ENTRY_INGESTION;
      case DATASETS -> ENTRY_DATASETS;
      case STREAMS -> ENTRY_STREAMS;
      case CONFIGS -> ENTRY_CONFIGS;
      case SCHEMAS -> ENTRY_SCHEMAS;
      default -> FEATURE_ID + "." + normalized;
    };
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String normalizeId(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Assets";
    private int order = 20;
    private Integer defaultFieldGridColumns = 4;
    private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation defaultNestedRecordPresentation =
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.TABS;
    private final Map<String, AssetScreenBuilder> screenBuilders = new LinkedHashMap<>();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFieldGridColumns(int value) {
      this.defaultFieldGridColumns = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, value));
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNestedRecordPresentation(
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation value) {
      this.defaultNestedRecordPresentation =
          value == null ? StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.TABS : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder apps(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(APPS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder app(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(APPS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder services(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(SERVICES, customizer);
    }

    public Builder service(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(SERVICES, customizer);
    }

    public Builder connections(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(CONNECTIONS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder connection(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(CONNECTIONS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder ingestion(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(INGESTION, customizer);
    }

    public Builder datasets(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(DATASETS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder dataset(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(DATASETS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder streams(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(STREAMS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder stream(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(STREAMS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder configs(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(CONFIGS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder config(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(CONFIGS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder schemas(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(SCHEMAS, customizer);
    }

    public Builder schema(Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      return screen(SCHEMAS, customizer);
    }

    private Builder screen(String id, Consumer<AssetScreenBuilder> customizer) {
      AssetScreenBuilder screenBuilder =
          screenBuilders.computeIfAbsent(normalizeId(id), ignored -> new AssetScreenBuilder());
      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(screenBuilder);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public StitchAssetsFeature build() {
      return new StitchAssetsFeature(this);
    }
  }

  public static final class AssetScreenBuilder {
    private Integer orderOverride;
    private final ResultsOverridesBuilder results = new ResultsOverridesBuilder();
    private final EditorOverridesBuilder editor = new EditorOverridesBuilder();

    public AssetScreenBuilder withOrder(int value) {
      this.orderOverride = value;
      return this;
    }

    public AssetScreenBuilder addFields(String... fields) {
      results.addFields(fields);
      return this;
    }

    public AssetScreenBuilder withSummaryFields(String... fields) {
      results.withSummaryFields(fields);
      return this;
    }

    public AssetScreenBuilder results(Consumer<ResultsOverridesBuilder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(results);
      return this;
    }

    public AssetScreenBuilder editor(Consumer<EditorOverridesBuilder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(editor);
      return this;
    }

    public AssetScreenBuilder withFieldGridColumns(int value) {
      editor.withFieldGridColumns(value);
      return this;
    }

    public AssetScreenBuilder withNestedRecordPresentation(
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation value) {
      editor.withNestedRecordPresentation(value);
      return this;
    }

    private StitchAssetUiBuilder.ResultsOverrides resultsOverrides() {
      return results.build();
    }

    private StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides editorOverrides(
        Integer defaultFieldGridColumns,
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation defaultNestedRecordPresentation) {
      return editor.build(defaultFieldGridColumns, defaultNestedRecordPresentation);
    }

    private List<String> summaryHints() {
      List<String> hints = results.summaryFieldsOverrideSet ? results.summaryFields : List.of();
      return StitchAssetResultsConfig.normalizeFieldKeys(hints);
    }
  }

  public static final class ResultsOverridesBuilder {
    private final List<String> additionalFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private final List<String> visibleFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private boolean visibleFieldsOverrideSet;
    private final List<String> summaryFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private boolean summaryFieldsOverrideSet;

    public ResultsOverridesBuilder addFields(String... fields) {
      if (fields == null) {
        return this;
      }
      for (String field : fields) {
        String normalized = normalizeFieldKey(field);
        if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
          additionalFields.add(normalized);
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public ResultsOverridesBuilder withFields(String... fields) {
      visibleFieldsOverrideSet = true;
      visibleFields.clear();
      if (fields != null) {
        for (String field : fields) {
          String normalized = normalizeFieldKey(field);
          if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
            visibleFields.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public ResultsOverridesBuilder withSummaryFields(String... fields) {
      summaryFieldsOverrideSet = true;
      summaryFields.clear();
      if (fields != null) {
        for (String field : fields) {
          String normalized = normalizeFieldKey(field);
          if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
            summaryFields.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    private StitchAssetUiBuilder.ResultsOverrides build() {
      List<String> extra = normalizeFieldKeys(additionalFields);
      List<String> visible = visibleFieldsOverrideSet ? normalizeFieldKeys(visibleFields) : null;
      List<String> summary = summaryFieldsOverrideSet ? normalizeFieldKeys(summaryFields) : null;
      return new StitchAssetUiBuilder.ResultsOverrides(extra, visible, summary);
    }
  }

  public static final class EditorOverridesBuilder {
    private final List<StitchAssetUiBuilder.GroupOverride> groups = new ArrayList<>();
    private final List<StitchAssetUiBuilder.VisibilityOverride> visibility = new ArrayList<>();
    private Integer fieldGridColumns;
    private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation =
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT;

    public EditorOverridesBuilder group(String label, Consumer<GroupBuilder> customizer) {
      GroupBuilder groupBuilder = new GroupBuilder(label);
      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(groupBuilder);
      }
      groups.add(groupBuilder.build());
      return this;
    }

    public EditorOverridesBuilder showWhen(
        String targetGroup, String controllerField, String... allowedValues) {
      List<String> values = normalizeFieldKeys(allowedValues == null ? List.of() : List.of(allowedValues));
      visibility.add(
          new StitchAssetUiBuilder.VisibilityOverride(targetGroup, controllerField, List.copyOf(values)));
      return this;
    }

    public EditorOverridesBuilder withFieldGridColumns(int value) {
      this.fieldGridColumns = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, value));
      return this;
    }

    public EditorOverridesBuilder withNestedRecordPresentation(
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation value) {
      this.nestedRecordPresentation =
          value == null ? StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT : value;
      return this;
    }

    private StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides build(
        Integer defaultFieldGridColumns,
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation defaultNestedRecordPresentation) {
      Integer resolvedColumns =
          fieldGridColumns == null
              ? (defaultFieldGridColumns == null
                  ? null
                  : Integer.valueOf(Math.max(1, Math.min(6, defaultFieldGridColumns)))
                  )
              : fieldGridColumns;
      StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation resolvedPresentation =
          nestedRecordPresentation == null
                  || nestedRecordPresentation == StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT
              ? (defaultNestedRecordPresentation == null
                  ? StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT
                  : defaultNestedRecordPresentation)
              : nestedRecordPresentation;
      return new StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides(
          List.copyOf(groups),
          List.copyOf(visibility),
          resolvedColumns,
          resolvedPresentation);
    }
  }

  public static final class GroupBuilder {
    private final String label;
    private final List<String> fields = new ArrayList<>();
    private Integer fieldGridColumns;
    private StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation nestedRecordPresentation =
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT;

    private GroupBuilder(String label) {
      this.label = label == null || label.isBlank() ? "Group" : label.trim();
    }

    public GroupBuilder addFields(String... paths) {
      if (paths == null) {
        return this;
      }
      for (String path : paths) {
        String normalized = normalizeFieldKey(path);
        if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
          fields.add(normalized);
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public GroupBuilder withFieldGridColumns(int value) {
      fieldGridColumns = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, value));
      return this;
    }

    public GroupBuilder withNestedRecordPresentation(
        StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation value) {
      nestedRecordPresentation =
          value == null ? StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT : value;
      return this;
    }

    private StitchAssetUiBuilder.GroupOverride build() {
      return new StitchAssetUiBuilder.GroupOverride(
          label,
          normalizeFieldKeys(fields),
          fieldGridColumns,
          nestedRecordPresentation);
    }
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeFieldKeys(List<String> keys) {
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = normalizeFieldKey(key);
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeFieldKey(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}

record StitchAssetSourceSpec(

    String defaultDraftName,

  StitchAssetSourceSpec {
    sourceId = require(sourceId, "sourceId");
    label = require(label, "label");
    routePath = require(routePath, "routePath");
    pageTitle = require(pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    pageSubtitle = optional(pageSubtitle);
    definitionClass = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(definitionClass, "definitionClass");
    definitionType = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(definitionType, "definitionType");
    defaultDraftName = require(defaultDraftName, "defaultDraftName");
    draftCustomizer = draftCustomizer == null ? StitchAssetDraftCustomizer.NOOP : draftCustomizer;
  }

  void customizeDraft(ObjectNode draft, String group, String name) {
    draftCustomizer.customize(draft, group, name);
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    String normalized = optional(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsRow.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;

public record StitchAssetsRow(
    String id,
    boolean enabled,
    String group,
    String name,
    Map<String, Object> fields,
    Object sourceObject) {

  public StitchAssetsRow {
    id = normalize(id);
    group = normalize(group);
    name = normalize(name);
    fields = immutableFields(fields);
  }

  public String field(String key) {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    String normalizedKey = key.trim();
    return switch (normalizedKey.toLowerCase()) {
      case "enabled" -> enabled ? "ENABLED" : "DISABLED";
      case "group" -> group;
      case "name" -> name;
      default -> normalize(stringValue(resolveFieldValue(normalizedKey)));
    };
  }

  public Map<String, String> detailFields() {
    Map<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("enabled", field("enabled"));
    values.put("group", group);
    values.put("name", name);
    values.putAll(flattenedFields());
    return Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  public Map<String, String> flattenedFields() {
    Map<String, String> flattened = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Object> entry : fields.entrySet()) {
      String key = normalize(entry.getKey());
      if (key.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      flattenValue(key, entry.getValue(), flattened);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(flattened);
  }

  private Object resolveFieldValue(String key) {
    Object direct = findInMap(fields, key);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    if (!key.contains(".")) {
      return null;
    }
    String[] path = key.split("\\.");
    if (path.length == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    Object current = findInMap(fields, path[0]);
    if (current == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (int i = 1; i < path.length; i++) {
      current = resolvePathSegment(current, path[i]);
      if (current == null) {
        return null;
      }
    }
    return current;
  }

  private static Object resolvePathSegment(Object current, String segment) {
    if (current instanceof Map<?, ?> values) {
      return findInMap(values, segment);
    }
    if (current == null || segment == null || segment.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }

    Class<?> type = current.getClass();
    if (type.isRecord()) {
      try {
        for (java.lang.reflect.RecordComponent component : type.getRecordComponents()) {
          if (component.getName().equalsIgnoreCase(segment)) {
            java.lang.reflect.Method accessor = component.getAccessor();
            accessor.setAccessible(true);
            return accessor.invoke(current);
          }
        }
      } catch (ReflectiveOperationException ignored) {
      }
    }

    String suffix = Character.toUpperCase(segment.charAt(0)) + segment.substring(1);
    for (String methodName : new String[] {"get" + suffix, "is" + suffix}) {
      try {
        java.lang.reflect.Method method = type.getMethod(methodName);
        method.setAccessible(true);
        return method.invoke(current);
      } catch (ReflectiveOperationException ignored) {
      }
    }

    Class<?> cursor = type;
    while (cursor != null && cursor != Object.class) {
      for (java.lang.reflect.Field field : cursor.getDeclaredFields()) {
        if (field.getName().equalsIgnoreCase(segment)) {
          try {
            field.setAccessible(true);
            return field.get(current);
          } catch (IllegalAccessException ignored) {
            return null;
          }
        }
      }
      cursor = cursor.getSuperclass();
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static Object findInMap(Map<?, ?> map, String key) {
    if (map == null || key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    Object direct = map.get(key);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    String normalizedKey = key.trim();
    for (Map.Entry<?, ?> entry : map.entrySet()) {
      if (!(entry.getKey() instanceof String candidate)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (candidate.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedKey)) {
        return entry.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static void flattenValue(String path, Object value, Map<String, String> target) {
    if (value instanceof Map<?, ?> nestedMap) {
      for (Map.Entry<?, ?> nestedEntry : nestedMap.entrySet()) {
        if (!(nestedEntry.getKey() instanceof String nestedKey)) {
          continue;
        }
        String nextPath = path + "." + nestedKey.trim();
        flattenValue(nextPath, nestedEntry.getValue(), target);
      }
      return;
    }
    target.put(path, normalize(stringValue(value)));
  }

  private static String stringValue(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return String.valueOf(value);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static Map<String, Object> immutableFields(Map<String, Object> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, Object> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Object> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      String key = normalize(entry.getKey());
      if (key.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.put(key, entry.getValue());
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Collections.unmodifiableMap(normalized);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsSchemasView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import com.vaadin.flow.server.StreamResource;
import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchJsonDiffDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

@Route(value = "assets/schemas", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchAssetsSchemasView extends StitchAssetsView {
  public StitchAssetsSchemasView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, Stitch stitch, StitchAssetsDataProviders providers) {
    super(runtimeContext, stitch, providers, StitchAssetsFeature.SCHEMAS);
    addClassName("stitch-assets-schemas-page");
    body().addClassName("stitch-assets-schemas-body");
    filtersBar().addClassName("stitch-assets-schemas-filters");
    resultsView().addClassName("stitch-assets-schemas-results");
    resultsView().grid().addClassName("stitch-assets-schemas-grid");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAssetsRow> grid) {
    super.configureGrid(grid);
    tuneColumn(grid, "enabled", "7.3rem", 0, false);
    tuneColumn(grid, "group", "11rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "name", "14rem", 2, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "schemaType", "10.5rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "schemaUsage", "9.5rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "versionSemantic", "9rem", 0, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "status", "9rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "format", "10rem", 1, true);
    tuneColumn(grid, "artifactType", "9rem", 1, true);
    grid.getStyle().set("min-height", "22rem");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureAdditionalRowActions(StitchRowActions<StitchAssetsRow> rowActions) {
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.<StitchAssetsRow>icon(VaadinIcon.INFO_CIRCLE_O, "COMPARE", this::compareRequested)
            .enabledWhen(this::isNavigableRow));
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.<StitchAssetsRow>icon(VaadinIcon.DOWNLOAD_ALT, "EXPORT", this::exportRequested)
            .enabledWhen(this::isNavigableRow));
  }

  private void compareRequested(StitchAssetsRow selected) {
    if (!isNavigableRow(selected)) {
      return;
    }
    List<StitchAssetsRow> candidates = compareCandidates(selected);
    if (candidates.isEmpty()) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "No compare candidate",
          "No additional schemas are available to compare against the selected schema.");
      return;
    }

    ComboBox<String> compareWith = new ComboBox<>("Compare With");
    compareWith.setWidthFull();
    compareWith.setAllowCustomValue(false);

    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchAssetsRow> byLabel = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (StitchAssetsRow candidate : candidates) {
      String base = StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.compareLabel(snapshot(candidate));
      String label = uniqueLabel(byLabel, base);
      byLabel.put(label, candidate);
    }
    compareWith.setItems(byLabel.keySet());
    compareWith.setValue(byLabel.keySet().iterator().next());

    Span hint =
        new Span("Compare schema JSON structures. Differences open in the shared side-by-side diff workspace.");
    hint.addClassName("stitch-assets-schemas-compare-hint");

    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Compare Schemas");
    dialog.addToBody(hint, compareWith);
    dialog.withJsonPayloadSupplier(
        () -> {
          com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode payload = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().createObjectNode();
          payload.put("selected", selected.group() + "/" + selected.name());
          payload.put("compareWith", compareWith.getValue());
          return payload;
        });
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "COMPARE",
        () -> {
          StitchAssetsRow candidate = byLabel.get(compareWith.getValue());
          if (candidate == null) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Choose schema", "Select a schema to compare.");
            return;
          }
          openCompareDialog(selected, candidate);
          dialog.close();
        });
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private void openCompareDialog(StitchAssetsRow leftRow, StitchAssetsRow rightRow) {
    StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.SchemaSnapshot left = snapshot(leftRow);
    StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.SchemaSnapshot right = snapshot(rightRow);
    JsonNode leftPayload = left.payload();
    JsonNode rightPayload = right.payload();
    String title =
        "Schema Compare - "
            + valueOrDash(left.group())
            + "/"
            + valueOrDash(left.name())
            + " vs "
            + valueOrDash(right.group())
            + "/"
            + valueOrDash(right.name());
    String leftLabel = "Selected " + valueOrDash(left.version());
    String rightLabel = "Compare " + valueOrDash(right.version());
    new StitchJsonDiffDialog(title, leftLabel, leftPayload, rightLabel, rightPayload).open();
  }

  private void exportRequested(StitchAssetsRow selected) {
    StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.SchemaSnapshot snapshot = snapshot(selected);
    if (!isNavigableRow(selected)) {
      return;
    }
    String prettyPayload;
    try {
      prettyPayload =
          DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(snapshot.payload());
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to export schema", "Failed to serialize schema JSON for export.");
      return;
    }

    String filename = StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.schemaExportFilename(snapshot.group(), snapshot.name());
    byte[] bytes = prettyPayload.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    StreamResource resource = new StreamResource(filename, () -> new ByteArrayInputStream(bytes));
    String uri =
        getUI()
            .map(
                ui ->
                    ui.getSession()
                        .getResourceRegistry()
                        .registerResource(resource)
                        .getResourceUri()
                        .toString())
            .orElse(null);
    if (uri == null) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to export schema", "Could not prepare the schema download.");
      return;
    }
    getUI().ifPresent(ui -> ui.getPage().open(uri));
  }

  private StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.SchemaSnapshot snapshot(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    return StitchSchemaPresentationSupport.snapshot(row);
  }

  private List<StitchAssetsRow> compareCandidates(StitchAssetsRow selected) {
    if (!isNavigableRow(selected)) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchAssetsRow> candidates = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchAssetsRow row : dataProvider().loadRows()) {
      if (row == null || !isNavigableRow(row)) {
        continue;
      }
      boolean sameIdentity =
          equalsIgnoreCase(selected.group(), row.group()) && equalsIgnoreCase(selected.name(), row.name());
      if (!sameIdentity) {
        candidates.add(row);
      }
    }
    candidates.sort(
        Comparator.comparing((StitchAssetsRow row) -> valueOrDash(row.group()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(row -> valueOrDash(row.name()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
            .thenComparing(
                row -> valueOrDash(row.field("versionSemantic")),
                String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return candidates;
  }

  private static String uniqueLabel(Map<String, StitchAssetsRow> values, String baseLabel) {
    String base = valueOrDash(baseLabel);
    if (!values.containsKey(base)) {
      return base;
    }
    int suffix = 2;
    while (values.containsKey(base + " (" + suffix + ")")) {
      suffix++;
    }
    return base + " (" + suffix + ")";
  }

  private static boolean equalsIgnoreCase(String left, String right) {
    String a = Strings.trimToNull(left);
    String b = Strings.trimToNull(right);
    return a != null && b != null && a.equalsIgnoreCase(b);
  }

  private static String valueOrDash(String value) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "-");
  }

  private static void tuneColumn(
      Grid<StitchAssetsRow> grid, String key, String width, int flexGrow, boolean resizable) {
    if (grid == null || key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    grid.getColumns().stream()
        .filter(column -> key.equalsIgnoreCase(column.getKey()))
        .findFirst()
        .ifPresent(
            column -> {
              if (Strings.isNotBlank(width)) {
                column.setAutoWidth(false);
                column.setWidth(width);
              }
              column.setFlexGrow(Math.max(0, flexGrow));
              column.setResizable(resizable);
            });
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchBooleanToggle;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchGroupedResultsPage;

public class StitchAssetsScreen extends StitchGroupedResultsPage<StitchAssetsRow> {
  private final StitchAssetsScreenConfig config;
  private final StitchAssetsDataProvider provider;

  public StitchAssetsScreen(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchAssetsScreenConfig config,
      StitchAssetsDataProvider provider) {
    super(
        runtimeContext,
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle(),
        "Type to filter results...",
        "Search asset rows");
    this.config = config;
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    initializeResultsScreen("No asset rows", "No matching asset rows were found.", "Refresh asset rows");
    setHeight(null);
    body().setHeight(null);
    resultsView().setHeight(null);
    resultsView().grid().setHeight(null);
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchAssetsRow> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Enabled", this::enabledToggle)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.ENABLED)
            .key("enabled")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("8.1rem")
            .resizable(false)
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Group", StitchAssetsRow::group)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.GROUP)
            .key("group"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Name", StitchAssetsRow::name)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.NAME)
            .key("name"));

    for (StitchAssetsColumn column : filteredAdditionalColumns()) {
      grid.addColumn(
          StitchGridColumn.<StitchAssetsRow>text(column.label(), row -> row.field(column.key()))
              .key(column.key())
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    }

    if (!config.resultsConfig().summaryFields().isEmpty()) {
      grid.addColumn(
          StitchGridColumn.<StitchAssetsRow>text(
                  summaryLabel(), row -> summarize(row, config.resultsConfig().summaryFields()))
              .key("summary")
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    }

    StitchRowActions<StitchAssetsRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
    configureRowActions(rowActions);
    rowActions.addColumn(grid);
    grid.addItemDoubleClickListener(event -> onRowOpenRequested(event.getItem()));
  }

  protected void configureRowActions(StitchRowActions<StitchAssetsRow> rowActions) {}

  protected void onRowOpenRequested(StitchAssetsRow row) {}

  protected final StitchAssetsScreenConfig screenConfig() {
    return config;
  }

  protected final StitchAssetsDataProvider dataProvider() {
    return provider;
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchAssetsRow> loadRows() {
    return provider.loadRows();
  }

  @Override
  protected Comparator<StitchAssetsRow> rowComparator() {
    return StitchAssetsSort.defaultComparator();
  }

  @Override
  protected String groupValue(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    return row == null ? null : row.group();
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesSearch(StitchAssetsRow row, String query) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (contains(row.field("enabled"), query)
        || contains(row.group(), query)
        || contains(row.name(), query)) {
      return true;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : row.flattenedFields().entrySet()) {
      if (contains(entry.getValue(), query)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private StitchBooleanToggle enabledToggle(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    boolean enabled = row != null && row.enabled();
    StitchBooleanToggle toggle = new StitchBooleanToggle("Enabled", enabled);
    toggle.setLabel("");
    toggle.setReadOnly(true);
    toggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled");
    return toggle;
  }

  private List<StitchAssetsColumn> filteredAdditionalColumns() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> seen = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    List<StitchAssetsColumn> filtered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchAssetsColumn column : config.resultsConfig().visibleFields()) {
      if (column == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = normalizeFieldKey(column.key());
      if (key.isBlank() || isStandardLeadingColumn(key) || !seen.add(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        continue;
      }
      filtered.add(new StitchAssetsColumn(key, column.label()));
    }
    return List.copyOf(filtered);
  }

  private static boolean isStandardLeadingColumn(String key) {
    return switch (normalizeFieldKey(key).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
      case "enabled", "group", "name" -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private static String normalizeFieldKey(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private String summarize(StitchAssetsRow row, List<String> keys) {
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = normalize(row == null ? null : row.field(key));
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        values.add(value);
      }
    }
    return String.join(" | ", values);
  }

  private String summaryLabel() {
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.defaultSummaryLabel(config.resultsConfig().summaryLabel());
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsScreenConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;

public final class StitchAssetsScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;
  private final StitchAssetResultsConfig resultsConfig;
  private final StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides editorOverrides;

  private StitchAssetsScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.resultsConfig = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.resultsConfig, "resultsConfig");
    this.editorOverrides = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.editorOverrides, "editorOverrides");
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public StitchAssetResultsConfig resultsConfig() {
    return resultsConfig;
  }

  public StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides editorOverrides() {
    return editorOverrides;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private final List<StitchAssetsColumn> additionalColumns = new ArrayList<>();
    private String summaryLabel = "Summary";
    private final List<String> summaryFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private StitchAssetResultsConfig resultsConfig = StitchAssetResultsConfig.builder().build();
    private StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides editorOverrides =
        new StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides(
            List.of(),
            List.of(),
            null,
            StitchAssetUiDescriptor.NestedRecordPresentation.USE_DEFAULT);

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = toDisplay(id);
      this.routePath = "assets/" + this.id.toLowerCase();
      this.pageTitle = "Assets " + this.label;
      this.pageSubtitle = "Assets view for " + this.label;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withResultsConfig(StitchAssetResultsConfig value) {
      if (value != null) {
        this.resultsConfig = value;
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEditorOverrides(StitchAssetUiBuilder.EditorOverrides value) {
      if (value != null) {
        this.editorOverrides = value;
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAdditionalColumns(List<StitchAssetsColumn> columns) {
      additionalColumns.clear();
      if (columns != null) {
        additionalColumns.addAll(columns.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList());
      }
      rebuildResultsConfig();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryLabel(String value) {
      summaryLabel = optional(value);
      rebuildResultsConfig();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryFields(List<String> keys) {
      summaryFields.clear();
      if (keys != null) {
        for (String key : keys) {
          String normalized = optional(key);
          if (normalized != null) {
            summaryFields.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      rebuildResultsConfig();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder customize(Consumer<Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(this);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchAssetsScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchAssetsScreenConfig(this);
    }

    private void rebuildResultsConfig() {
      StitchAssetResultsConfig.Builder builder = StitchAssetResultsConfig.builder();
      builder.withVisibleFields(additionalColumns);
      builder.withSummaryLabel(summaryLabel);
      builder.withSummaryFields(summaryFields);
      this.resultsConfig = builder.build();
    }

    private static String toDisplay(String value) {
      String normalized = value.replace('-', ' ').replace('_', ' ').trim();
      if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
        return value;
      }
      return Character.toUpperCase(normalized.charAt(0)) + normalized.substring(1);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsSort.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import java.util.Comparator;

public final class StitchAssetsSort {
  private StitchAssetsSort() {}

  public static Comparator<StitchAssetsRow> defaultComparator() {
    return Comparator.comparing((StitchAssetsRow row) -> row == null ? 1 : (row.enabled() ? 0 : 1))
        .thenComparing(row -> normalize(row == null ? null : row.group()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(row -> normalize(row == null ? null : row.name()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(row -> normalize(row == null ? null : row.id()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

abstract class StitchAssetsView extends StitchAssetsScreen {
  private final String sourceId;
  private final StitchAssetEditorDescriptor descriptor;
  private final StitchAssetsEditorProvider editorProvider;

  protected StitchAssetsView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchAssetsDataProviders providers,
      String sourceId) {
    super(
        runtimeContext,
        StitchAssetsViewSupport.requireConfig(stitch, sourceId),
        requireProvider(providers, sourceId));
    this.sourceId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sourceId), "");
    this.descriptor = new StitchAssetEditorDescriptors(stitch, providers).find(this.sourceId).orElse(null);
    this.editorProvider = new StitchAssetsEditorProvider(runtimeContext);
    configureCreateAction();
  }

  @Override
  protected final void configureRowActions(StitchRowActions<StitchAssetsRow> rowActions) {
    rowActions.addAction(
        StitchRowActions.Action.<StitchAssetsRow>icon(
                VaadinIcon.EXTERNAL_LINK, "OPEN", row -> openEditorDialog(row, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.VIEW))
            .enabledWhen(this::isNavigableRow));
    configureAdditionalRowActions(rowActions);
  }

  @Override
  protected final void onRowOpenRequested(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    if (isNavigableRow(row)) {
      openEditorDialog(row, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.VIEW);
    }
  }

  protected void configureAdditionalRowActions(StitchRowActions<StitchAssetsRow> rowActions) {}

  private static StitchAssetsDataProvider requireProvider(
      StitchAssetsDataProviders providers, String sourceId) {
    return providers.provider(sourceId);
  }

  private void configureCreateAction() {
    Button create =
        new Button(
            "CREATE",
            event ->
                openEditorDialog(
                    null,
                    StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.CREATE,
                    selectedGroupFilterValue()));
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(create);
    create.addClassName("stitch-create-action");
    create.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Create new " + singularLabel(screenConfig().label()));
    create.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Create new " + singularLabel(screenConfig().label()));
    filtersBar().withRightActionFirst(create);
  }

  protected final boolean isNavigableRow(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    return row != null && Strings.isNotBlank(row.group()) && Strings.isNotBlank(row.name());
  }

  protected final void openInEditor(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    openEditorDialog(row, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.VIEW);
  }

  protected final void editInEditor(StitchAssetsRow row) {
    openEditorDialog(row, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.EDIT);
  }

  protected final void createInEditor() {
    openEditorDialog(null, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.CREATE, selectedGroupFilterValue());
  }

  private void openEditorDialog(StitchAssetsRow row, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode mode) {
    openEditorDialog(row, mode, row == null ? null : row.group());
  }

  private void openEditorDialog(
      StitchAssetsRow row, StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode mode, String preferredCreateGroup) {
    if (descriptor == null || editorProvider == null) {
      return;
    }
    StitchAssetEditorDialog dialog =
        new StitchAssetEditorDialog(
            descriptor,
            editorProvider,
            row,
            mode == null ? StitchAssetEditorDialog.OpenMode.VIEW : mode,
            preferredCreateGroup,
            definition -> refreshRows());
    dialog.open();
  }

  private static String singularLabel(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "asset";
    }
    if (normalized.toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT).endsWith("s") && normalized.length() > 1) {
      return normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1).toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/assets/StitchAssetsViewSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.assets;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;

final class StitchAssetsViewSupport {
  private StitchAssetsViewSupport() {}

  static StitchAssetsScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch, String sourceId) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .assets()
        .flatMap(feature -> feature.screen(sourceId))
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }
}
